                    to the 1938 edition of Trikamji Acharya, not the 1931 edition as for the rest of
                    the sūtrasthāna. (In fact, the transcript of the "1931" edition is somewhat
                    mixed between the 1931 and 1938 editions.)</change>

     <text xml:lang="sa-Latn">

          <body>
               <div n="1" type="sthāna">

                    <head xml:lang="en">[Sūtrasthāna 1-31]</head>

                    <div n="1" type="adhyāya">

                         <l xml:id="SS.1.1.0"/>

                         <l xml:id="SS.1.1.1">athāto vedotpattim adhyāyaṃ vyākhyāsyāmaḥ ||1|| </l>

                         <l xml:id="SS.1.1.2"><label>1931 ed. 1.1.2</label> yathovāca bhagavān
                              dhanvantariḥ||2||</l>

                         <l xml:id="SS.1.1.3"><label>1931 ed. 1.1.3</label> atha khalu bhagavantam
                              amaravaram ṛṣigaṇaparivṛtam āśramasthaṃ kāśirājaṃ divodāsaṃ
                              dhanvantarim aupadhenava<pc> </pc>vaitaraṇaurabhra<pc
                                   > </pc>pauṣkalāvata<pc> </pc>-karavīrya<pc
                                   > </pc>gopurarakṣita<pc> </pc>suśruta<pc> </pc>prabhṛtaya ūcuḥ
                              ||3|| <note type="footnote"> karavīra</note>
                         </l>

                         <l xml:id="SS.1.1.4"><label>1931 ed. 1.1.4</label> bhagavan
                              śārīramānasāgantuvyādhibhir vividhavedanābhighātopadrutān sanāthān apy
                              anāthavad viceṣṭamānān vikrośataś ca mānavān abhisamīkṣya manasi naḥ
                              pīḍā bhavati </l>

                         <l xml:id="SS.1.1.4b"> teṣāṃ sukhaiṣiṇāṃ rogopaśamārtham ātmanaś ca
                              prāṇayātrārthaṃ prajāhitahetor āyurvedaṃ śrotum icchāma
                              ihopadiśyamānaṃ atrāyattam aihikam āmuṣmikaṃ ca śreyaḥ tad bhagavantam
                              upapannāḥ smaḥ śiṣyatveneti ||</l>

                         <l xml:id="SS.1.1.5"><label>1931 ed. 1.1.5</label> tān uvāca bhagavān
                              svāgataṃ vaḥ sarva evāmīmāṃsyā adhyāpyāś ca bhavanto vatsāḥ || </l>

                         <l xml:id="SS.1.1.6"><label>1931 ed. 1.1.6</label> iha khalv āyurvedaṃ
                              nāmopāṅgam atharvavedasyānutpādyaiva prajāḥ ślokaśatasahasram
                              adhyāyasahasraṃ ca kṛtavān svayambhūḥ tato 'lpāyuṣṭvam alpamedhastvaṃ
                              cālokya narāṇāṃ bhūyo 'ṣṭadhā praṇītavān || </l>

                         <l xml:id="SS.1.1.7"><label>1931 ed. 1.1.7</label> tad yathā śalyaṃ
                              śālākyaṃ kāyacikitsā bhūtavidyā kaumārabhṛtyaṃ agadatantraṃ
                              rasāyanatantraṃ vājīkaraṇatantram iti || </l>

                         <l xml:id="SS.1.1.8.1"><label>1931 ed. 1.1.8.0</label> athāsya
                              pratyaṅgalakṣaṇasamāsaḥ | </l>

                         <l xml:id="SS.1.1.8.1a"> tatra śalyaṃ nāma
                              vividhatṛṇakāṣṭhapāṣāṇapāṃśulohaloṣṭāsthibālanakhapūyāsrāvaduṣṭavraṇāntargarbhaśalyoddharaṇārthaṃ
                              yantraśastrakṣārāgnipraṇidhānavraṇaviniścayārthaṃ ca || </l>

                         <l xml:id="SS.1.1.8.2"><label>1931 ed. 1.1.8.2</label> śālākyaṃ
                              nāmordhvajatrugatānāṃ śravaṇanayanavadanaghrāṇādisaṃśritānāṃ vyādhīnām
                              upaśamanārtham || </l>

                         <l xml:id="SS.1.1.8.3"><label>1931 ed. 1.1.8.3</label> kāyacikītsā nāma
                              sarvāṅgasaṃśritānāṃ vyādhīnāṃ
                              jvararaktapittaśoṣonmādāpasmārakuṣṭhamehātisārādīnām upaśamanārtham || </l>

                         <l xml:id="SS.1.1.8.4"><label>1931 ed. 1.1.8.4</label> bhūtavidyā nāma
                              devāsuragandharvayakṣarakṣaḥpitṛpiśācanāgagrahādyupasṛṣṭacetasāṃ
                              śāntikarmabaloharaṇādigrahopaśamanārtham || </l>

                         <l xml:id="SS.1.1.8.5"><label>1931 ed. 1.1.8.5</label> kaumārabhṛtyaṃ nāma
                              kumārabharaṇadhātrīkṣīradoṣasaṃśodhanārthaṃ
                              duṣṭastanyagrahasamutthānāṃ ca vyādhīnām upaśamanārtham || </l>

                         <l xml:id="SS.1.1.8.6"><label>1931 ed. 1.1.8.6</label> agadatantraṃ nāma
                              sarpakīṭalūtāmūśikādidaṣṭaviṣavyañjanārthaṃ
                              vividhaviṣasaṃyogopaśamanārthaṃ ca || </l>

                         <l xml:id="SS.1.1.8.7"><label>1931 ed. 1.1.8.7</label> rasāyanatantraṃ nāma
                              vayaḥsthāpanam āyurmedhābalakaraṃ rogāpaharaṇasamarthaṃ ca || </l>

                         <l xml:id="SS.1.1.8.8"><label>1931 ed. 1.1.8.8</label> vājīkaraṇatantraṃ
                              nāmālpaduṣṭakṣīṇaviśuṣkaretasām āpyāyanaprasādopacayajanananimittaṃ
                              praharṣajananārthaṃ ca || </l>

                         <l xml:id="SS.1.1.9"><label>1931 ed. 1.1.9</label> evam ayam āyurvedo
                              'ṣṭāṅga upadiśyate atra kasmai kim ucyatām iti || </l>

                         <l xml:id="SS.1.1.10"><label>1931 ed. 1.1.10</label> ta ūcuḥ asmākaṃ
                              sarveṣām eva śalyajñānaṃ mūlaṃ kṛtvopadiśatu bhagavān iti || </l>

                         <l xml:id="SS.1.1.11"><label>1931 ed. 1.1.11</label> sa uvācaivam astv iti
                              || </l>

                         <l xml:id="SS.1.1.12"><label>1931 ed. 1.1.12</label> ta ūcur bhūyo 'pi
                              bhagavantam asmākam ekamatīnāṃ matam abhisamīkṣya suśruto bhagavantaṃ
                              prakṣyati asmai copadiśyamānaṃ vayam apy upadhārayiṣyāmaḥ || </l>

                         <l xml:id="SS.1.1.13"><label>1931 ed. 1.1.13</label> sa hovācaivam astv iti
                              || </l>

                         <l xml:id="SS.1.1.14-16"><label>1931 ed. 1.1.14</label> vatsa suśruta iha
                              khalv āyurvedaprayojanaṃ vyādhyupasṛṣṭānāṃ vyādhiparimokṣaḥ svasthasya
                              rakṣaṇaṃ ca || <label>1931 ed. 1.1.15</label> āyur asmin vidyate 'nena
                              vā+āyur vindatīty āyurvedaḥ || <label>1931 ed. 1.1.16</label>
                              tasyāṅgavaram ādyaṃ pratyakṣāgamānumānopamānair aviruddham ucyamānam
                              upadharaya || </l>

                         <l xml:id="SS.1.1.17"><label>1931 ed. 1.1.17</label> etad dhy aṅgaṃ
                              prathamaṃ prāg abhighātavraṇasaṃrohāt yajñaśiraḥsandhānāc ca | śrūyate
                              hi yathā rudreṇa yajñasya śiraś chinnam iti tato devā aśvināv
                              abhigamyocuḥ bhagavantau naḥ śreṣṭhatamau yuvāṃ bhaviṣyathaḥ
                              bhavadbhyāṃ yajñasya śiraḥ sandhātavyam iti | tāv ūcatur evam astv iti
                              | atha tayor arthe devā indraṃ yajñabhagena prāsādayan | tābhyāṃ
                              yajñasya śiraḥ saṃhitam iti || </l>

                         <l xml:id="SS.1.1.18"><label>1931 ed. 1.1.18</label> aṣṭāsv api
                              cāyurvedatantreṣv etad evādhikam abhimataṃ āmāśu kriyākaraṇād
                              yantraśastrakṣārāgnipraṇidhānāt sarvatantrasāmānyāc ca || </l>

                         <l xml:id="SS.1.1.19"><label>1931 ed. 1.1.19</label> tad idaṃ śāśvataṃ
                              puṇyaṃ svargyaṃ yaśasyamāyuṣyaṃ vṛttikaraṃ ceti || </l>

                         <l xml:id="SS.1.1.20"><label>1931 ed. 1.1.20</label> brahmā provāca tataḥ
                              prajāpatir adhijage tasmād aśvinau aśvibhyām indraḥ indrād aḥaṃ mayā
                              tv iha pradeyam arthibhyaḥ prajāhitahetoḥ || </l>

                         <l xml:id="SS.1.1.21"><label>1931 ed. 1.1.21</label> bhavati cātra | ahaṃ
                              hi dhanvantarir ādidevo jarārujāmṛtyuharo 'marāṇām |
                              <caesura/>
                               śalyāṅgam aṅgair aparair upetaṃ prāpto 'smi gāṃ bhūya ihopadeṣṭum || </l>

                         <l xml:id="SS.1.1.22"><label>1931 ed. 1.1.22</label> asmin śāstre
                              pañcamahābhūtaśarīrisamavāyaḥ puruṣa ity ucyate | tasmin kriyā so
                              'dhiṣṭhānaṃ kasmāt lokasya dvaividhyāt loko hi dvividhaḥ sthāvaro
                              jaṅgamaś ca dvividhātmaka evāgneyaḥ saumyaś ca tadbhūyastvāt
                              pañcātmako vā tatra caturvidho bhūtagrāmaḥ
                              saṃsvedajarāyujāṇḍajodbhijjasaṃjñaḥ tatra puruṣaḥ pradhānaṃ
                              tasyopakaraṇam anyat tasmāt puruṣo 'dhiṣṭhānam || </l>

                         <l xml:id="SS.1.1.23"><label>1931 ed. 1.1.23</label> tadduḥkhasaṃyogā
                              vyādhaya ucyante || </l>

                         <l xml:id="SS.1.1.24"><label>1931 ed. 1.1.24</label> te caturvidhāḥ
                              āgantavaḥ śārīrāḥ mānasāḥ svābhāvikāś ceti || </l>

                         <l xml:id="SS.1.1.25.1"><label>1931 ed. 1.1.25.1</label> teṣām āgantavo
                              'bhighātanimittāḥ || </l>

                         <l xml:id="SS.1.1.25.2"><label>1931 ed. 1.1.25.2</label> śārīrās tv
                              annapānamūlā vātapittakaphaśoṇitasannipātavaiṣamyanimittāḥ || </l>

                         <l xml:id="SS.1.1.25.3"><label>1931 ed. 1.1.25.3</label> mānasās tu
                              krodhaśokabhayaharṣaviṣāderṣyābhyasūyādainyamātsaryakāmalobhaprabhṛtaya
                              icchādveṣabhedair bhavanti || </l>

                         <l xml:id="SS.1.1.25.4"><label>1931 ed. 1.1.25.4</label> svābhāvikās tu
                              kṣutpipāsājarāmṛtyunidrāprakṛtayaḥ || </l>

                         <l xml:id="SS.1.1.26"><label>1931 ed. 1.1.26</label> ta ete
                              manaḥśarīrādhiṣṭhānāḥ || </l>

                         <l xml:id="SS.1.1.27"><label>1931 ed. 1.1.27</label> teṣāṃ
                              saṃśodhanasaṃśamanāhārācārāḥ samyak prayuktā nigrahahetavaḥ || </l>

                         <l xml:id="SS.1.1.28"><label>1931 ed. 1.1.28</label> prāṇināṃ punar mūlam
                              āhāro balavarṇaujasāṃ ca sa ṣaṭsu raseṣv āyattaḥ rasāḥ punar
                              dravyāśrayāḥ dravyāṇi punar oṣadhayaḥ | tās tu dvividhāḥ sthāvarā
                              jaṅgamāś ca || </l>

                         <l xml:id="SS.1.1.29"><label>1931 ed. 1.1.29</label> tāsāṃ sthāvarāś
                              caturvidhāḥ vanaspatayo vṛkṣā vīrudha oṣadhaya iti | tāsu apuṣpāḥ
                              phalavanto vanaspatayaḥ puṣpaphalavanto vṛkṣāḥ pratānavatyaḥ
                              stambinyaś ca vīrudhaḥ phalapākaniṣṭhā oṣadhaya iti || </l>

                         <l xml:id="SS.1.1.30"><label>1931 ed. 1.1.30</label> jaṅgamāḥ khalv api
                              caturvidhāḥ jarāyujāṇḍajasvedajodbhijjāḥ | tatra paśumanuṣyavyālādayo
                              jarāyujāḥ khagasarpasarīsṛpaprabhṛtayo 'ṇḍajāḥ
                              kṛmikīṭapipīlikāprabhṛtayaḥ svedajāḥ indragopamaṇḍūkaprabhṛtaya
                              udbhijjāḥ || </l>

                         <l xml:id="SS.1.1.31"><label>1931 ed. 1.1.31</label> tatra sthāvarebhyas
                              tvakpatrapuṣpaphalamūlakandaniryāsasvarasādayaḥ prayojanavantaḥ
                              jaṅgamebhyaś carmanakharomarudhirādayaḥ || </l>

                         <l xml:id="SS.1.1.32"><label>1931 ed. 1.1.32</label> pārthivāḥ
                              suvarṇarajatamaṇimuktāmanaḥśilāmṛtkapālādayaḥ || </l>

                         <l xml:id="SS.1.1.33"><label>1931 ed. 1.1.33</label> kālakṛtāḥ
                              pravātanivātātapacchāyājyotsnātamaḥśītoṣṇavarṣāhorātrapakṣamāsartvayanādayaḥ
                              saṃvatsaraviśeṣāḥ || </l>

                         <l xml:id="SS.1.1.34"><label>1931 ed. 1.1.34</label> ta ete svabhāvata eva
                              doṣāṇāṃ sañcayaprakopapraśamapratīkārahetavaḥ prayojanavantaś ca || </l>

                         <l xml:id="SS.1.1.35"><label>1931 ed. 1.1.35</label> bhavanti cātra ślokāḥ
                              <caesura/>
                               śārīrāṇāṃ vikārāṇām eṣa vargaś caturvidhaḥ |
                              <caesura/>
                               prakope praśame caiva hetur uktaś cikitsakaiḥ || </l>

                         <l xml:id="SS.1.1.36"><label>1931 ed. 1.1.36</label> āgantavas tu ye rogās
                              te dvidhā nipatanti hi |
                              <caesura/>
                               manasy anye śarīre 'nye teṣāṃ tu dvividhā kriyā || </l>

                         <l xml:id="SS.1.1.37"><label>1931 ed. 1.1.37</label> śarīrapatitānāṃ tu
                              śārīravad upakramaḥ |
                              <caesura/>
                               mānasānāṃ tu śabdādir iṣṭo vargaḥ sukhāvahaḥ || </l>

                         <l xml:id="SS.1.1.38"><label>1931 ed. 1.1.38</label> evam etat puruṣo
                              vyādhir auṣadhaṃ kriyā kāla iti catuṣṭayaṃ samāsena vyākhyātam | tatra
                              puruṣagrahaṇāt tatsaṃbhavadravyasamūho bhūtādir uktas
                              tadaṅgapratyaṅgavikalpāś ca tvaṅmāṃsāsthisirāsnāyuprabhṛtayaḥ
                              vyādhigrahaṇād vātapittakaphaśoṇitasannipātavaiṣamyanimittāḥ sarva eva
                              vyādhayo vyākhyātāḥ oṣadhagrahaṇād dravyarasaguṇavīryavipākānām ādeśaḥ
                              kriyāgrahaṇāc chedyādīni snehādīni ca karmāṇi vyākhyātāni kālagrahaṇāt
                              sarvakriyākālānām ādeśaḥ || </l>

                         <l xml:id="SS.1.1.39"><label>1931 ed. 1.1.39</label> bhavati cātra | 
                              <caesura/>
                              bījaṃ cikitsitasyaitat
                              samāsena prakīrtitam |
                              <caesura/>
                               saviṃśam adhyāyaśatam asya vyākhyā bhaviṣyati || </l>

                         <l xml:id="SS.1.1.40"><label>1931 ed. 1.1.40</label> tac ca saviṃśam
                              adhyāyaśataṃ pañcasu sthāneṣu sūtranidānaśārīracikitsitakalpeṣv
                              arthavaśāt saṃvibhajya uttare tantre śeṣān arthān vyākhyāsyāmaḥ || </l>

                         <l xml:id="SS.1.1.41x"><label>1931 ed. 1.1.41</label>
                         </l>

                         <l xml:id="SS.1.1.41"><label>1931 ed. 1.1.41</label> bhavati cātra |
                              <caesura/>
                               svayambhuvā proktam idaṃ sanātanaṃ
                              <caesura/>
                               paṭhed dhi yaḥ kāśipatiprakāśitam |
                              <caesura/>
                               sa puṇyakarmā bhuvi pūjito nṛpair
                              <caesura/>
                               asukṣaye śakrasalokatāṃ vrajet || </l>




                         <p xml:id="SS.1.1">iti suśrutasaṃhitāyāṃ sūtrasthāne vedotpattir nāma
                              prathamo 'dhyāyaḥ ||</p>
                    </div>


                    <div n="2" type="adhyāya">

                         <head>[dvitīyo 'dhyāyaḥ|]</head>

                         <p xml:id="SS.1.2.1"><label>1931 ed. 1.2.1</label> athātaḥ śiṣyopanayanīyam
                              adhyāyaṃ vyākhyāsyāmaḥ || </p>

                         <p xml:id="SS.1.2.2"><label>1931 ed. 1.2.2</label> yathovāca bhagavān
                              dhanvantariḥ || </p>

                         <p xml:id="SS.1.2.3"><label>1931 ed. 1.2.3</label>
                              brāhmaṇakṣatriyavaiśyānām anyatamam anvaya<pc
                                   > </pc>vayaḥ<pc/>śīla<pc> </pc>śaurya<pc
                                   > </pc>śaucācāra<pc> </pc>vinaya<pc> </pc>śakti<pc
                                   > </pc>bala<pc> </pc>medhā<pc> </pc>dhṛti<pc
                                   > </pc>smṛti<pc> </pc>mati<pc> </pc>pratipattiyuktaṃ
                                   tanu<pc> </pc>jihvauṣṭha<pc> </pc>dantāgram ṛjuvaktrākṣināsaṃ
                              prasannacittavākceṣṭaṃ kleśasahaṃ ca bhiṣak śiṣyam upanayet ato
                              viparītaguṇaṃ nopanayet || </p>

                         <p xml:id="SS.1.2.4"><label>1931 ed. 1.2.4</label> upanayanīyaṃ tu
                              brāhmaṇaṃ praśasteṣu tithikaraṇamuhūrtanakṣatreṣu praśastāyāṃ diśi
                              śucau same deśe caturhastaṃ caturasraṃ sthaṇḍilam upalipya gomayena
                              darbhaiḥ saṃstīrya puṣpair lājabhaktai ratnaiś ca devatāḥ pūjayitvā
                              viprān bhiṣajaś ca tatrollikhyābhyukṣya ca dakṣiṇato brahmāṇaṃ
                              sthāpayitvā'gnim upasamādhāya khadirapalāśadevadārubilvānāṃ samidbhiś
                              caturṇāṃ vā kṣīravṛkṣāṇāṃ (? nyagrodhodumbarāśvatthamadhūkānāṃ )
                              dadhimadhughṛtāktābhir dārvīhaumikena vidhinā sruveṇājyāhutīr juhuyāt
                              sapraṇavābhir mahāvyahṛtibhiḥ tataḥ pratidaivatamṛṣīṃś ca svāhākāraṃ
                              kuryāt śiṣyam api kārayet || </p>

                         <p xml:id="SS.1.2.5"><label>1931 ed. 1.2.5</label> brāhmaṇas trayāṇāṃ
                              varṇānām upanayanaṃ kartum arhati rājanyo dvayasya vaiśyo
                              vaiśyasyaiveti śūdram api kulaguṇasaṃpannaṃ mantravarjam anupanītam
                              adhyāpayed ity eke || </p>

                         <p xml:id="SS.1.2.6"><label>1931 ed. 1.2.6</label> tato 'gniṃ triḥ
                              pariṇīyāgnisākṣikaṃ śiṣyaṃ brūyāt
                              kāmakrodhalobhamohamānāhaṇkārerṣyāpāruṣyapaiśunyānṛtālasyāyaśasyāni
                              hitvā nīcanakharomṇā śucinā kaṣāyavāsasā
                              satyavratabrahmacaryābhivādanatatpareṇā'vaśyaṃ bhavitavyaṃ
                              madanumatasthānagamanaśayanāsanabhojanādhyayanapareṇa bhūtvā
                              matpriyahiteṣu vartitavyaṃ ato 'nyathā te vartamānasyādharmo bhavati
                              aphalā ca vidyā na ca prākāśyaṃ prāpnoti || </p>

                         <p xml:id="SS.1.2.7"><label>1931 ed. 1.2.7</label> ahaṃ vā tvayi
                              samyagvartamāne yady anyathādarśī syām enobhāg bhaveyam aphalavidyaś
                              ca || </p>

                         <p xml:id="SS.1.2.7.a"/>

                         <p xml:id="SS.1.2.8"><label>1931 ed. 1.2.8</label>
                              dvijagurudaridramitrapravrajitopanatasādhvanāthābhyupagatānāṃ
                              cātmabāndhavānām iva svabhaiṣajaiḥ pratikartavyam evaṃ sādhu bhavati
                              vyādhaśākunikapatitapāpakāriṇāṃ ca na pratikartavyaṃ evaṃ vidyā
                              prakāśate mitra<pc> </pc>yaśo<pc> </pc>dharmārtha<pc> </pc>kāmāṃś ca
                              prāpnoti || </p>

                         <p xml:id="SS.1.2.9X"><label>1931 ed. 1.2.9x</label> bhavataś cātra | </p>

                         <l xml:id="SS.1.2.9"><label>1931 ed. 1.2.9</label> kṛṣṇe 'ṣṭamī tannidhane
                              'hanī dve
                              <caesura/>
                               śukle tathā 'py evam ahar dvisandhyam |
                              <caesura/>
                               akālavidyutstanayitnughoṣe
                              <caesura/>
                               svatantrarāṣṭrakṣitipavyathāsu || </l>

                         <l xml:id="SS.1.2.10"><label>1931 ed. 1.2.10</label>
                              śmaśānayānādyatanāhaveṣu
                              <caesura/>
                               mahotsavautpātikadarśaneṣu |
                              <caesura/>
                               nādhyeyam anyeṣu ca yeṣu vaprā
                              <caesura/>
                               nādhīyate nāśucinā ca nityam || </l>

                         <p xml:id="SS1.2.trailer">iti suśrutasaṃhitāyāṃ sūtrasthāne śiṣyopanayanīyo
                              nāma dvitīyo 'dhyāyaḥ ||</p>

                    <div n="4" type="adhyāya">

                         <head>caturtho 'dhyāyaḥ |</head>

                         <l xml:id="SS.1.4.1"><label>1931 ed. 1.4.1</label> athātaḥ prabhāṣaṇīyam
                              adhyāyaṃ vyākhyāsyāmaḥ || </l>

                         <l xml:id="SS.1.4.2"><label>1931 ed. 1.4.2</label> yāthovāca bhagavān
                              dhanvantariḥ || </l>

                         <l xml:id="SS.1.4.3"><label>1931 ed. 1.4.3</label> adhigatam apy adhyayanam
                              aprabhāṣitam arthataḥ kharasya candanabhāra iva kevalaṃ pariśramakaraṃ
                              bhavati || </l>

                         <l xml:id="SS.1.4.4"><label>1931 ed. 1.4.4</label> bhavati cātra |
                              <caesura/>
                               yathā kharaś candanabhāravāhī bhārasya vettā na tu candanasya |
                              <caesura/>
                               evaṃ hi śāstrāṇi baḥūnyadhītya cārtheṣu mūḍhāḥ kharavadvahanti || </l>

                         <l xml:id="SS.1.4.5"><label>1931 ed. 1.4.5</label> tasmāt saviṃśam
                              adhyāyaśatam anupadapādaślokam anuvarṇayitavyam anuśrotavyaṃ ca kasmāt
                              sūkṣmā hi
                              dravyarasaguṇavīryavipākadoṣadhātumalāśayamarmasirāsnāyusandhyasthigarbhasaṃbhavadravyasamūhavibhāgās
                              tathā pranaṣṭaśalyoddharaṇavraṇaviniścayabhagnavikalpāḥ sādhyayāpy
                              apratyākhyeyatā ca vikārāṇām evam ādayaś cānye sahasraśo viśeṣā ye
                              vicintyamānā vimalavipulabuddher api buddhim ākulīkuryuḥ kiṃ punar
                              alpabuddheḥ tasmād avaśyam anupadapādaślokam anuvarṇayitavyam
                              anuśrotavyaṃ ca || </l>

                         <l xml:id="SS.1.4.6"><label>1931 ed. 1.4.6</label> anyaśāstropapannānāṃ
                              cārthānām ihopanītānām arthavaśāt teṣāṃ tadvidyebhya eva vyākhyānam
                              anuśrotavyaṃ kasmāt na hy ekasmin śāstre śakyaḥ sarvaśāstrāṇām
                              avarodhaḥ kartum || </l>

                         <l xml:id="SS.1.4.7"><label>1931 ed. 1.4.7</label> bhavanti cātra |
                              <caesura/>
                               ekaṃ śāstram adhīyāno na vidyāc chāstraniścayam |a
                              <caesura/>
                               tasmād bahuśrutaḥ śāstraṃ vijānīyāc cikitsakaḥ || </l>

                         <l xml:id="SS.1.4.8"><label>1931 ed. 1.4.8</label> śāstraṃ gurumukhodbīrṇam
                              ādāyopāsya cāsakṛt |
                              <caesura/>
                               yaḥ karmakurute vaiyaḥ sa vaidyo 'nye tu taskarāḥ || </l>

                         <l xml:id="SS.1.4.9"><label>1931 ed. 1.4.9</label> aupadhenavam aurabhraṃ
                              sauśrutaṃ pauṣkalāvatam |
                              <caesura/>
                               śeṣāṇāṃ śalyatantrāṇāṃ mūlāny etāni nirdiśet || </l>

                         <p ana="1.4.trailer">iti suśrutasaṃhitāyāṃ sūtrasthāne prabhāṣanīyo nāma
                              caturtho 'dhyāyaḥ ||</p>
                    </div>

                         <head>śaṣṭho 'dhyāyaḥ |</head>

                         <l xml:id="SS.1.6.1"><label>1931 ed. 1.6.1</label> athāta ṛtucaryam
                              adhyāyaṃ vyākhyāsyāmaḥ || </l>

                         <l xml:id="SS.1.6.2"><label>1931 ed. 1.6.2</label> yathovāca bhagavān
                              dhanvantariḥ || </l>

                         <l xml:id="SS.1.6.3"><label>1931 ed. 1.6.3</label> kālo hi nāma bhagavān
                              svayambhur anādimadhyanidhano 'tra rasavyāpatsampattī jīvitamaraṇe ca
                              manuṣyāṇām āyatte | sa sūkṣmām api kalāṃ na līyata iti kālaḥ
                              saṃkalayati kālayati vā bhūtānīti kālaḥ || </l>

                         <l xml:id="SS.1.6.4"><label>1931 ed. 1.6.4</label> tasya saṃvatsarātmano
                              bhagavān ādityo gativiśeṣeṇa
                              nimeṣakāṣṭhākalāmuhūrtāhorātrapakṣamāsartvayanasaṃvatsarayugapravibhāgaṃ
                              karoti || </l>

                         <l xml:id="SS.1.6.5"><label>1931 ed. 1.6.5</label> tatra
                              laghvakṣaroccāraṇamātro 'kṣinimeṣaḥ pañcadaśā'kṣinimeṣāḥ kāṣṭhā
                              triṃśatkāṣṭhāḥ kalā viṃśatikalo muhūrtaḥ kalādaśabhāgaś ca
                              triṃśanmuhūrtam ahorātraṃ pañcadaśāhorātrāṇi pakṣaḥ sa ca dvividhaḥ
                              śuklaḥ kṛṣṇaś ca tau māsaḥ || </l>

                         <l xml:id="SS.1.6.6"><label>1931 ed. 1.6.6</label> tatra māghādayo dvādaśa
                              māsāḥ saṃvatsaraḥ dvimāsikam ṛtuṃ kṛtva ṣaḍṛtavo bhavanti te
                              śiśiravasantagrīṣmavarṣāśaraddhemantāḥ teṣaṃ tapastapsyau śiśiraḥ
                              madhumādhavau vasantaḥ śuciśukrau grīṣmaḥ nabhonabhasyau varśāḥ
                              iṣorjau śarat sahaḥsahasyau hemanta iti || </l>

                         <l xml:id="SS.1.6.7"><label>1931 ed. 1.6.7</label> ta ete
                              śītoṣṇavarṣalakṣaṇāś candrād ity ayoḥ kālavibhāgakaratvād ayane dve
                              bhavato dakṣiṇam uttaraṃ ca | tayor dakṣiṇaṃ varṣāśaraddhemantāḥ teṣu
                              bhagavān āpyāyate somaḥ amlalavaṇamadhurāś ca rasā balavanto bhavanti
                              uttarottaraṃ ca sarvaprāṇināṃ balam abhivardhate | uttaraṃ ca
                              śiśiravasantagrīṣmāḥ teṣu bhagavān āpyāyate 'rkaḥ tiktakaṣāyakaṭukāś
                              ca rasā balavanto bhavanti uttarottaraṃ ca sarvaprāṇināṃ balam
                              apahīyate || </l>

                         <l xml:id="SS.1.6.8"><label>1931 ed. 1.6.8</label> bhavati cātra | </l>

                         <l xml:id="SS.1.6.8ab"><label>1931 ed. 1.6.8ab</label> śītāṃśuḥ kledayaty
                              urvīṃ vivasvān śoṣayaty api | </l>

                         <l xml:id="SS.1.6.8cd"><label>1931 ed. 1.6.8cd</label> tāv ubhāv api
                              saṃśritya vāyuḥ pālayati prajāḥ || </l>

                         <l xml:id="SS.1.6.9"><label>1931 ed. 1.6.9</label> atha khalv ayane dve
                              yugapat saṃvatsaro bhavati te tu pañca yugam iti saṃjñāṃ labhante sa
                              eṣa nimeṣādir yugaparyantaḥ kālaś cakravat parivartamānaḥ kālacakram
                              ucyata ity eke || </l>

                         <l xml:id="SS.1.6.10"><label>1931 ed. 1.6.10</label> iha tu
                              varṣāśaraddhemantavasantagrīṣmaprāvṛṣaḥ ṣaḍṛtavo bhavanti
                              doṣopacayaprakopopaśamanimittaṃ te tu bhādrapadādyena dvimāsikena
                              vyākhyātāḥ tad yathā bhādrapadāśvayujau varṣāḥ kārtikamārgaśīrṣau
                              śarat pauṣamāghau hemantaḥ phālgunacaitrau vasantaḥ vaiśākhajyeṣṭhau
                              grīṣmaḥ āṣāḍhaśrāvaṇau prāvṛḍ iti || </l>

                         <l xml:id="SS.1.6.11"><label>1931 ed. 1.6.11</label> tatra varṣāsv
                              oṣadhayas taruṇyo 'lpavīryā āpaś cāprasannāḥ kṣitimalaprāyāḥ tā
                              upayujyamānā nabhasi meghāvatate jalapraklinnāyāṃ bhūmau klinnadehānāṃ
                              prāṇināṃ śītavātaviṣṭambhitāgnīnāṃ vidahyante vidāhāt pittasaṃcayam
                              āpādayanti sa saṃcayaḥ śaradi praviralameghe viyaty upaśuṣyati paṅke
                              'rkakiraṇapravilāyitaḥ paittikān vyādhīn janayati | tā evauṣadhayaḥ
                              kālapariṇāmāt pariṇatavīryā balavatyo hemante bhavanty āpaś ca
                              prasannāḥ snigdhā atyarthaṃ gurvyaś ca tā upayujyamānā mandakiraṇatvād
                              bhānoḥ satuṣārapavanopastambhitadehānāṃ dehinām avidagdhāḥ snehāc
                              chaityād gauravād upalepāc ca śleṣmasaṃcayam āpādayanti sa saṃcayo
                              vasante 'rkraśmipravilāyita īṣatstabdhadehānāṃ dehināṃ ślaiṣmikān
                              vyādhīn janayati | tā evauṣadhayo nidāghe niḥsārā rūkṣā atimātraṃ
                              laghvyo bhavanty āpaś ca tā upayujyamānāḥ sūryapratāpopaśoṣitadehānāṃ
                              dehināṃ raukṣyāl laghutvād vaiśadyāc ca vāyoḥ saṃcayam āpādyanti sa
                              saṃcayaḥ prāvṛṣi cātyarthaṃ jalopaklinnāyāṃ bhūmau klinnadehānāṃ
                              prāṇināṃ śītavātavarṣerito vātikān vyādhīn janayati | evam eṣa doṣāṇāṃ
                              saṃcayaprakopahetur uktaḥ ||</l>

                              yantrakarmaṇām || </l>

                         <l xml:id="SS.1.7.4"><label>1931 ed. 1.7.4</label> tatra
                              manaḥśarīrābādhakarāṇi śalyāni teṣām āharaṇopāyo yantrāṇi || </l>

                         <l xml:id="SS.1.7.5"><label>1931 ed. 1.7.5</label> tāni ṣaṭprakārāṇi tad
                              yathā svastikayantrāṇi saṃdaṃśayantrāṇi tālayantrāṇi nāḍīyantrāṇi
                              śalākāyantrāṇi upayantrāṇi ceti || </l>

                         <l xml:id="SS.1.7.6"><label>1931 ed. 1.7.6</label> tatra caturviṃśatiḥ
                              svastikayantrāṇi dve saṃdaṃśayantre dve eva tālayantre viṃśatirnāḍyaḥ
                              aṣṭāviṃśatiḥ śalākāḥ panñcaviṃśatirupayantrāṇi || </l>

                         <l xml:id="SS.1.7.7"><label>1931 ed. 1.7.7</label> tāni prāyaśo lauhāni
                              bhavanti tatpratirūpakāṇi vā tadalābhe || </l>

                         <l xml:id="SS.1.7.8"><label>1931 ed. 1.7.8</label> tatra nānāprakārāṇāṃ
                              vyālānāṃ mṛgapakṣiṇāṃ mukhair mukhāni yantrāṇāṃ prāyaśaḥ sadṛśāni
                              tasmāt tatsārūpyādāgamādupadeśādanyayantradarśanādyuktitaś ca kārayet
                              || </l>

                              kharaślakṣṇamukhāni ca | </l>

                         <l xml:id="SS.1.7.9cd"><label>1931 ed. 1.7.9cd</label> sudṛḍhāni surūpāṇi
                              sugrahāṇi ca kārayet || </l>

                         <l xml:id="SS.1.7.10"><label>1931 ed. 1.7.10</label> tatra svastikayantrāṇi
                              aṣṭādaśāṅgulapramāṇāni
                              siṃhavyāghravṛkatarakṣvṛkṣadvīpimārjāraśṛgālamṛgair
                              ivārukakākakaṅkakuraracāsabhāsaśaśaghātyulūkacilliśyenagṛdhrakrauñcabhṛṅgarājāñjalikarṇāvabhañjananandi(ā.ndī)mukhamukhāni
                              masūrākṛtibhiḥ kīlair avabaddhāni mūle 'ṅkuśavadāvṛttavāraṅgāṇi
                              asthividaṣṭaśalyoddharaṇārtham upadiśyante || </l>

                         <l xml:id="SS.1.7.11"><label>1931 ed. 1.7.11</label> sanigraho 'nigrahaś ca
                              saṃdaṃśau ṣoḍaśāṅgulau bhvataḥ tau
                              svaṅnāṃsasirāsnāyugataśalyoddharaṇārtham upadiśyete || </l>

                         <l xml:id="SS.1.7.12"><label>1931 ed. 1.7.12</label> tālayantre
                              dvādaśāṅgule matsyatālavadekatāladvitālake
                              karṇanāsānāḍīśalyānāmāharaṇārtham || </l>

                         <l xml:id="SS.1.7.13"><label>1931 ed. 1.7.13</label> nāḍīyantrāṇi
                              apyanekaprakārāṇi anekaprayojanāni ekatomukhānyubhayatomukhāni ca tāni
                              srotogataśalyoddharaṇārthaṃ rogadarśanārthaṃ ācūṣaṇārthaṃ
                              kriyāsaukaryārthaṃ ceti tāni srotodvārapariṇāhāni yathāyogadīrghāṇi ca
                              | tatra
                              bhagandarārśovraṇabastyuttarabastimūtravṛddhidakodaradhūmaniruddhaprakaśasanniruddhagudayantrāṇy
                              alābūśṛṅgayantrāṇi coprariṣṭād vakṣyāmaḥ || </l>

                         <l xml:id="SS.1.7.14"><label>1931 ed. 1.7.14</label> śalākāyantrāṇy api
                              nānāprakārāṇi nānāprayojanāni yathāyogapariṇāhadīrghāṇi ca teṣāṃ
                              gaṇḍūpadasarpaphaṇaśarapuṅkhabaḍiśamukhe dve dve
                              eṣaṇavyūhanacālanāharaṇārtham upadiśyete masūradalamātramukhe dve
                              kiṃcidānatāgre srotogataśalyoddharaṇārthaṃ ṣaṭ kārpāsakṛtoṣṇīṣāṇi
                              pramārjanakriyāsu trīṇi darvyākṛtīni khallamukhāni
                              kṣārauṣadhapraṇidhānārthaṃ trīṇyanyāni jāmbavavadanāni
                              trīṇyaṅkuśavadanāni ṣaḍevāgnikarmasvabhipretāni
                              nāsārbudaharaṇārthamekaṃ kolāsthidalamātramukhaṃ khallatīkṣṇoṣṭhaṃ
                              añjanārthamekaṃ kalāyaparimaṇḍalamubhuyato mukulāgraṃ
                              mūtramārgaviśodhanārthamekaṃ mālatīpuṣpavṛntāgrapramāṇaparimaṇḍalam
                              iti || </l>

                         <l xml:id="SS.1.7.15"><label>1931 ed. 1.7.15</label>
                              upayantrāṇyapi-rajjuveṇikāpaṭṭacarmāntavalkalalatāvastrāṣṭhīlāśmamudgarapāṇipādatalāṅgulijihvādantanakhamukhabālāśvakaṭakaśākhāṣṭhīvanapravāhaṇaharṣāyaskāntamayāni
                              kṣārāgnibheṣajāni ceti || </l>

                         <l xml:id="SS.1.7.16ab"><label>1931 ed. 1.7.16ab</label> etāni dehe
                              sarvasmin dehasyāvayave tathā | </l>

                         <l xml:id="SS.1.7.16cd"><label>1931 ed. 1.7.16cd</label> saṃdhau koṣṭhe
                              dhamanyāṃ ca yathāyogaṃ prayojayet || </l>

                         <l xml:id="SS.1.7.17"><label>1931 ed. 1.7.17</label> yantrakarmāṇi tu
                              nirghātanapūraṇabandhanavyūhanavartanacālanavivartanavivaraṇapīḍanamārgaviśodhanavikarṣaṇāharaṇāñchanonnamanavinamanabhañjanonmathanācūṣaṇaiṣaṇadāraṇarjūkaraṇaprakṣālanapradhamanapramārjanāni
                              caturviṃśatiḥ || </l>

                         <l xml:id="SS.1.7.18ab"><label>1931 ed. 1.7.18ab</label> svabuddhyā cāpi
                              vibhajedyantrakarmāṇi buddhimān | </l>

                         <l xml:id="SS.1.7.18cd"><label>1931 ed. 1.7.18cd</label>
                              asaṃkhyeyavikalpatvāc chalyānām iti niścayaḥ || </l>

                         <l xml:id="SS.1.7.19"><label>1931 ed. 1.7.19</label> tatra atisthūlaṃ
                              asāraṃ atidīrghaṃ atihrasvaṃ agrāhi viṣamagrāhi vakraṃ śithilaṃ
                              atyunnataṃ mṛdukīlaṃ mṛdumukhaṃ mṛdupāśam iti dvādaśa yantradoṣāḥ || </l>

                         <l xml:id="SS.1.7.20ab"><label>1931 ed. 1.7.20ab</label> etair doṣair
                              vinirmuktaṃ yantramaṣṭādaśāṅgulam | </l>

                         <l xml:id="SS.1.7.20cd"><label>1931 ed. 1.7.20cd</label> praśastaṃ bhiṣajā
                              jñeyaṃ taddhi karmasu yojayet || </l>

                         <l xml:id="SS.1.7.21ab"><label>1931 ed. 1.7.21ab</label> dṛśyaṃ
                              siṃhamukhādyais tu gūḍhaṃ kaṅkamukhādibhiḥ | </l>

                         <l xml:id="SS.1.7.21cd"><label>1931 ed. 1.7.21cd</label> nirharet tu śanaiḥ
                              śalyaṃ śa(ā.śā)strayuktivyapekṣayā || </l>

                         <l xml:id="SS.1.7.22ab"><label>1931 ed. 1.7.22ab</label> ni(ā.vi)vartate
                              sādhvavagāhate ca śalyaṃ nigṛhyoddharate ca yasmāt || </l>

                         <l xml:id="SS.1.7.22cd"><label>1931 ed. 1.7.22cd</label> yantreṣv ataḥ
                              kaṅkamukhaṃ pradhānaṃ sthāneṣu sarveṣv adhi(ā.vi)kāri caiva || </l>
                         <p ana="trailer">iti suśrutasaṃhitāyāṃ sūtrasthāne yantravidhirnāma saptamo
                              'dhyāyaḥ ||</p>

                    <div n="8" type="adhyāya">
                         <head>aṣṭamo 'dhyāyaḥ |</head>

                         <l xml:id="SS.1.8.1"><label>1931 ed. 1.8.1</label> athātaḥ
                              śastrāvacāraṇīyam adhyāyaṃ vyākhyāsyāmaḥ || </l>

                         <l xml:id="SS.1.8.2"><label>1931 ed. 1.8.2</label> yathovāca bhagavān
                              dhanvantariḥ || </l>

                         <l xml:id="SS.1.8.3"><label>1931 ed. 1.8.3</label> viṃśatiḥ śastrāṇi; tad
                              yathā— maṇḍalāgrakarapatra<pc> </pc>vṛddhipatra<pc
                                   > </pc>nakhaśastra<pc
                                   > </pc>mudrikotpalapatrakārdhadhāra<pc> </pc>sūcī<pc
                                   > </pc>kuśapatrāṭīmukha<pc> </pc>śarārimukhāntarmukha<pc
                                   > </pc>trikūrcaka<pc> </pc>kuṭhārikā<pc
                                   > </pc>vrīhimukhārā<pc> </pc>vetasapatraka<pc
                                   > </pc>baḍiśa<pc> </pc>dantaśaṅkveṣaṇya iti || </l>

                         <l xml:id="SS.1.8.4"><label>1931 ed. 1.8.4</label> tatra
                              maṇḍalāgrakarapatre syātāṃ chedane lekhane ca, vṛddhipatra<pc
                                   > </pc>nakhaśastra<pc> </pc>mudrikotpalapatrakārdhadhārāṇi
                              chedane bhedane ca,
                              sūcīkuśapatrāṭī(ṭā)mukhaśarārimukhāntarmukhatrikūrcakāni visrāvaṇe,
                                   kuṭhārikā<pc> </pc>vrīhimukhārā<pc> </pc>vetasapatrakāṇi vyadhane
                              sūcī ca, baḍiśaṃ dantaśaṅkuś cāharaṇe, eṣaṇy eṣaṇe ānulomye ca sūcyaḥ
                              sīvane; ity aṣṭavidhe karmaṇy upayogaḥ śastrāṇāṃ vyākkhyātaḥ || </l>

                         <l xml:id="SS.1.8.5"><label>1931 ed. 1.8.5</label> teṣām atha yathāyogaṃ
                              grahaṇasamāsopāyaḥ karmasu vakṣyate— tatra vṛddhipatraṃ
                              vṛntaphalasādhāraṇe bhāge gṛhṇīyāt, bhedanāny evaṃ sarvāṇi,
                              vṛddhipatraṃ maṇḍalāgraṃ ca kiṃcid uttānena pāṇinā lekhane bahuśo
                              'vacāryaṃ, vṛntāgre visrāvaṇāni, viśeṣeṇa tu
                              bālavṛddhasukumārabhīrunārīṇāṃ rājñāṃ rājamā(pu)trāṇāṃ ca trikūrcakena
                              visrāvayet, talapracchādita<pc> </pc>vṛntam aṅguṣṭhapradeśinībhyāṃ
                              vrīhimukhaṃ, kuṭhārikāṃ vāmahastanyastām
                                   itarahastamadhyamāṅgulyā'ṅguṣṭhaviṣṭabdhay<pc> </pc>'bhihanyāt,
                              ārākarapatraiṣaṇyo mūle, śeṣāṇi tu yathāyogaṃ gṛhṇīyāt || </l>

                         <l xml:id="SS.1.8.6"><label>1931 ed. 1.8.6</label> teṣāṃ nāmabhir
                              evākṛtayaḥ prāyeṇa vyākhyātāḥ || </l>

                         <l xml:id="SS.1.8.7-8"><label>1931 ed. 1.8.7</label> tatra
                              nakhaśastraiṣaṇyāv aṣṭāṅgule, sūcyo vakṣyante,
                              (pradeśinyagraparvapradeśapramāṇā mudrikā, daśāṅgulā śarārimukhī sā ca
                              (yā sā) kartarīti kathyate |), śeṣāṇi tu ṣaḍaṅgulāni || <label>1931
                                   ed. 1.8.8</label> tāni sugrahāṇi sulohāni sudhārāṇi surūpāṇi
                              susamāhitamukhāgrāṇi akarālāni ceti śastrasaṃpat || </l>

                         <l xml:id="SS.1.8.9"><label>1931 ed. 1.8.9</label> tatra vakraṃ, kuṇṭhaṃ,
                              khaṇḍaṃ, kharadhāram, atisthūlam, atyalpam, atidīrgham, atihrasvam,
                              ity aṣṭau śastradoṣāḥ | ato viparītaguṇam ādadīta, anyatra karapatrāt;
                              tad dhi kharadhāram asthicchedanārtham || </l>

                         <l xml:id="SS.1.8.10"><label>1931 ed. 1.8.10</label> tatra dhārā bhedanānāṃ
                              māsūrī, lekhanānām ardhamāsūrī, vyadhanānāṃ visrāvaṇānāṃ ca kaiśikī,
                              chedanānām ardhakaiśikīti || </l>

                         <l xml:id="SS.1.8.11"><label>1931 ed. 1.8.11</label> baḍiśaṃ dantaśaṅkuś
                              cānatāgre | tīkṣṇakaṇṭakaprathamayavapatramukhyeṣaṇī
                              (gaṇḍūpadākāramukhī ca) || </l>

                         <l xml:id="SS.1.8.12"><label>1931 ed. 1.8.12</label> teṣāṃ pāyanā trividhā
                              kśārodakataileṣu | tatra kṣārapāyitaṃ śaraśalyāsthicchedaneṣu
                              udakapāyitaṃ māṃsacchedanabhedanapāṭaneṣu tailapāyitaṃ
                              sirāvyadhanasnāyucchedaneṣu || </l>

                         <l xml:id="SS.1.8.13"><label>1931 ed. 1.8.13</label> teṣāṃ niśānārthaṃ
                              ślakṣṇaśilā māṣavarṇā dhārāsaṃsthāpanārthaṃ śālmalīphalakam iti || </l>

                         <l xml:id="SS.1.8.14"><label>1931 ed. 1.8.14</label> bhavati cātra—</l>

                         <l xml:id="SS.1.8.14a"><label>1931 ed. 1.8.14</label> yadā suniśitaṃ
                              śastraṃ romacchedi susaṃsthitam |
                              <caesura/>
                               sugṛhītaṃ pramāṇena tadā karmasu yojayet || </l>

                         <l xml:id="SS.1.8.15-16"><label>1931 ed. 1.8.15</label> anuśastrāṇi tu
                                   tvaksāra<pc> </pc>sphaṭika<pc> </pc>kāca<pc
                                   > </pc>kuruvinda<pc> </pc>jalaukogni<pc
                              > </pc>kṣāranakhagojīśephālikāśākapatrakarīrabālāṅgulaya iti ||
                              <caesura/>
                              <label>1931 ed. 1.8.16</label> śiśūnāṃ śastrabhīrūṇāṃ śastrābhāve ca
                              yojayet |
                              <caesura/>
                               tvaksārādicaturvargaṃ chedye ca buddhimān || </l>

                         <l xml:id="SS.1.8.17"><label>1931 ed. 1.8.17</label> āhārya<pc
                                   > </pc>cchedya<pc> </pc>bhedyeṣu nakhaṃ śakyeṣu yojayet |
                              <caesura/>
                               vidhiḥ pravakṣyate paścāt kṣāravahnijalaukasām || </l>

                         <l xml:id="SS.1.8.18"><label>1931 ed. 1.8.18</label> ye syur mukhagatā rogā
                              netravartmagatāś ca ye |
                              <caesura/>
                               gojī<pc> </pc>śephālikā<pc> </pc>śākapatrair visrāvayet tu tān || </l>

                         <l xml:id="SS.1.8.19"><label>1931 ed. 1.8.19</label> eṣyeṣv eṣaṇyalābhe tu
                              bālāṅgulyaṅkurā hitāḥ ||
                              <caesura/>
                               śastrāṇy etāni matimān śuddhaśaikyāyasāni tu ||
                              <caesura/>
                               kārayet karaṇaprāptaṃ karmāraṃ karmakovidam || </l>

                         <l xml:id="SS.1.8.20"><label>1931 ed. 1.8.20</label> prayogajñasya
                              vaidyasya siddhir bhavati nity aśaḥ |
                              <caesura/>
                               tasmāt paricayaṃ kuryāc chastrāṇāṃ grahaṇe sadā || </l>

                         <p ana="trailer">iti suśrutasaṃhitāyāṃ sūtrasthāne śastrāvacāraṇīyo
                              nāmāṣṭamo 'dhyāyaḥ ||</p>

                    <div n="9" type="adhyāya">
                         <head>navamo 'dhyāyaḥ |</head>

                         <l xml:id="SS.1.9.1"><label>1931 ed. 1.9.1</label> athāto yogyāsūtrīyam
                              adhyāyaṃ vyākhyāsyāmaḥ || </l>

                         <l xml:id="SS.1.9.2"><label>1931 ed. 1.9.2</label> yathovāca bhagavān
                              dhanvantariḥ || </l>

                         <l xml:id="SS.1.9.3"><label>1931 ed. 1.9.3</label> adhigatasarvaśāstrārtham
                              api śiṣyaṃ yogyāṃ kārayet | snehādiṣu chedyādīṣu ca karmapatham
                              upadiśet | subahuśruto 'pyakṛtayogyaḥ karmasvayogyo bhavati || </l>

                         <l xml:id="SS.1.9.4"><label>1931 ed. 1.9.4</label> tatra
                              puṣpaphalālābūkālindakatrapusai(ā.so)rvārukarkārukaprabhṛtiṣu
                              chedyaviśeṣān darśayet utkartanaparikartanāni copadiśet
                              dṛtibastiprasevakaprabhṛtiṣūdakapaṅkapūrṇeṣu bhedyayogyāṃ saromṇi
                              carmaṇyātate lekhyasya mṛtapaśusirāsūtpalanāleṣu ca vedhyasya
                              ghuṇopahatakāṣṭhaveṇunalanālīśuṣkālābūmukheṣveṣyasya
                              panasabimbībilvaphalamajjamṛtapaśudanteṣvāhāryasya madhūcchiṣṭopalipte
                              śālmalīphalake visrāvyasya sūkṣmaghanavastrāntayor mṛducarmāntayoś ca
                              sīvyasya pustamayapuruśāṅgapratyaṅgaviśeṣeṣu bandhanayogyāṃ
                              mṛducarmamāṃsapeśīṣūtpalanāleṣu ca karṇasandhibandhayogyāṃ mṛduṣu
                              māṃsakhaṇḍeṣv agnikṣārayogyāṃ
                              udakapūṇaghaṭapārśvasrotasyalābūmukhādiṣu ca
                              netrapraṇidhānabastivraṇabastipīḍanayogyām iti || </l>

                         <l xml:id="SS.1.9.5"><label>1931 ed. 1.9.5</label> bhavataś cātra | </l>

                         <l xml:id="SS.1.9.5ab"><label>1931 ed. 1.9.5ab</label> evam ādiṣu medhāvī
                              yogyārheṣu yathāvidhi | </l>

                         <l xml:id="SS.1.9.5cd"><label>1931 ed. 1.9.5cd</label> dravyeṣu yogyāṃ
                              kurvāṇo na pramuhyati karmasu || </l>

                         <l xml:id="SS.1.9.6ab"><label>1931 ed. 1.9.6ab</label> tasmāt
                              kauśalamanvicchan śastrakṣārāgnikarmasu | </l>

                         <l xml:id="SS.1.9.6cd"><label>1931 ed. 1.9.6cd</label> yasya yatreha
                              sādharmyaṃ tatra yogyāṃ samācaret || </l>
                         <p ana="trailer">iti suśrutasaṃhitāyāṃ sūtrasthāne yogyāsūtrīyo nāma navamo
                              'dhyāyaḥ || </p>
                    </div>
                    <div n="10" type="adhyāya">
                         <head>daśamo 'dhyāyaḥ |</head>

                         <l xml:id="SS.1.10.1"><label>1931 ed. 1.10.1</label> athāto
                              viśikhānupraveśanīyam adhyāyaṃ vyākhyāsyāmaḥ || </l>

                         <l xml:id="SS.1.10.2"><label>1931 ed. 1.10.2</label> yathovāca bhagavān
                              dhanvantariḥ || </l>

                         <l xml:id="SS.1.10.3"><label>1931 ed. 1.10.3</label>
                              adhigatatantreṇopāsitatantrārthena dṛṣṭakarmaṇā kṛtayogyena śāstraṃ
                              nigadatā rājānujñātena nīcanakharomṇā ṣucinā śuklavastraparihitena
                              chatravatā daṇḍahastena sopānatkenānuddhataveśena sumanasā
                              kalyāṇābhivyāhāreṇākuhakena bandhubhūtena bhūtānāṃ susahāyavatā
                              vaidyena niśikhā'nupraveṣṭavyā || </l>

                         <l xml:id="SS.1.10.4"><label>1931 ed. 1.10.4</label> tato
                              dūtanimittaśakunamaṅgalānulomyenāturagṛhamabhigamya upaviśya
                              āturamabhipaśyet spṛśet pṛcchec ca tribhir etair vijñānopāyai rogāḥ
                              prāyaśo veditavyā ity eke tat tu na samyak ṣaḍvidho hi rogāṇāṃ
                              vijñānopāyaḥ tad yathā pañcabhiḥ śrotrādibhiḥ praśnena ceti || </l>

                         <l xml:id="SS.1.10.5"><label>1931 ed. 1.10.5</label> tatra
                              śrotrendriyavijñeyā viśeṣā rogeṣu vraṇāsrāvanijñānīyādiṣu vakṣyante
                              tatra saphenaṃ raktam īrayann anilaḥ saśabdo nirgacchati ity evam
                              ādayaḥ sparśanendriyavijñeyāḥ śītoṣṇaślakṣṇakarkaśamṛdukaṭhinatvād
                              ayaḥ sparśaviśeṣā jvaraśophādeṣu cakṣurindriyavijñeyāḥ
                              śarīropacayāpacayāyurlakṣaṇabalavarṇavikārādayaḥ rasanendriyavijñeyāḥ
                              pramehādiṣu rasaviśeṣāḥ ghrāṇendriyavijñeyā ariṣṭaliṅgādiṣu
                              vraṇānāmavraṇānāṃ ca gandhaviśeṣāḥ praśnena ca vijānīyāddeśaṃ kālaṃ
                              jātiṃ sātmyamātaṅkasamutpattiṃ vedanāsamucchrāyaṃ balamantaragniṃ
                              vātamūtrapurīṣāṇāṃ pravṛttyapravṛttī kālaprakarṣādīṃś ca viśeṣān |
                              ātmasadṛśeṣu vijñānābhyupāyeṣu tatsthānīyair jānīyāt || </l>

                         <l xml:id="SS.1.10.6"><label>1931 ed. 1.10.6</label> bhavati cātra | </l>

                         <l xml:id="SS.1.10.6ab"><label>1931 ed. 1.10.6ab</label> mithyādṛṣṭā vikārā
                              hi durākhyātās tathaiva ca | </l>

                         <l xml:id="SS.1.10.6cd"><label>1931 ed. 1.10.6cd</label> tathā
                              duṣparimṛṣṭāś ca mohayeyuś cikitsakam || </l>

                         <l xml:id="SS.1.10.6ef"/>

                         <l xml:id="SS.1.10.7"><label>1931 ed. 1.10.7</label> yāpayet asādhyān
                              nopakramet parisaṃvatsarotthitāṃś ca vikārān prāyaśo varjayet || </l>

                         <l xml:id="SS.1.10.8"><label>1931 ed. 1.10.8</label> tatra sādhyā api
                              vyādhayaḥ prāyeṇaiṣāṃ duścikitsyatamā bhavanti | tad yathā
                              śrotriyanṛpatistrībālavṛddhabhīrurājasevakakitavadrubalavaidyavidagdhavyādhigopakadaridrakṛpaṇakrodhanānāmanātmavatāmanāthānāṃ
                              ca evaṃ nirūpya cikitsāṃ kurvan dharmārthakāmayaśāṃsi prāpnoti || </l>


                         <l xml:id="SS.1.10.9"><label>1931 ed. 1.10.9</label> bhavati cātra | </l>

                         <l xml:id="SS.1.10.9ab"><label>1931 ed. 1.10.9ab</label> strībhiḥ sahāsyāṃ
                              saṃvāsaṃ parihāsaṃ ca varjayet | </l>

                         <l xml:id="SS.1.10.9cd"><label>1931 ed. 1.10.9cd</label> dattaṃ ca tābhyo
                              nādeyam annād anyad bhiṣagvaraiḥ || </l>

                         <l xml:id="SS.1.10.9ef"/>
                         <l xml:id="SS.1.10.9ef1"/>
                         <l xml:id="SS.1.10.9gh"/>
                         <l xml:id="SS.1.10.9gh1"/>

                         <p ana="trailer">iti suśrutasaṃhitāyāṃ sūtrasthāne viśikhānupraveśanīyo
                              nāma daśamo 'dhyāyaḥ || </p>

                    <div n="11" type="adhyāya">
                         <head>ekādaśo 'dhyāyaḥ |</head>

                         <l xml:id="SS.1.11.1"><label>1931 ed. 1.11.1</label> athātaḥ
                              kṣārapākavidhim adhyāyaṃ vyākhyāsyāmaḥ || </l>

                         <l xml:id="SS.1.11.2"><label>1931 ed. 1.11.2</label> yathovāca bhagavān
                              dhanvantariḥ || </l>

                         <l xml:id="SS.1.11.3"><label>1931 ed. 1.11.3</label> śastrānuśastrebhyaḥ
                              kṣāraḥ pradhānatamaḥ chedyabhedyalekhyakaraṇāt tridoṣaghnatvād
                              viśeṣakriyāvacāraṇāc ca || </l>

                         <l xml:id="SS.1.11.4"><label>1931 ed. 1.11.4</label> tatra kṣaraṇāt
                              kṣaṇanād vā kṣāraḥ || </l>

                         <l xml:id="SS.1.11.5"><label>1931 ed. 1.11.5</label> nānauṣadhisamavāyāt
                              tridoṣaghnaḥ śuklatvāt saumyaḥ tasya saumyasyāpi sato
                              dahanapacanadāraṇādiśaktiraviruddhā sa khalv
                              āgneyauṣadhiguṇabhūyiṣṭhatvāt kaṭuka uṣṇastīkṣṇaḥ pa(ā.pā)cano
                              vilayanaḥ śodhano ropaṇaḥ śoṣaṇaḥ stambhano lekhanaḥ
                              kṛmyāmakaphakuṣṭhaviṣamedasām upahantā puṃstvasya cātisevitaḥ || </l>

                         <l xml:id="SS.1.11.6"><label>1931 ed. 1.11.6</label> sa dvividhaḥ
                              pratisāraṇīyaḥ pānīyaś ca || </l>

                         <l xml:id="SS.1.11.7"><label>1931 ed. 1.11.7</label> tatra pratisāraṇīyaḥ
                              kuṣṭhakiṭibhadadrumaṇḍalakilāsabhagandarārbudārśoduṣṭavraṇanāḍīcarmakīlatilakālakanyacchavyaṅgamaśakabāhyavidradhikṛmiviṣādiṣūpadiśyate
                              saptasu ca mukharogeṣūpajihvādhijihvopakuśadantavaidarbheṣu tisṛṣu ca
                              rohiṇīṣu eteṣv evānuśastrapraṇidhānam uktam || </l>

                         <l xml:id="SS.1.11.8"><label>1931 ed. 1.11.8</label> pānīyas tu
                              garagulmodarāgnisaṅgājīrṇārocakānāhaśarkarāśmaryābhyantaravidradhikṛmiviṣārśaḥsūpayujyate
                              || </l>

                         <l xml:id="SS.1.11.9"><label>1931 ed. 1.11.9</label> ahitastu
                              raktapitta(ā.tti)jvaritapittaprakṛtibālavṛddhadurbalabhramamadamūrcchātimiraparītebhyo
                              'nyebhyaś caivaṃvidhebhyaḥ || </l>

                         <l xml:id="SS.1.11.10"><label>1931 ed. 1.11.10</label> taṃ cetarakṣāravad
                              dagdhvā parisrāvayet tasya vistaro 'nyatra || </l>

                         <l xml:id="SS.1.11.11"><label>1931 ed. 1.11.11</label> athetaras trividho
                              mṛdurmadhyastīkṣṇaś ca | taṃ cikīrṣuḥ śaradi girisānujaṃ śucir upoṣya
                              praśaste 'hani praśastadeśajātam anupahataṃ madhyamavayasaṃ
                              mahāntamasitamuṣkakamadhivāsyāparedyuḥ pāṭayitvā svaṇḍaśaḥ
                              prakalpyāvapāṭya nirvāte deśe nicitiṃ kṛtvā sudhāśarkarāś ca prakṣipya
                              nilanālair ādīpayet | athopaśānte 'gnau tadbhasma
                              pṛthaggṛhṇīyādbhasmaśarkarāś ca | athānenaiva vidhānena
                              kuṭajapalāśāśvakarṇapāribhadrakabibhītakāragvadhatilvakārkasnuhyapāmārgapāṭalānaktamālavṛṣakadalīcitrakapūtīkendravṛkṣāsphotāśvamārakasaptacchadāgnimanthaguñjāś
                              catasraś ca kośātakīḥ samūlaphalapatraśākhā dahet | tataḥ kṣāradroṇam
                              udakadroṇaiḥ ṣaḍbhir āloḍya mūtrair vā yathoktair ekaviṃśatikṛtvaḥ
                              parisrāvya mahati kaṭāhe śanair darvyāvaghaṭṭayan vipacet | sa yadā
                              bhavaty accho raktas tīkṣṇaḥ picchilaś ca tamādāya mahati vastre
                              parisrāvyetaraṃ vibhajya punar agnāv adhiśrayet | tata eva
                              cakṣārodakāt kuḍavamadhyardhaṃ vā'panayet | tataḥ
                              kaṭaśarkarābhasmaśarkarākṣīrapākaśaṅkhanābhīragnivarṇāḥ kṛtvā+āyase
                              pātre tasminn eva kṣārodake niṣicya piṣṭvā tenaiva dvidroṇe
                              'ṣṭapalasaṃmitaṃ śaṅkhānābhyādīnāṃ pramāṇaṃ prativāpya satatam
                              aprmattaś cainam avaghaṭṭayan vipacet | sa yathā nātisāndro nātidravaś
                              ca bhavati tathā prayateta | athainam āgatapākam avatāryānuguptam
                              āyase kumbhe saṃvṛtamukhe nidadhyād eṣa madhyamaḥ || </l>

                         <l xml:id="SS.1.11.12"><label>1931 ed. 1.11.12</label> eṣa evāpratīvāpaḥ
                              pakvaḥ saṃvyūhimo sṛduḥ || </l>

                         <l xml:id="SS.1.11.13"><label>1931 ed. 1.11.13</label> pratīvāpe

                              pakvaḥ pākyastīkṣṇaḥ || </l>

                         <l xml:id="SS.1.12.1"><label>1931 ed. 1.12.1</label> athāto 'gnikarmavidhim
                              adhyāyaṃ vyākhyāsyāmaḥ || </l>

                         <l xml:id="SS.1.12.2"><label>1931 ed. 1.12.2</label> yathovāca bhagavān
                              dhanvantariḥ || </l>

                         <l xml:id="SS.1.12.3"><label>1931 ed. 1.12.3</label> kṣārādagnirgarīyān
                              kriyāsu vyākhyātaḥ taddagdhānāṃ
                              rogāṇāmapunarbhāvādbheṣajaśastrakṣārair asādhyānāṃ satsādhyatvāc ca || </l>

                         <l xml:id="SS.1.12.4"><label>1931 ed. 1.12.4</label> athemāni
                              dahanopakaraṇāni tad yathā
                              pippalyajāśakṛdgodantaśaraśalākājāmbavauṣṭhetaralauhāḥ
                              kṣaudraguḍasnehāś ca | tatra
                              pippalyajāśakṛdgodantaśaraśalākāstvaggatānāṃ jāmbavauṣṭhetaralauhā
                              māṃsagatānāṃ kṣaudraguḍasnehāḥ sirāsnāyusandhyasthigatānām || </l>

                         <l xml:id="SS.1.12.5"><label>1931 ed. 1.12.5</label> tatrāgnikarma
                              sarvartuṣu kuryād anyatra śaradgrīṣmābhyāṃ tatrāpyātyayike
                              'gnikarmasādhye vyādhau tatpratyanīkaṃ vidhiṃ kṛtvā || </l>

                         <l xml:id="SS.1.12.6"><label>1931 ed. 1.12.6</label> sarvavyādhiṣvṛtuṣu ca
                              picchilamannaṃ bhuktavataḥ (? karma kurvīta)
                              aśmarībhagandarārśomukharogeṣv abhuktavataḥ || </l>

                         <l xml:id="SS.1.12.7"><label>1931 ed. 1.12.7</label> tatra
                              dvividhamagnikarmāhureke tvagdagdhaṃ māṃsadagdhaṃ ca iha tu
                              sirāsnāyusandhyasthiṣv api va pratiṣiddho 'gniḥ || </l>

                         <l xml:id="SS.1.12.8"><label>1931 ed. 1.12.8</label> tatra śabdaprādurbhāvo
                              durgandhatā tvaksaṃkocaś ca tvagdagdhe kapotavarṇatā'lpaśvayathuvedanā
                              śuṣkasaṃkucitavraṇatā ca māṃsadagdhe kṛṣṇonnatavraṇatā
                              srāvasannirodhaś ca sirāsnāyudagdhe rūkṣāruṇatā karkaśasthiravraṇatā
                              ca sandhyasthidagdhe || </l>

                         <l xml:id="SS.1.12.9"><label>1931 ed. 1.12.9</label> tatra
                              śirorogādhimanthayor bhrūlalāṭaśaṅkhapradeśeṣu dahet
                              vartmarogeṣvārdrālaktakapraticchannāṃ dṛṣṭiṃ kṛvā vartmaromakūpān (?
                              dahet ) || </l>

                         <l xml:id="SS.1.12.10"><label>1931 ed. 1.12.10</label>
                              tvaṅnāṃsasirāsnāyusandhyasthisthite 'tyugraruji
                              vāyāvucchritakaṭhinasupramāṃse vraṇe granthyarśo
                              'rbudabhagandarāpacīślīpadacarmakīlatilakālakāntravṛddhisandhisirācchedanādiṣu
                              nāḍīśoṇitātipravṛttiṣu cāgnikarma kuryāt || </l>

                         <l xml:id="SS.1.12.11"><label>1931 ed. 1.12.11</label> tatra
                              valaya-bindu-vilekhā-pratisāraṇānīti dahanaviśeṣāḥ || </l>

                         <l xml:id="SS.1.12.12"><label>1931 ed. 1.12.12</label> bhavati cātra | </l>

                         <l xml:id="SS.1.12.12ab"><label>1931 ed. 1.12.12ab</label> rogasya
                              saṃsthānamavekṣya samyaṅgarasya marmāṇi balābalaṃ ca | </l>

                         <l xml:id="SS.1.12.12cd"><label>1931 ed. 1.12.12cd</label> vyādhiṃ
                              tathartuṃ ca samīkṣya samyak tato vyavasyed bhiṣagagnikarma || </l>

                         <l xml:id="SS.1.12.13"><label>1931 ed. 1.12.13</label> tatra samyagdagdhe
                              madhusarpirbhyāmabhyaṅgaḥ || </l>

                         <l xml:id="SS.1.12.14"><label>1931 ed. 1.12.14</label> athemānagninā

                              durbalaṃ bālaṃ vṛddhaṃ bhīrumanekavraṇapīḍitamasvedyāṃś ceti || </l>

                         <l xml:id="SS.1.12.15"><label>1931 ed. 1.12.15</label> ata
                              ūrdhvamitarathādagdhalakṣaṇaṃ vakṣyāmaḥ | tatra snigdhaṃ rūkṣaṃ
                              va+āśritya dravyam agnir dahati agnisaṃtapto hi snehaḥ
                              sūkṣmasirānusāritvāt tvagādīn anupraviśyāśu dahati tasmāt snehadagdhe
                              'dhikā rujo bhavanti || </l>

                         <l xml:id="SS.1.12.16"><label>1931 ed. 1.12.16</label> tatra pluṣṭaṃ
                              durdagdhaṃ samyagdagdhamatidagdhaṃ ceti caturvidhamagnidagdham | tatra
                              yadvivarṇaṃ pluṣyate 'timātraṃ tat pluṣṭaṃ yatrottiṣṭhanti
                              sphoṭāstīvrāś coṣadāharāgapākavedanāś cirāccopaśāmyanti taddrudagdhaṃ
                              samyagdgdhamanavagāḍhaṃ tālaphalavarṇaṃ susaṃsthitaṃ
                              pūrvalakṣaṇayuktaṃ ca atidagdhe māṃsāvalambanaṃ gātraviśleṣaḥ
                              sirāsnāyusandhyasthivyāpādanamatimātraṃ jvaradāhapipāsāmūrcchāś
                              copadravā bhavanti vraṇaś cāsya cireṇa rohati rūḍhaś ca vivarṇo
                              bhavati |
                              tadetaccaturvidhamagnidagdhalakṣaṇamātmakarmaprasādhakaṃ(ā.naṃ)bhavati
                              || </l>

                         <l xml:id="SS.1.12.17ab"><label>1931 ed. 1.12.17ab</label> agninā kopitaṃ

                         <l xml:id="SS.1.12.19ab"><label>1931 ed. 1.12.19ab</label> sphoṭāḥ śīghraṃ
                              prajāyante jvarastṛṣṇā ca vardhate || </l>

                         <l xml:id="SS.1.12.19cd"><label>1931 ed. 1.12.19cd</label>
                              dagdhasyopaśamārthāya cikitsā saṃpravakṣyate || </l>

                         <l xml:id="SS.1.12.20ab"><label>1931 ed. 1.12.20ab</label>
                              pluṣṭasyāgnipratapanaṃ kāryamuṣṇaṃ tathauṣadham | </l>

                         <l xml:id="SS.1.12.20cd"><label>1931 ed. 1.12.20cd</label> śarīre
                              svinnabhūyiṣṭhe svinnaṃ bhavati śoṇitam || </l>

                         <l xml:id="SS.1.12.21ab"><label>1931 ed. 1.12.21ab</label> prakṛtyā
                              hyudakaṃ śītaṃ skandayatyatiśoṇitam | </l>

                         <l xml:id="SS.1.12.21cd"><label>1931 ed. 1.12.21cd</label> tasmāt sukhayati
                              hyuṣṇaṃ natu śītaṃ kathaṃcana || </l>

                         <l xml:id="SS.1.12.22ab"><label>1931 ed. 1.12.22ab</label> śītāmuṣṇāṃ ca
                              durdagdhe kriyāṃ kuryād bhiṣak punaḥ | </l>

                         <l xml:id="SS.1.12.22cd"><label>1931 ed. 1.12.22cd</label>

                         <l xml:id="SS.1.12.24ab"><label>1931 ed. 1.12.24ab</label>

                         <l xml:id="SS.1.12.25ab"><label>1931 ed. 1.12.25ab</label> atidagdhe

                         <l xml:id="SS.1.12.25cd"><label>1931 ed. 1.12.25cd</label> kriyāṃ kuryād
                              bhiṣak paś cācchālitaṇḍulakaṇḍanaiḥ || </l>

                         <l xml:id="SS.1.12.26ab"><label>1931 ed. 1.12.26ab</label>
                              tindukītvakkapālair vā ghṛtamiśraiḥ pralepayet | </l>

                         <l xml:id="SS.1.12.26cd"><label>1931 ed. 1.12.26cd</label> vraṇaṃ
                              guḍūcīpatrair vā chādayed athavaudakaiḥ || </l>

                         <l xml:id="SS.1.12.27ab"><label>1931 ed. 1.12.27ab</label> kriyāṃ ca
                              nikhilāṃ kuryād bhiṣak pittavisarpavat | </l>

                         <l xml:id="SS.1.12.27cd"><label>1931 ed. 1.12.27cd</label> madhūcchiṣṭaṃ
                              samadhukaṃ rodhraṃ sarjarasaṃ tathā || </l>

                         <l xml:id="SS.1.12.28ab"><label>1931 ed. 1.12.28ab</label> mañjiṣṭhāṃ

                         <l xml:id="SS.1.12.28cd"><label>1931 ed. 1.12.28cd</label>

                         <l xml:id="SS.1.12.29ab"><label>1931 ed. 1.12.29ab</label> snehadagdhe
                              kriyāṃ rūkṣāṃ viśeṣeṇāvacārayet | </l>

                         <l xml:id="SS.1.12.29cd"><label>1931 ed. 1.12.29cd</label> ata ūrdhvaṃ
                              pravakṣyāmi dhūmopahatalakṣaṇam || </l>

                         <l xml:id="SS.1.12.30ab"><label>1931 ed. 1.12.30ab</label> śvasiti kṣauti
                              cātyarthamatyādhamati kāsate | </l>

                         <l xml:id="SS.1.12.30cd"><label>1931 ed. 1.12.30cd</label> cakṣuṣoḥ
                              paridāhaś ca rāgaś caivopajāyate || </l>

                         <l xml:id="SS.1.12.31ab"><label>1931 ed. 1.12.31ab</label> sadhūmakaṃ
                              niśvasiti ghreyamanyanna vetti ca | </l>

                         <l xml:id="SS.1.12.31cd"><label>1931 ed. 1.12.31cd</label> tathaiva ca

                         <l xml:id="SS.1.12.32ab"><label>1931 ed. 1.12.32ab</label>
                              tṛṣṇādāhajvarayutaḥ sīdatyatha ca mūrcchati | </l>

                         <l xml:id="SS.1.12.32cd"><label>1931 ed. 1.12.32cd</label> dhūmopahata ity
                              evaṃ śṛṇu tasya cikitsitam || </l>

                         <l xml:id="SS.1.12.33ab"><label>1931 ed. 1.12.33ab</label> sarpirikṣurasaṃ
                              drākṣāṃ payo vā śarkarāmbu vā | </l>

                         <l xml:id="SS.1.12.33cd"><label>1931 ed. 1.12.33cd</label> madhurāmlau
                              rasau vā'pi vamanāya pradāpayet || </l>

                         <l xml:id="SS.1.12.34ab"><label>1931 ed. 1.12.34ab</label> vamataḥ

                         <l xml:id="SS.1.12.34cd"><label>1931 ed. 1.12.34cd</label> vidhinā'nena
                              śāmyanti sadanakṣavathujvarāḥ || </l>

                         <l xml:id="SS.1.12.35ab"><label>1931 ed. 1.12.35ab</label>
                              dāhamūrcchātṛḍādhmānaśvāsakāsāś ca dāruṇāḥ | </l>

                         <l xml:id="SS.1.12.35cd"><label>1931 ed. 1.12.35cd</label> madhurair
                              lavaṇāmlaiś ca kaṭukaiḥ kavalagrahaiḥ || </l>

                         <l xml:id="SS.1.12.36ab"><label>1931 ed. 1.12.36ab</label>
                              samyaggṛhṇātīndriyārthān manaś cāsya prasīdati | </l>

                         <l xml:id="SS.1.12.36cd"><label>1931 ed. 1.12.36cd</label> śirovirecanaṃ
                              cāsmai dadyādyogena śāstravit || </l>

                         <l xml:id="SS.1.12.37ab"><label>1931 ed. 1.12.37ab</label> dṛṣṭirviśudhyate
                              cāsya śirogrīvaṃ ca dehinaḥ | </l>

                         <l xml:id="SS.1.12.37cd"><label>1931 ed. 1.12.37cd</label> avidāhi laghu
                              snigdhamāhāraṃ cāsya kalpayet || </l>

                         <l xml:id="SS.1.12.38ab"><label>1931 ed. 1.12.38ab</label> uṣṇavātātapair
                              dagdhe śītaḥ kāryo vidhiḥ sadā | </l>

                         <l xml:id="SS.1.12.38cd"><label>1931 ed. 1.12.38cd</label> śītavarṣānilair
                              dagdhe snigdhamuṣṇaṃ ca śasyate || </l>

                              dagdhe siddhirnāsti kathaṃcan | </l>

                         <l xml:id="SS.1.12.39cd"><label>1931 ed. 1.12.39cd</label>
                              indravajrāgnidaghe 'pi jīvati pratikārayet || </l>

                              dvādaśo 'dhyāyaḥ || </p>
