                    <div n="13" type="adhyāya">

                         <head>trayodaśo 'dhyāyaḥ |</head>

                         <note>The vulgate text is here transcribed from the 1938 edition, not the
                              1931 edition.</note>

                         <l xml:id="SS.1.13.1"><label>1938 ed. 1.13.1</label> athāto
                              jalaukāvacāraṇīyam adhyāyaṃ vyākhyāsyāmaḥ || </l>

                         <l xml:id="SS.1.13.2"><label>1938 ed. 1.13.2</label> yathovāca bhagavān
                              dhanvantariḥ || </l>

                         <l xml:id="SS.1.13.3"><label>1938 ed. 1.13.3</label> nṛpāḍhya<pc
                                   > </pc>bāla<pc> </pc>sthavira<pc> </pc>bhīru<pc
                                   > </pc>durbala<pc> </pc>nārī<pc> </pc>sukumārāṇām anugrahārthaṃ
                              paramasukumāro 'yaṃ śoṇitāvasecanopāyo 'bhihito jalaukasaḥ || </l>

                         <l xml:id="SS.1.13.4"><label>1938 ed. 1.13.4</label> tatra
                              vātapittakaphaduṣṭaśoṇitaṃ yathāsaṃkhyaṃ śṛṅgajalaukālābubhir
                              avasecayet sarvāṇi sarvair vā (viśeṣas tu visrāvyaṃ
                              śṛṅgajalaukālābubhir gṛhṇīyāt) || </l>


                         <l xml:id="SS.1.13.5"><label>1938 ed. 1.13.5ab</label> bhavanti cātra
                              ślokāḥ |
                              <caesura/>
                               uṣṇaṃ samadhuraṃ snigdhaṃ gavāṃ śṛṅgaṃ prakīrtitam |
                              <caesura/>
                               tasmād vātopasṛṣṭe tu hitaṃ tad avasecane || </l>



                         <l xml:id="SS.1.13.6"><label>1938 ed. 1.13.6</label> śītādhivāsā madhurā
                              jalaukā vārisaṃbhavā |
                              <caesura/>
                               tasmāt pittopasṛṣṭe tu hitā sā tv avasecane || </l>

                         <l xml:id="SS.1.13.7"><label>1938 ed. 1.13.7</label> alābu kaṭukaṃ rūkṣaṃ
                              tīkṣṇaṃ ca parikīrtitam |
                              <caesura/>
                               tasmāc chleṣmopasṛṣṭe tu hitaṃ tad avasecane || </l>

                         <l xml:id="SS.1.13.8"><label>1938 ed. 1.13.8</label> tatra pracchite
                                   tanu<pc> </pc>basti<pc> </pc>paṭalāvanaddhena śṛṅgeṇa śoṇitam
                              avasecayed ācūṣaṇāt sāntardīpayā 'lābvā | (jalāyukā vakṣyante) || </l>

                         <l xml:id="SS.1.13.9"><label>1938 ed. 1.13.9</label> jalam āsām āyur iti
                              jalāyukāḥ jalam āsām oka iti jalaukasaḥ || </l>

                         <l xml:id="SS.1.13.10"><label>1938 ed. 1.13.10</label> tā dvādaśa tāsāṃ
                              saviṣāḥ ṣaṭ tāvatya eva nirviṣāḥ || </l>

                         <l xml:id="SS.1.13.11"><label>1938 ed. 1.13.11</label> tatra saviṣāḥ kṛṣṇā
                              karburā alagardā indrāyudhā sāmudrikā gocandanā ceti | tāsu
                              añjanacūrṇavarṇā pṛthuśirāḥ kṛṣṇā varmimatsyavad āyatā
                              chinnonnatakukṣiḥ karburā romaśā mahāpārśvā kṛṣṇamukhī alagardā
                              indrāyudhavad ūrdhvarājibhiś citritā indrāyudhā īṣadasitapītikā
                              vicitrapuṣpākṛticitrā sāmudrikāḥ govṛṣaṇavad adhobhāge
                              dvidhābhūtākṛtir aṇumukhī gocandaneti | tābhir daṣṭe puruṣe daṃśe
                              śvayathur atimātraṃ kaṇḍūrmūrcchā jvaro dāhaś chardir madaḥ sadanam
                              iti liṅgāni bhavanti | tatra mahāgadaḥ pānālepananasya
                              karmādiṣūpayojyaḥ | indrāyudhādaṣṭam asādhyam | ity etāḥ saviṣāḥ
                              sacikitsitā vyākhyātāḥ || </l>

                         <l xml:id="SS.1.13.12"><label>1938 ed. 1.13.12</label> atha nirviṣāḥ kapilā
                              piṅgalā śaṅkumukhī mūṣikā puṇḍarīkamukhī sāvarikā ceti | tatra
                              manaḥśilārañjitābhyām iva pārśvābhyāṃ pṛṣṭhe snigdhā mudgavarṇā kapilā
                              kiṃcidraktā vṛttakāyā piṅgalā ''śugā ca piṅgalā yakṛdvarṇā
                              śīghrapāyinī dīrghatīkṣṇamukhī śaṅkumukhīḥ mūṣikākṛtivarṇā
                              'niṣṭagandhā ca mūṣikā mudgavarṇā puṇḍarīkatulyavaktrā puṇḍarīkamukhī
                              snigdhā padmapatravarṇā 'ṣṭādaśāṅgulapramāṇā sāvarikā sā ca paśvarthe
                              ity etā aviṣā vyākhyātāḥ || </l>

                         <l xml:id="SS.1.13.13"><label>1938 ed. 1.13.13</label> tāsāṃ
                                   yavanapāṇḍyasahya<pc> </pc>pautanādīni kṣetrāṇi teṣu mahāśarīrā
                              balavatyaḥ śīghrapāyinyo mahāśanā nirviṣāś ca viśeṣeṇa bhavanti |</l>

                         <l xml:id="SS.1.13.14"><label>1938 ed. 1.13.14</label> tatra
                              saviṣamatsyakīṭadarduramūtrapurīṣakothajātāḥ kaluṣeṣv ambhaḥsu ca
                              saviṣāḥ
                              padmotpalanalinakumudasaugandhikakuvalayapuṇḍarīkaśaivalakothajātā
                              vimaleṣv ambhaḥsu ca nirviṣāḥ || </l>

                         <l xml:id="SS.1.13.15"><label>1938 ed. 1.13.15</label> bhavati cātra |
                              <caesura/>
                               kṣetreṣu vicaranty etāḥ salilāḍhyasugandhiṣu |
                              <caesura/>
                               na ca saṃkīrṇacāriṇyo na ca paṅkeśayāḥ sukhāḥ || </l>

                         <l xml:id="SS.1.13.16"><label>1938 ed. 1.13.16</label> tāsāṃ grahaṇam
                              ārdracarmaṇā, anyair vā prayogair gṛhṇīyāt || </l>

                         <l xml:id="SS.1.13.17"><label>1938 ed. 1.13.17</label> athaināṃ nave mahati
                              ghaṭe sarastaḍāgodakapaṅkam āvāpya nidadhyāt bhakṣyārthe cāsām
                              upaharec chaivalaṃ vallūram audakāṃś ca kandāṃś cūrṇīkṛtya śayyārthaṃ
                              tṛṇam audakāni ca patrāṇi tryahāt tryahāc cābhyo 'nyaj jalaṃ bhakṣyaṃ
                              ca dadyāt saptarātrāt saptarātrāc ca ghaṭam anyaṃ saṃkrāmayet || </l>

                         <l xml:id="SS.1.13.18"><label>1938 ed. 1.13.18</label> bhavati cātra |
                              <caesura/>
                               sthūlamadhyāḥ parikliṣṭāḥ pṛthvyo mandaviceṣṭitāḥ |
                              <caesura/>
                               agrāhiṇyo 'lpapāyinyaḥ saviṣāś ca na pūjitāḥ || </l>

                         <l xml:id="SS.1.13.19"><label>1938 ed. 1.13.19</label> atha jalauko
                              'vasekasādhyavyādhitam upaveśya saṃveśya vā virūkṣya cāsya tam
                              avakāśaṃ mṛdgomayacūrṇair yady arujaḥ syāt | gṛhītāś ca tāḥ
                                   sarṣaparajanī<pc> </pc>kalkodaka<pc> </pc>pradigdha<pc
                              > </pc>gātrīḥ salilasarakamadhye muhūrtasthitā vigataklamā jñātvā
                              tābhī rogaṃ grāhayet | ślakṣṇaśuklārdrapicuprotāvacchannāṃ kṛtvā
                              mukham apāvṛṇuyāt agṛhṇantyai kṣīrabinduṃ śoṇitabinduṃ vā dadyāt,
                              śastrapadāni vā kurvīta yady evam api na gṛhṇīyāt tadā'nyāṃ grāhayet
                              || </l>

                         <l xml:id="SS.1.13.20"><label>1938 ed. 1.13.20</label> yadā ca niviśate
                              'śvakhuravad ānanaṃ kṛtvonnamya ca skandhaṃ tadā jānīyād gṛhṇātīti
                              gṛhṇantīṃ cārdravastrāvacchannāṃ kṛtvā dhārayet || </l>

                         <l xml:id="SS.1.13.21"><label>1938 ed. 1.13.21</label> daṃśe toda<pc
                                   > </pc>kaṇḍu<pc> </pc>prādur<pc> </pc>bhāvair jānīyāc chuddham
                              iyam ādatta iti śuddham ādadānām apanayet atha śoṇitagandhena na
                              muñcen mukham asyāḥ saindhavacūrṇenāvakiret || </l>

                         <l xml:id="SS.1.13.22"><label>1938 ed. 1.13.22</label> atha patitāṃ
                                   taṇḍula<pc> </pc>kaṇḍana<pc> </pc>pradigdhagātrīṃ
                              tailalavaṇābhyaktamukhīṃ vāmahastāṅguṣṭhāṅgulībhyāṃ gṛhītapucchāṃ
                              dakṣiṇahastāṅguṣṭhāṅgulibhyāṃ śanaiḥ śanair anulomam anumārjayed ā
                              mukhāt vāmayet tāvad yāvat samyagvāntaliṅgānīti | samyagvāntā
                                   salilasarake<pc> </pc>nyastā bhoktukāmā satī caret | yā sīdatī na
                              ceṣṭate sā durvāntā tāṃ punaḥ samyag vāmayet | durvāntāyā vyādhir
                              asādhya indramado nāma bhavati | 
                              atha suvāntāṃ pūrvavat sannidadhyāt || </l>


                         <l xml:id="SS.1.13.23"><label>1938 ed. 1.13.23</label> śoṇitasya yogāyogān
                              avekṣya śatadhautaghṛtābhyaṅgas tat picudhāraṇaṃ vāi jalaukovraṇān
                              madhunā'vaghaṭṭayet śitābhir adbhiś pariṣecayed badhnīta vā
                              kaṣāyamadhurasnigdhaśītaiś ca pradehaiḥ pradihyād iti || </l>

                         <l xml:id="SS.1.13.23x"/>

                         <l xml:id="SS.1.13.24"><label>1938 ed. 1.13.24</label> bhavati cātra |
                              kṣetrāṇi grahaṇaṃ jātīḥ poṣaṇaṃ sāvacāraṇam |
                              <caesura/>
                               jalaukasāṃ ca yo vetti tat sādhyān sa jayed gadān || </l>

                         <p ana="trailer">iti suśrutasaṃhitāyāṃ sūtrasthāne jalaukāvacāraṇīyo nāma
                              trayodaśo 'dhyāyaḥ || </p>
                    </div>

                    <div n="14" type="adhyāya">
                         <head>caturdaśo 'dhyāyaḥ |</head>

                         <l xml:id="SS.1.14.1"><label>1931 ed. 1.14.1</label> athātaḥ
                              śoṇitavarṇanīyam adhyāyaṃ vyākhyāsyāmaḥ || </l>

                         <l xml:id="SS.1.14.2"><label>1931 ed. 1.14.2</label> yathovāca bhagavān
                              dhanvantariḥ || </l>

                         <l xml:id="SS.1.14.3"><label>1931 ed. 1.14.3</label> tatra pāñcabhautikasya
                              caturvidhasya ṣaḍrasasya dvividhavīryasyāṣṭavidhāvīryasya
                              vā'nekaguṇasyopayuktasyāhārasya samyakpariṇatasya yas tejobhūtaḥ sāraḥ
                              paramasūkṣmaḥ sa rasa ity ucyate tasya ca hṛdayaṃ sthānaṃ sa hṛdayāc
                              caturviṃśati dhamanīr anupraviśyor dhvagā daśa daśa cādhogāminyaś
                              catasraś ca tiryaggāḥ kṛtsnaṃ śarīram aharahas tarpayati vardhayati
                              dhārayati yāpayati cādṛṣṭahetukena karmaṇā | tasya śarīram anusarato
                              'numānād gatir upalakṣayitavyā kṣayavṛddhivaikṛtaiḥ | tasmin
                              sarvaśarīrāvayavadoṣadhātumalāśayānusāriṇi rase jijñāsā kim ayaṃ
                              saumyas taijasa iti | atrocyate sa khalu dravānusārī
                              snehanajīvanatarpaṇadhāraṇādibhir viśeṣaiḥ saumya ity avagamyate || </l>

                         <l xml:id="SS.1.14.4"><label>1931 ed. 1.14.4</label> sa khalv āpyo raso
                              yakṛtplīhānau prāpya rāgam upaiti || </l>

                         <l xml:id="SS.1.14.5"><label>1931 ed. 1.14.5</label> bhavataś cātra |
                              <caesura/>
                               rañjitās tejasā tv āpaḥ śarīrasthena dehinām |
                              <caesura/>
                               avyāpannāḥ prasannena raktam ity abhidhīyate || </l>

                         <l xml:id="SS.1.14.6"><label>1931 ed. 1.14.6</label> rasād eva striyā
                              raktaṃ rajaḥsaṃjñaṃ pravartate | tad varṣād dvyādaśād ūrdhvaṃ yāti
                              pañcāśataḥ kṣayam || </l>

                         <l xml:id="SS.1.14.7"><label>1931 ed. 1.14.7</label> ārtavaṃ śoṇitaṃ tv
                              āgneyaṃ agnīṣomīyatvād garbhasya || </l>

                         <l xml:id="SS.1.14.8"><label>1931 ed. 1.14.8</label> pāñcabhautikaṃ tv
                              apare jīvaraktam āhur ācāryāḥ || </l>

                         <l xml:id="SS.1.14.9"><label>1931 ed. 1.14.9</label> vesratā dravatā rāgaḥ
                              spandanaṃ laghutā tathā |
                              <caesura/>
                               bhūmyādīnāṃ guṇā hyete dṛśyante cātra śoṇite || </l>

                         <l xml:id="SS.1.14.10"><label>1931 ed. 1.14.10</label> rasād raktaṃ tato
                              māṃsaṃ māṃsān medaḥ prajāyate |
                              <caesura/>

                         <l xml:id="SS.1.15.5"><label>1931 ed. 1.15.5</label> rasas tuṣṭiṃ prīṇanaṃ

                              niṣprabhatvaṃ(ā.tā) ca śleṣmakṣaye rūkṣatā'ntardāha

                         <l xml:id="SS.1.15.11"><label>1931 ed. 1.15.11</label> rasakṣaye

                                   sphiggaṇḍauṣṭhopasthoruvakṣaḥ<pc
                              > </pc>kakṣāpiṇḍikodaragrīvāśuṣkatā raukṣyatodau gātrāṇāṃ sadanaṃ

                         <l xml:id="SS.1.15.13"><label>1931 ed. 1.15.13</label> purīṣakṣaye
                              hṛdayapārśvapīḍā saśabdasya ca vāyor ūrdhvagamanaṃ kukṣau saṃcaraṇaṃ
                              ca mūtrakṣaye bastitodo 'lpamūtratā ca atrāpi svayonivardhanadravyāṇi

                         <l xml:id="SS.1.15.14"><label>1931 ed. 1.15.14</label> ārtavakṣaye
                              yathocitakālādarśanamalpatā vā yonivedanā ca tatra

                              stnayor mlānatā stanyāsaṃbhavo 'lpatā vā tatra

                         <l xml:id="SS.1.15.15"><label>1931 ed. 1.15.15</label> ata ūrdhvam

                              svayonivardhanātyupasevanād bhavati | tatra vātavṛddhau vākpāruṣyaṃ

                         <l xml:id="SS.1.15.16"><label>1931 ed. 1.15.16</label> raso 'tivṛddho

                              ca māṃsaṃ sphiggaṇḍauṣṭhopasthorubāhujaṅghāsu vṛddhiṃ gurugātratāṃ ca

                         <l xml:id="SS.1.15.17"><label>1931 ed. 1.15.17</label> purīṣamāṭopaṃ kukṣau
                              śūlaṃ ca mūtraṃ mūtravṛddhiṃ muhurmuhuḥ pravṛttiṃ bastitodamādhmānaṃ
                              ca svedastvaco daugandhyaṃ kaṇḍūṃ ca || </l>

                         <l xml:id="SS.1.15.18"><label>1931 ed. 1.15.18</label> ārtavam aṅgamardam
                              atipravṛttiṃ daurgandhyaṃ ca stanyaṃ stanayor āpīnatvaṃ muhur muhuḥ
                              pravṛttiṃ todaṃ ca garbho jaṭharābhivṛddhiṃ svedaṃ ca || </l>

                         <l xml:id="SS.1.15.19"><label>1931 ed. 1.15.19</label> teṣāṃ yathāsvaṃ
                              saṃśodhanaṃ kṣapaṇaṃ ca kṣayād aviruddhaiḥ kriyāviśeṣaiḥ prakurvīt || </l>

                         <l xml:id="SS.1.15.20ab"><label>1931 ed. 1.15.20ab</label> pūrvaḥ pūrvo
                              'tivṛddhatvād vardhayed dhi paraṃ param | </l>

                         <l xml:id="SS.1.15.20cd"><label>1931 ed. 1.15.20cd</label> tasam
                              ātipravṛddhānāṃ dhātūnāṃ hrāsanaṃ hitam || </l>

                         <l xml:id="SS.1.15.21"><label>1931 ed. 1.15.21</label> balalakṣaṇaṃ
                              balakṣayalakṣaṇaṃ cāta ūrdhvam upadekṣyāmaḥ | tatra rasādīnāṃ
                              śukrāntānāṃ dhātūnāṃ yatparaṃ tejastat khalvojastad eva balam ity
                              ucyate svaśāstrasiddhāntāt || </l>

                         <l xml:id="SS.1.15.22"><label>1931 ed. 1.15.22</label> tatra balena
                              sthiropacitamāṃsatā sarvaceṣṭāsvapratighātaḥ svaravarṇaprasādo
                              bāhyānām ābhyantarāṇāṃ ca karaṇānām ātmakāryapratipattir bhavati || </l>

                         <l xml:id="SS.1.15.23"><label>1931 ed. 1.15.23</label> bhavanti cātra | </l>

                         <l xml:id="SS.1.15.23ab"><label>1931 ed. 1.15.23ab</label> ojaḥ somātmakaṃ
                              snigdhaṃ śuklaṃ śītaṃ sthiraṃ saram | </l>

                         <l xml:id="SS.1.15.23cd"><label>1931 ed. 1.15.23cd</label> viviktaṃ mṛdu
                              mṛtsnaṃ ca prāṇāyatanamutttamam || </l>

                         <l xml:id="SS.1.15.24ab"><label>1931 ed. 1.15.24ab</label> dehaḥ sāvayavas
                              tena vyāpto bhavati dehinām | </l>

                         <l xml:id="SS.1.15.24cd"><label>1931 ed. 1.15.24cd</label> tadabhāvāc ca
                              śīryante śarīrāṇi śarīriṇām || </l>

                         <l xml:id="SS.1.15.25"><label>1931 ed. 1.15.25</label> abhighātāt kṣayāt
                              kopāc chokādd hyānāc chramāt kṣudhaḥ | </l>

                         <l xml:id="SS.1.15.25ab"><label>1931 ed. 1.15.25ab</label> ojaḥ saṃkṣīyate
                              hy ebhyo dhātugrahaṇaniḥsṛtam | </l>

                         <l xml:id="SS.1.15.25cd"><label>1931 ed. 1.15.25cd</label> tejaḥ samīritaṃ
                              tasmād visraṃsayate dehinaḥ || </l>

                         <l xml:id="SS.1.15.26-27"><label>1931 ed. 1.15.26-27</label> tasya visraṃso
                              vyāpat kṣaya iti liṅgāni vyāpannasya bhavanti sandhiviśleṣo gātrāṇāṃ
                              sadanaṃ doṣacyavanaṃ kriyā'(O.kriyā)sannirodhaś ca visraṃse
                              stabdhagurugātratā vātaśopho varṇabhedo glānistandrā nidrā ca vyāpanne
                              mūrcchā māṃsakṣayo mohaḥ pralāpo maraṇam iti ca kṣaye || </l>

                         <l xml:id="SS.1.15.28"><label>1931 ed. 1.15.28</label> bhavanti cātra | </l>

                         <l xml:id="SS.1.15.28ab"><label>1931 ed. 1.15.28ab</label> trayo doṣā
                              balasyoktā vyāpadvisraṃsanakṣayāḥ | </l>

                         <l xml:id="SS.1.15.28cd"><label>1931 ed. 1.15.28cd</label> viśleṣasādau
                              gātrāṇāṃ doṣavisraṃsanaṃ śramaḥ | </l>

                         <l xml:id="SS.1.15.28ef"><label>1931 ed. 1.15.28ef</label> aprācuryaṃ
                              kriyānāṃ ca balavisraṃsalakṣaṇam || </l>

                         <l xml:id="SS.1.15.29ab"><label>1931 ed. 1.15.29ab</label> gurutvaṃ
                              stabdhatā'ṇgeṣu glānirvarṇasya bhedanam | </l>

                         <l xml:id="SS.1.15.29cd"><label>1931 ed. 1.15.29cd</label> tandrā nidrā
                              vātaśopho balavyāpadi lakṣaṇam || </l>

                         <l xml:id="SS.1.15.30ab"><label>1931 ed. 1.15.30ab</label> mūrcchā
                              māṃsakṣāyo mohaḥ pralāpo 'jñānam eva ca | </l>

                         <l xml:id="SS.1.15.30cd"><label>1931 ed. 1.15.30cd</label> pūrvoktāni ca
                              liṅgāni maraṇaṃ ca balakṣaye || </l>

                         <l xml:id="SS.1.15.31"><label>1931 ed. 1.15.31</label> tatra visraṃse
                              vyāpanne ca kriyāviśeṣair aviruddhair balamāpyāyayet itaraṃ tu
                              mūḍhasaṃjñaṃ varjayet || </l>

                         <l xml:id="SS.1.15.32ab"><label>1931 ed. 1.15.32ab</label>
                              doṣadhātumalakṣīṇo balakṣīṇi'pi vā naraḥ | </l>

                         <l xml:id="SS.1.15.32cd"><label>1931 ed. 1.15.32cd</label> svayonivardhanaṃ
                              yattadannapānaṃ prakāṅkṣati || </l>

                         <l xml:id="SS.1.15.33ab"><label>1931 ed. 1.15.33ab</label> yadyadāhārajātaṃ
                              tu kṣīṇaḥ prārthayate naraḥ | </l>

                         <l xml:id="SS.1.15.33cd"><label>1931 ed. 1.15.33cd</label> tasya tasya sa
                              lābhe tu taṃ taṃ kṣayamapohati || </l>

                         <l xml:id="SS.1.15.34ab"><label>1931 ed. 1.15.34ab</label> yasya
                              dhātukṣayādvāyuḥ saṃjñāṃ karma ca nāśayet | </l>

                         <l xml:id="SS.1.15.34cd"><label>1931 ed. 1.15.34cd</label> prakṣiṇaṃ ca
                              balaṃ yasya nāsu śakyaś cikitsitum || </l>

                         <l xml:id="SS.1.15.35"><label>1931 ed. 1.15.35</label> rasanimittam eva
                              sthaulyaṃ kārśyaṃ ca | tatra śleṣmalāhārasevino
                              'dhyaśanaśīlasyāvyāyāmino divāsvapnaratasya cāma evānnaraso
                              madhurataraś ca śarīramanukrāmannatisnehānmedo janayati
                              tadatisthaulyamāpādayati tamatisthūlaṃ
                              kṣudraśvāsapipāsākṣutsvapnasvedagātradaurgandhyakrathanagātrasādagadgadatvāni
                              kṣipramevāviśanti saukumāryānmedasaḥ sarvakriyāsvasamarthaḥ
                              kaphamedoniruddhamārgartvāccālpavyavāyo bhavati āvṛtamārgatvād eva
                              śeṣā dhātavo nāpyāyante 'tyarthamato 'lpaprāṇo bhavati
                              pramehapīḍakājvarabhagandaravidradhivātavikārāṇāmanyataṃ prāpya
                              pañcatvam upayāti sarva eva cāsya rogā balavanto
                              bhavantyāvṛtamārgatvāt srotasāṃ atas tasyotpattihetuṃ pariharet |
                              utpanne tu
                              śilājatuguggulugomūtratriphalāloharajorasāñjanamadhuyavamudgakoradūṣakaśyāmākoddālakādīnāṃ
                              virūkṣaṇacchedanīyānāṃ dravyāṇaṃ vidhivadupayogo vyāyāmo
                              lekhanabastyupayogaś ceti || </l>

                         <l xml:id="SS.1.15.36"><label>1931 ed. 1.15.36</label> tatra punar
                              vātalāhārasevino
                              'tivyāyāmavyavāyādhyayanabhayaśokadhyānarātrijāgaraṇapipāsākṣutkaṣāyālpāśanaprabhṛtibhir
                              upaśoṣito rasadhātuḥ śarīram ananukrāman nalpatvān na prīṇāti tasmād
                              atikārśyaṃ bhavati so 'tikṛśaḥ kṣutpipāsāśītoṣṇavātavarṣabhārādāneṣv
                              asahiṣṇur vātarogaprāyo 'lpaprāṇaś ca kriyāsu bhavati
                              śvāsakāsaśoṣaplīhodarāgnisādagulmaraktapittānām anyatamam āsādya
                              maraṇam upayāti sarva eva cāsya rogā balavanto bhavanty alpaprāṇatvāt
                              atas tasyotpattihetuṃ pariharet | utpanne tu
                              payasyāśvagandhāvidārigandhāśatāvarībalātibalānāgabalānāṃ madhurāṇām
                              anyāsaṃ cauṣadhīnām upayogaḥ
                              kṣīradadhighṛtamāṃsaśāliṣaṣṭikayavagodhūmānāṃ ca
                              divāsvapnabrahmacaryāvyāyāmabṛhaṇabastyupayogaś ceti || </l>

                         <l xml:id="SS.1.15.37"><label>1931 ed. 1.15.37</label> yaḥ punar
                              ubhayasādhāraṇāny āseveta tasyān narasaḥ śarīram anukrāman samān
                              dhātūn upacinoti samadhātutvān madhyaśarīro bhavati sarvakriyāsu
                              samarthaḥ kṣutpipāsāśītoṣṇavarṣātapasaho balavāṃś ca sa satatam
                              anupālayitavya iti || </l>

                         <l xml:id="SS.1.15.38"><label>1931 ed. 1.15.38</label> bhavanti cātra | </l>

                         <l xml:id="SS.1.15.38ab"><label>1931 ed. 1.15.38ab</label> atyantagarhitāv
                              etau sadā sthūlakṛśau narau | </l>

                         <l xml:id="SS.1.15.38cd"><label>1931 ed. 1.15.38cd</label> śreṣṭho
                              madhyaśarīras tu kṛśaḥ sthūlāt tu pūjitaḥ || </l>

                         <l xml:id="SS.1.15.39ab"><label>1931 ed. 1.15.39ab</label> doṣaḥ prakupito
                              dhātūn kṣapayaty ātmatejasā | </l>

                         <l xml:id="SS.1.15.39cd"><label>1931 ed. 1.15.39cd</label> iddhaḥ svatejasā
                              vahnir ukhāgatam ivodakam || </l>

                         <l xml:id="SS.1.15.40ab"><label>1931 ed. 1.15.40ab</label> vailakṣaṇyāc
                              charīrāṇām asthāyitvāt tathaiva ca | </l>

                         <l xml:id="SS.1.15.40cd"><label>1931 ed. 1.15.40cd</label> doṣadhātumalānāṃ
                              tu parimāṇaṃ na vidyate || </l>

                         <l xml:id="SS.1.15.41ab"><label>1931 ed. 1.15.41ab</label> eṣāṃ samatvaṃ
                              yac cāpi bhiṣagbhir avadhāryate | </l>

                         <l xml:id="SS.1.15.41cd"><label>1931 ed. 1.15.41cd</label> na tat
                              svāsthyādṛte śakyaṃ vaktum anyena hetunā || </l>

                         <l xml:id="SS.1.15.42ab"><label>1931 ed. 1.15.42ab</label> doṣādīnāṃ tv
                              asamatām anumānena lakṣayet | </l>

                         <l xml:id="SS.1.15.42cd"><label>1931 ed. 1.15.42cd</label> aprasannendriyaṃ
                              vīkṣya puruṣaṃ kuśalo bhiṣak || </l>

                         <l xml:id="SS.1.15.43ab"><label>1931 ed. 1.15.43ab</label> svasthasya
                              rakṣaṇaṃ kuryād asvasthasya tu buddhimān | </l>

                         <l xml:id="SS.1.15.43cd"><label>1931 ed. 1.15.43cd</label> kṣapayed
                              bṛṃhayec cāpi doṣadhātumalān bhiṣak | </l>

                         <l xml:id="SS.1.15.43ef"><label>1931 ed. 1.15.43ef</label> tāvad yāvad
                              arogaḥ syād etat sāmyasya lakṣaṇam || </l>

                         <l xml:id="SS.1.15.44ab"><label>1931 ed. 1.15.44ab</label> samadoṣaḥ
                              samāgniś ca samadhātumalakriyaḥ | </l>

                         <l xml:id="SS.1.15.44cd"><label>1931 ed. 1.15.44cd</label>
                              prasannātmendriyamanāḥ svasthā ity abhidhīyate ||</l>

                    <div n="16" type="adhyāya">

                         <head>ṣoḍaśo 'dhyāyaḥ |</head>

                         <l xml:id="SS.1.16.1"><label>1931 ed. 1.16.1</label> athātaḥ
                                   karṇavyadha<pc> </pc>bandha<pc> </pc>vidhim adhyāyaṃ
                              vyākhyāsyāmaḥ || </l>

                         <l xml:id="SS.1.16.2"><label>1931 ed. 1.16.2</label> yathovāca bhagavān
                              dhanavatariḥ || </l>

                         <l xml:id="SS.1.16.3"><label>1931 ed. 1.16.3</label> rakṣābhūṣaṇanimittaṃ
                              bālasya karṇau vidhyete | tau ṣaṣṭhe māsi saptame vā śuklapakṣe
                              praśasteṣu tithikaraṇamuhūrtanakṣatreṣu kṛtamaṅgalasvastivācanaṃ
                              dhātryaṅke kumāradharāṅke vā kumāram upaveśya bālakrīḍanakaiḥ
                              pralobhyābhisāntvayan bhiṣag vāmahastenākṛṣya karṇaṃ daivakṛte chidra
                              ādityakarāvabhāsite śanaiḥ śanair dakṣiṇahastena rju vidhyet
                              pratanukaṃ sūcyā bahalam ārayā pūrvaṃ dakṣiṇaṃ kumārasya vāmaṃ
                              kumāryāḥ tataḥ picuvartiṃ praveśayet || </l>

                         <l xml:id="SS.1.16.4"><label>1931 ed. 1.16.4</label> śoṇita<pc
                              > </pc>bahutvena vedanayā cānyadeśaviddham iti jānīyāt nirupadravatayā
                              taddeśaviddham iti || </l>

                         <l xml:id="SS.1.16.5"><label>1931 ed. 1.16.5</label> tatrājñena yadṛcchayā
                              viddhāsu sirāsu kālikāmarmarikālohitikāsūpadravā bhavanti | tatra
                              kālikāyāṃ jvaro dāhaḥ śvayathur vedanā ca bhavati marmarikāyāṃ vedanā
                              jvaro granthayaś ca lohitikāyāṃ
                              manyāstambhāpatānakaśirograhakarṇaśūlāni bhavanti | teṣu yathāsvaṃ
                              pratikurvīta || </l>

                         <l xml:id="SS.1.16.6"><label>1931 ed. 1.16.6</label>
                              kliṣṭajihmāpraśastasūcīvyadhād gāḍhataravartitvād doṣasamudāyād
                              apraśastavyadhād vā yatra saṃrambho vedanā vā bhavati tatra vartim
                              upahṛtyāśu madhukairaṇḍa<pc> </pc>mūla<pc> </pc>mañjiṣṭhā<pc
                                   > </pc>yava<pc> </pc>tila<pc> </pc>kalkair madhughṛtapragāḍhair
                              ālepayet tāvad yāvat surūḍha iti surūḍhaṃ cainaṃ punar vidhyet
                              vidhānaṃ tu pūrvoktam eva || </l>

                         <l xml:id="SS.1.16.7"><label>1931 ed. 1.16.7</label> tatra samyagviddham
                              āmatailena pariṣecayet tryahāt tryahāc ca vartiṃ sthūlatarāṃ dadyāt
                              pariṣekaṃ ca tam eva || </l>

                         <l xml:id="SS.1.16.8"><label>1931 ed. 1.16.8</label> atha
                              vyapagatadoṣopadrave karṇe vardhanārthaṃ laghuvardhanakaṃ kuryāt || </l>

                         <l xml:id="SS.1.16.9"><label>1931 ed. 1.16.9ab</label> evaṃ vivardhitaḥ
                              karṇaś chidyate tu dvidhā nṛṇām |
                              <caesura/>
                               doṣato vā'bhighātād vā sandhānaṃ tasya me śṛṇu || </l>

                         <l xml:id="SS.1.16.10"><label>1931 ed. 1.16.10</label> tatra samāsena
                              pañcadaśakarṇabandhākṛtayaḥ | tad yathā nemisandhānaka utpalabhedyako
                              vallūraka āsaṅgimo gaṇḍakarṇa āhāryo nirvedhimo vyāyojimaḥ
                              kapāṭasandhiko 'rdhakapāṭasandhikaḥ saṃkṣipto hīnakarṇo vallīkarṇo
                              yaṣṭikarṇaḥ kākauṣṭhaka iti | teṣu pṛthulāyatasamobhayapālir
                              nemisandhānakaḥ vṛttāyatasamobhayapālir utpalabhedyakaḥ
                              hrasvavṛttasamobhayapālir vallūrakaḥ abhyantaradīrghaikapālir
                              āsaṅgimaḥ bāhya<pc> </pc>dīrghaikapālir gaṇḍakarṇaḥ | apālir ubhayato
                              'py āhāryaḥ pīṭhopamapālir ubhayataḥ kṣīṇaputrikāśrito nirvedhimaḥ |
                              sthūlāṇusamaviṣamapālir vyāyojimaḥ | abhyantaradīrghaikapālir
                              itarālpapāliḥ | kapāṭasandhikaḥ bāhyadīrghaikapālir itarālpapālir
                              ardhakapāṭasandhikaḥ | tatra daśaite karṇabandhavikalpāḥ sādhyāḥ teṣāṃ
                              svanāmabhir evākṛtayaḥ prāyeṇa vyākhyātāḥ | saṃkṣiptādayaḥ
                              pañcāsādhyāḥ | tatra śuṣkaśaṣkulir utsannapālir itarālpapāliḥ
                              saṃkṣiptaḥ anadhiṣṭhānapāliḥ paryantayoḥ kṣīṇamāṃso hīnakarṇaḥ
                              tanuviṣamālpapālir vallīkarṇaḥ
                              grathitamāṃsastabdhasirāsaṃtatasūkṣmapālir yaṣṭikarṇaḥ
                              nirmāṃsasaṃkṣiptāgrālpaśoṇitapāliḥ kākauṣṭhaka iti | baddheṣv api tu
                                   śopha<pc> </pc>dāha<pc> </pc>rāga<pc> </pc>pāka<pc
                                   > </pc>piḍakā<pc> </pc>srāva<pc> </pc>yuktā na siddhim upayānti
                              || </l>

                         <l xml:id="SS.1.16.11"><label>1931 ed. 1.16.11</label> bhavanti cātra
                                   |<anchor n="SS.1.16.11"/></l>


                         <ab corresp="#SS.1.16.11" type="apparatus">
                              <list type="notes">
                                   <item corresp="#SS.1.16.11-n1">These verses in A (from
                                             <foreign>bhavanti cātra to śāstravit</foreign>) are
                                        absent from the Nepalese MSS and were probably absent in the
                                        version of the <emph>Suśrutasaṃhitā</emph> commented on by
                                        Cakrapāṇi, who cited them in his commentary as being "read
                                        by some" in regard to the joins
                                        (<foreign>sandhāna</foreign>) they describe.</item>
                              </list>

                         <l xml:id="SS.1.16.11ab"><label>1931 ed. 1.16.11ab</label> yasya pālidvayam
                              api karṇasya na bhaved iha | </l>

                         <l xml:id="SS.1.16.11cd"><label>1931 ed. 1.16.11cd</label> karṇapīṭhaṃ same
                              madhye tasya viddhvā vivardhayet || </l>

                         <l xml:id="SS.1.16.12ab"><label>1931 ed. 1.16.12ab</label> bāhyāyām iha
                              dīrghāyāṃ sandhir ābhyantaro bhavet | </l>

                         <l xml:id="SS.1.16.12cd"><label>1931 ed. 1.16.12cd</label> ābhyantarāyāṃ
                              dīrghāyāṃ bāhyasandhir udāhṛtaḥ || </l>

                         <l xml:id="SS.1.16.13ab"><label>1931 ed. 1.16.13ab</label> ekaiva tu bhavet
                              pāliḥ sthūlā pṛthvī sthirā ca yā | </l>

                         <l xml:id="SS.1.16.13cd"><label>1931 ed. 1.16.13cd</label> tāṃ dvidhā
                              pāṭayitvā tu chittvā copari sandhayet || </l>

                         <l xml:id="SS.1.16.14ab"><label>1931 ed. 1.16.14ab</label> gaṇḍād utpāṭya
                              māṃsena sānubandhena jīvatā | </l>

                         <l xml:id="SS.1.16.14cd"><label>1931 ed. 1.16.14cd</label> karṇapālīm
                              āpāles tu kuryān nirlikhya śāstravit || </l>

                         <l xml:id="SS.1.16.15"><label>1931 ed. 1.16.15</label> ato nyatamaṃ bandhaṃ
                              cikīrṣur agropaharaṇīyoktopasaṃbhṛtasaṃbhāraṃ viśeṣataś cātropaharet
                              surāmaṇḍaṃ kṣīram udakaṃ dhānyāmlaṃ kapālacūrṇaṃ ceti | tato 'ṅganāṃ
                              puruṣaṃ vā grathitakeśāntaṃ laghubhuktavantam āptaiḥ suparigṛhītaṃ ca
                              kṛtvā bandham upadhārya chedyabhedyalekhyavyadhanair upapannair
                              upapādya karṇaśoṇitam avekṣya duṣṭam aduṣṭaṃ veti tatra vātaduṣṭe
                              dhānyāmloṣṇodakābhyāṃ pittaduṣṭe śītodakapayobhyāṃ śleṣmaduṣṭe
                              surāmaṇḍoṣṇodakābhyāṃ prakṣālya karṇau punar avalikhyānunnatam ahīnam
                              aviṣamaṃ ca karṇasandhiṃ sanniveśya sthitaraktaṃ sandadhyāt | tato
                              madhughṛtenābhyajya picuprotayor anyatareṇāvaguṇṭhya
                              sūtreṇānavagāḍhaman atiśithilaṃ ca baddhvā kapālacūrṇenāvakīryācārikam
                              upadiśed dvivraṇīyoktena ca vidhānenopacaret || </l>

                         <l xml:id="SS.1.16.16"><label>1931 ed. 1.16.16</label> bhavati cātra | </l>

                         <l xml:id="SS.1.16.16x">vighaṭṭanaṃ divāsvapnaṃ vyāyāmam atibhojanam |
                              <caesura/>
                               vyavāyam agnisaṃtāpaṃ vākśramaṃ ca vivarjayet || </l>

                         <l xml:id="SS.1.16.16.1ab"><label>1931 ed. 1.16.16.1ab</label>
                              (?āmatailaparīṣekaṃ trirātramavacārayet | </l>

                         <l xml:id="SS.1.16.16.1cd"><label>1931 ed. 1.16.16.1cd</label> tatas
                              tailena saṃsṛṣṭaṃ tryahādapanayet picum ||) </l>

                         <l xml:id="SS.1.16.17"><label>1931 ed. 1.16.17</label> na cāśuddharaktam
                              atipravṛttaraktaṃ kṣīṇaraktaṃ vā saṃdadhyāt | sa hi vātaduṣṭe rakte
                              rūḍho 'pi paripuṭanavān pittaduṣṭe dāhapākarāgavedanāvān śleṣmaduṣṭe
                              stabdhaḥ kaṇḍūmān atipravṛttarakte śyāvaśophavān kṣīṇo 'lpamāṃso na
                              vṛddhim upaiti || </l>

                         <l xml:id="SS.1.16.18"><label>1931 ed. 1.16.18</label> āmatailena trirātraṃ
                              pariṣecayet trirātrāc ca picuṃ parivartayet | sa yadā surūḍho
                              nirupadravaḥ savarṇo bhavati tadainaṃ śanaiś śanair abhivardhayet |
                              ato 'nyathā saṃrambhadāhapākarāgavedanāvān punaś chidyate vā || </l>

                         <l xml:id="SS.1.16.19"><label>1931 ed. 1.16.19</label>
                              athāsyāpraduṣṭasyābhivardhanārtham abhyaṅgaḥ | tad yathā
                              godhāpratudaviṣkirānūpaudakavasāmajjānau payaḥ sarpis tailaṃ
                              gaurasarṣapajaṃ ca yathālābhaṃ
                              saṃbhṛtyārkālarkabalātibalānantāpāmārgāśvagandhāvidārigandhākṣīraśuklājalaśūkamadhuravargapayasyāprativāpaṃ
                              tailaṃ vā pācayitvā svanuguptaṃ nidadhyāt || </l>

                         <l xml:id="SS.1.16.20"><label>1931 ed. 1.16.20</label> sveditonmarditaṃ
                              karṇaṃ snehenaitena yojayet |
                              <caesura/>
                               ato 'nupadravaḥ samyag balavāṃś ca vivardhate || </l>


                         <l xml:id="SS.1.16.21"><label>1931 ed. 1.16.21</label>
                              yavāśvagandhāyaṣṭyāhvais tilaiś codvartanaṃ hitam |
                              <caesura/>
                               śatāvaryaśvagandhābhyāṃ payasyair aṇḍajīvanaiḥ || </l>

                         <l xml:id="SS.1.16.22"><label>1931 ed. 1.16.22</label> tailaṃ vipakvaṃ
                              sakṣīram abhyaṅgāt pālivardhanam |
                              <caesura/>
                               ye tu karṇā na vardhante svedasnehopapāditāḥ ||</l>

                         <l xml:id="SS.1.16.23"><label>1931 ed. 1.16.23</label> teṣām apāṅgadeśe tu
                              kuryāt pracchānam eva tu |</l>
                         <l xml:id="SS.1.16.23b"><label>1931 ed. 1.16.23cd</label> bāhyacchedaṃ na
                              kurvīta vyāpadaḥ syus tato dhruvāḥ || </l>

                         <l xml:id="SS.1.16.24"><label>1931 ed. 1.16.24</label> baddhamātraṃ tu yaḥ
                              karṇaṃ sahasaivābhivardhayet |
                              <caesura/>
                               āmakośī samādhmātaḥ kṣipram eva vimucyate || </l>

                         <l xml:id="SS.1.16.25"><label>1931 ed. 1.16.25</label> jātaromā suvartmā ca
                              śliṣṭasandhiḥ samaḥ sthiraḥ |
                              <caesura/>
                               surūḍho 'vedano yaś ca taṃ karṇaṃ vardhayec chanaiḥ || </l>

                         <l xml:id="SS.1.16.26.0"><label>1931 ed. 1.16.26.0</label> amitāḥ
                              karṇabandhās tu vijñeyāḥ kuśalair iha |
                              <caesura/>
                               yo yathā suviśiṣṭaḥ syāt taṃ tathā viniyojayet || </l>

                         <l xml:id="SS.1.16.26.1"><label>1931 ed. 1.16.26.1</label> (karṇapālyāmayān
                              nṝṇāṃ punar vakṣyāmi suśruta |
                              <caesura/>
                               karṇapalyāṃ prakupaitā vātapittakaphās trayaḥ || </l>

                         <l xml:id="SS.1.16.26.3"><label>1931 ed. 1.16.26.3</label> dvidhā vāpy atha
                              saṃsṛṣṭāḥ kurvanti vividhā rujaḥ |
                              <caesura/>
                               visphoṭaḥ stabdhatā śophaḥ pālyāṃ doṣe tu vātike ||
                              <caesura/>
                               dāhavisphoṭajananaṃ śophaḥ pākaś ca paittike |
                              <caesura/>
                               kaṇḍūḥ saśvayathuḥ stambho gurutvaṃ ca kaphātmake || </l>

                         <l xml:id="SS.1.16.26.4"><label>1931 ed. 1.16.26.4</label> yathādoṣaṃ ca
                              saṃśodhya kuryāt teṣāṃ cikitsitam |
                              <caesura/>
                               svedābhyaṅgaparīṣekaiḥ pralepāsṛgvimokṣaṇaiḥ || </l>

                         <l xml:id="SS.1.16.26.5"><label>1931 ed. 1.16.26.5</label> mṛdvīṃ kriyāṃ
                              bṛṃhaṇīyair yathāsvaṃ bhojanais tathā |
                              <caesura/>
                               ya evaṃ vetti doṣāṇāṃ cikitsāṃ kartum arhati || </l>

                         <l xml:id="SS.1.16.26.6"><label>1931 ed. 1.16.26.6</label> ata ūrdhvaṃ
                              nāmaliṅgair vakṣye pālyām upadravān |
                              <caesura/>
                               atpāṭakaś cotpuṭakaḥ śyāvaḥ kaṇḍūyuto bhṛśam || </l>

                         <l xml:id="SS.1.16.26.7"><label>1931 ed. 1.16.26.7</label> avamanthaḥ
                              sakaṇḍūko granthiko jambulas tathā |
                              <caesura/>
                               srāvī ca dāhavāṃś caiva śṛṇveṣāṃ kramaśaḥ kriyām || </l>

                         <l xml:id="SS.1.16.26.8"><label>1931 ed. 1.16.26.8</label> apāmārgaḥ
                              sarjarasaḥ pāṭalālakucatvacau |
                              <caesura/>
                               utpāṭake pralepaḥ syāt tailam ebhiś ca pācayet || </l>

                         <l xml:id="SS.1.16.26.9"><label>1931 ed. 1.16.26.9</label>
                              śampākaśigrupūtīkān godhāmedo 'tha tadvasām |
                              <caesura/>
                               vārāhaṃ gavyam aiṇeyaṃ pittaṃ sarpiś ca saṃsṛjet || </l>

                         <l xml:id="SS.1.16.26.10"><label>1931 ed. 1.16.26.10</label> lepam utpuṭake
                              dadyāt tailam ebhiś ca sādhitam |
                              <caesura/>
                               gaurīṃ sugandhāṃ saśyāmām anantāṃ taṇḍulīyakam | </l>

                         <l xml:id="SS.1.16.26.11"><label>1931 ed. 1.16.26.11</label> śyāve
                              pralepanaṃ dadyāt tailam ebhiś ca sādhitam |
                              <caesura/>
                               pāṭhāṃ rasāñjanaṃ kṣaudraṃ tathā syād uṣṇakāñjikam || </l>

                         <l xml:id="SS.1.16.26.12"><label>1931 ed. 1.16.26.12</label> dadyāl lepaṃ
                              sakaṇḍūke tailam ebhiś ca sādhitam |
                              <caesura/>
                               vraṇībhūtasya deyaṃ syād idaṃ tailaṃ vijānatā || </l>

                         <l xml:id="SS.1.16.26.13"><label>1931 ed. 1.16.26.13</label>
                              madhukakṣīrakākolījīvakādyair vipācitam |
                              <caesura/>
                               godhāvarāhasarpāṇāṃ vasāḥ syuḥ kṛtabṛṃhaṇe || </l>

                         <l xml:id="SS.1.16.26.14"><label>1931 ed. 1.16.26.14</label> pralepanam
                              idaṃ dadyād avasicyāvamanthake |
                              <caesura/>
                               prapauṇḍarīkaṃ madhukaṃ samaṅgāṃ dhavam eva ca || </l>

                         <l xml:id="SS.1.16.26.15"><label>1931 ed. 1.16.26.15</label> tailam ebhiś
                              ca saṃpakvaṃ śṛṇu kaṇḍūmataḥ kriyām |
                              <caesura/>
                               sahadevā viśvadevā ajākṣīraṃ sasaindhavam |
                              <caesura/>
                               etair ālepanaṃ dadyāt tailam ebhiś ca sādhitam || </l>

                         <l xml:id="SS.1.16.26.16"><label>1931 ed. 1.16.26.16</label> granthike
                              guṭikāṃ pūrvaṃ srāvayed avapāṭya tu |
                              <caesura/>
                               tataḥ saindhavacūrṇaṃ tu ghṛṣṭvā lepaṃ pradāpayet || </l>

                         <l xml:id="SS.1.16.26.17"><label>1931 ed. 1.16.26.17</label> likhitvā
                              tatsrutaṃ ghṛṣṭvā cūrṇair lodhrasya jambule |
                              <caesura/>
                               kṣīreṇa pratisāryainaṃ śuddhaṃ saṃropayet tataḥ || </l>

                         <l xml:id="SS.1.16.26.18"><label>1931 ed. 1.16.26.18</label> madhuparṇī
                              madhūkaṃ ca ma madhukaṃ madhunā saha |
                              <caesura/>
                               lepaḥ srāviṇi dātavyas tailam ebhiś ca sādhitam || </l>

                         <l xml:id="SS.1.16.26.19"><label>1931 ed. 1.16.26.19</label> pañcavalkaiḥ
                              samadhukaiḥ piṣṭais taiś ca ghṛtānvitaiḥ |
                              <caesura/>
                               jīvakādyaiḥ sasarpiṣkair dahyamānaṃ pralepayet ||) </l>

                         <l xml:id="SS.1.16.27"> viśleṣitāyās tv atha nāsikāyā
                              <caesura/>
                               vakṣyāmi sandhānavidhiṃ yathāvat |
                              <caesura/>
                               nāsāpramāṇaṃ pṛthivīruhāṇāṃ
                              <caesura/>
                               patraṃ gṛhītvā tv avalambi tasya || </l>

                         <l xml:id="SS.1.16.28"><label>1931 ed. 1.16.28</label> tena pramāṇena hi
                              gaṇḍapārśvād
                              <caesura/>
                               utkṛtya baddhaṃ tv atha nāsikāgram |
                              <caesura/>
                               vilikhya cāśu pratisaṃdadhīta
                              <caesura/>
                               tat sādhubandhair bhiṣag apramattaḥ || </l>

                         <l xml:id="SS.1.16.29"><label>1931 ed. 1.16.29</label> susaṃhitaṃ samyag
                              ato yathāvan
                              <caesura/>
                               nāḍīdvayenābhisamīkṣya baddhvā |
                              <caesura/>
                               pronnamya cainām avacūrṇayet tu
                              <caesura/>
                               pataṅgayaṣṭīmadhukāñjanaiś ca || </l>

                         <l xml:id="SS.1.16.30">saṃchādya samyak picunā sitena
                              <caesura/>
                               tailena siñced asakṛt tilānām |
                              <caesura/>
                               ghṛtaṃ ca pāyyaḥ sa naraḥ sujīrṇe
                              <caesura/>
                               snigdho virecyaḥ sa yathopadeśam || </l>

                         <l xml:id="SS.1.16.31">rūḍhaṃ ca sandhānam upāgataṃ syāt
                              <caesura/>
                               tad ardhaśeṣaṃ tu punar nikṛntet |
                              <caesura/>
                               hīnāṃ punar vardhayituṃ yateta
                              <caesura/>
                               samāṃ ca kuryād ativṛddhamāṃsām || </l>

                              vinauṣṭhasya nāsāsandhānavad vidhim |
                              <caesura/>
                               ya evam eva jānīyāt sa rājñaḥ kartum arhati || </l>

                         <head>saptadaśo 'dhyāyaḥ |</head>

                         <l xml:id="SS.1.17.1"><label>1931 ed. 1.17.1</label> athāta
                              āmapakvaiṣaṇīyam adhyāyaṃ vyākhyāsyāmaḥ || </l>

                         <l xml:id="SS.1.17.2"><label>1931 ed. 1.17.2</label> yathovāca bhagavān
                              dhanvantariḥ || </l>

                         <l xml:id="SS.1.17.3"><label>1931 ed. 1.17.3</label> śophasamutthānā
                              granthividradhyalajīprabhṛtayaḥ prāyeṇa vyādhayo 'bhihitā anekākṛtayaḥ
                              tair vilakṣaṇaḥ pṛthurgrathitaḥ samo viṣamo vā tvaṅnāṃsasthāyī
                              doṣasaṃghātaḥ śarīraikadeśotthitaḥ śopha ity ucyate || </l>

                         <l xml:id="SS.1.17.4"><label>1931 ed. 1.17.4</label> sa ṣaḍvidho
                              vātapittakaphaśoṇitasannipātāgantunimittaḥ | tasya doṣarūpavyañjanair
                              lakṣaṇāni vyākhyāsyāmaḥ | tatra vātaśopho 'ruṇaḥ kṛṣṇo vā paruṣo
                              mṛduranavasthitāstodāyaś cātra vedanāviśeṣā bhavanti pittaśophaḥ pīto
                              mṛduḥ sarakto vā śīghrānusāryoṣādayaś cātra vedanāviśeṣā bhavanti
                              śleṣmaśophaḥ pāṇḍuḥ śuklo vā kaṭhinaḥ śitaḥ snigdho mandānusārī
                              kaṇḍvādayaś cātra vedanāviśeṣā bhavanti sarvavarṇavedanaḥ sannipātajaḥ
                              pittavacchoṇitajo 'tikṛṣṇaś ca pittaraktalakṣaṇa āganturlohitāvabhāsaś
                              ca || </l>

                         <l xml:id="SS.1.17.5"><label>1931 ed. 1.17.5</label> sa yadā
                              bāhyābhyantaraiḥ kriyāviśeṣair na saṃbhāvitaḥ praśamayituṃ
                              kriyāviparyayādbahutvād vā doṣāṇāṃ tadā pākābhimukho bhavati |
                              tasyāmsya pacyamānasya pakvasya ca lakṣaṇamucyamānam upadhāraya |
                              tatra mandoṣmatā tvaksavarṇatā śītaśophatā sthairyaṃ
                              mandavedanatā'lpaśophatā cāmalakṣaṇamuddiṣṭaṃ sūcibhir iva nistudyate
                              daśyata iva pipīlikābhis tābhiś ca saṃsarpyata iva chidyata iva
                              śastreṇa bhidyata iva śaktibhis tāḍyata iva daṇḍena pīḍyata iva pāṇinā
                              ghaṭyata iva cāṅgulyā dahyate pacyata iva cāgnikṣārābhyāṃ
                              oṣacoṣaparīdāhāś ca bhavanti vṛś cikaviddha iva ca sthānāsanaśayaneṣu
                              na śāntim upaiti ādhmātabastirivātataś ca śopho bhavati tvagvaivarṇyaṃ
                              śophābhivṛddhirjvaradāhapipāsā bhaktāruciś ca pacyamānaliṅgaṃ
                              vedanopaśāntiḥ pāṇḍutā'lpaśophatā valīprādurbhāvastvakparipuṭanaṃ
                              nimnadarśanamaṅgulyā'vapīḍite pratyunnamanaṃ bastāvivodakasaṃcaraṇaṃ
                              pūyasya prapīḍayatyekamantamante vā'vapīḍite muhurmuhustodaḥ
                              kaṇḍūrunnatatā vyādherupadravaśāntirbhaktābhikāṅkṣā ca pakvaliṅgam || </l>

                         <l xml:id="SS.1.17.6"><label>1931 ed. 1.17.6</label> kaphajeṣu tu rogeṣu
                              gambhīragatitvād abhighātajeṣu vā keṣucid asamastaṃ pakvalakṣaṇaṃ
                              dṛṣṭvā pakvam apakvam iti manyamāno bhiṣaṅnoham upaiti | yatra hi
                              tvaksavarṇatā śītaśophatā sthaulyamalparujatā'śmavac ca ghanatā na
                              tatra moham upeyād iti || </l>

                         <l xml:id="SS.1.17.10"><label>1931 ed. 1.17.10</label> tatra āmacchede

                              vedanāprādurbhāvo 'vadaraṇam anekopadravadarśanaṃ kṣatavidradhirvā

                         <l xml:id="SS.1.17.15ab"><label>1931 ed. 1.17.15ab</label> alpo mahān vā

                              ca pradehas tūṣṇaḥ śīto vā bahalo 'bahur aviśoṣī ca madhaymo 'trālepaḥ

                              saṃdhānaḥ śodhano ropaṇaḥ śophavedanāpahaś ca tasyopayogaḥ
                              kṣatākṣateṣu yas tu kṣateṣūpayujyate sa bhūyaḥ kalka iti saṃjñāṃ

                         <l xml:id="SS.1.20.1"><label>1931 ed. 1.20.1</label> athāto hitāhitīyam
                              adhyāyaṃ vyākhyāsyāmaḥ || </l>

                         <l xml:id="SS.1.20.2"><label>1931 ed. 1.20.2</label> yathovāca bhagavān
                              dhanvantariḥ || </l>

                         <l xml:id="SS.1.20.3"><label>1931 ed. 1.20.3</label> yadvāyoḥ pathyaṃ tat
                              pittasyāpathyam ity anena hetunā na kiṃcid dravyam ekāntena hitam
                              ahitaṃ vā'stīti kecid ācāryā bruvate | tat tu na samyak | iha khalu
                              yasmād dravyāṇi svabhāvataḥ saṃyogataś caikāntahitāny ekāntāhitāni
                              hitāhitāni ca bhavanti || </l>

                         <l xml:id="SS.1.20.4"><label>1931 ed. 1.20.4</label> tatra ekāntahitāni
                              jātisātmyāt salilaghṛtadugdhaudanaprabhṛtīni ekāntāhitāni tu
                              dahanapacanamāraṇādiṣu pravṛttānyagnikṣāraviṣādīni saṃyogādaparāṇi
                              viṣatulyāni bhavanti hitāhitāni tu yadvāyoḥ pathyaṃ tatpittasyāpathyam
                              iti || </l>

                         <l xml:id="SS.1.20.5"><label>1931 ed. 1.20.5</label> ataḥ
                              sarvaprāṇināmayamāhārārthaṃ varga upadiśyate tad yathā
                              raktaśaliṣaṣṭikakaṅgukamukundakapāṇḍukapītakapramodakakālakāsanapuṣpakakardamakaśakunāhṛtasugandhakakalamanīvārakodravoddālakaśyāmākagodhūmaveṇuyavādaya
                              eṇahariṇakuraṅgamṛgamātṛkāśvadaṃṣṭrākarālakrakarakapotalāvatittirikapiñjalavartīravartikādīnāṃ
                              māṃsāni
                              mudgavanamudgamakuṣṭhakalāyamasūramaṅgalyacaṇakahareṇvāḍhakīsatīnāḥ
                              cillivāstukasuniṣaṇṇakajīvantītaṇḍulīyakamaṇḍūkaparṇyaḥ gavyaṃ ghṛtaṃ
                              saindhavadāḍimāmalakam ity eṣa vargaḥ sarvaprāṇināṃ sāmānyataḥ
                              pathyatamaḥ || </l>

                         <l xml:id="SS.1.20.6"><label>1931 ed. 1.20.6</label> tathā
                              brahmacaryanivātaśayanoṣṇodakasnānaniśāsvapnavyāyāmāś caikāntataḥ
                              pathyatamāḥ || </l>

                              ekāntahitānyekāntāhitāni ca prāgupadiṣṭāni hitāhitāni tu yadvāyoḥ
                              pathyaṃ tatpittasyāpathyam iti || </l>

                         <l xml:id="SS.1.20.13"><label>1931 ed. 1.20.13</label> ato 'nyāny api
                              saṃyogādahitāni vakṣyāmaḥ na vavirūḍhadhānyair vasāmadhupayoguḍamāṣair
                              vā grāmyānūpaudakapiśitādīni nābhyavaharet na payomadhubhyāṃ
                              rohiṇīśākaṃ jātukaśākaṃ vā'śnīyāt balākāṃ vāruṇīkulmāṣābhyāṃ kākamācīṃ
                              pippalīmaricābhyāṃ nāḍībhaṅgaśākakukkuṭadadhīni ca naikadhyaṃ madhu
                              coṣṇodakānupānaṃ pittena cāmamāṃsāni surākṛśarāpāyasāṃś ca naikadhyaṃ
                              sauvīrakeṇa saha tilaśaṣkulīṃ matsyaiḥ sahekṣuvikārān guḍena kākamācīṃ
                              madhunā mūlakaṃ guḍena vārāhaṃ madhunā ca saha viruddhaṃ kṣīreṇa
                              mūlakamāmrajāmbavaśvāvicchūkaragodhāś ca sarvāṃś ca matsyān payasā
                              viśeṣeṇa cilicimaṃ kadalīphalaṃ tālaphalena payasā dadhnā takreṇa vā
                              lakucaphalaṃ payasā dadhnā māṣasūpena vā prāk payasaḥ payaso 'nte vā
                              || </l>

                         <l xml:id="SS.1.20.14"><label>1931 ed. 1.20.14</label> ataḥ karmaviruddhān
                              vakṣyāmaḥ kapotān sarṣapatailabhṛṣṭānnādyāt
                              kapiñjalamayūralāvatittirigodhāś cairaṇḍadārvyagnisiddhā
                              eraṇḍatailasiddhā vā nādyāt kāṃsyabhājane daśarātraparyuṣitaṃ sarpiḥ
                              madhu coṣṇair uṣṇe vā matsyaparipacane śrṇgaveraparipacane vā siddhāṃ
                              kākamācīṃ tilakalkasiddhamupodikāśākaṃ nārikelena varāhavasā
                              paribhṛṣṭāṃ balākāṃ bhāsamaṅgāraśūlyaṃ nāśnīyād iti || </l>

                         <l xml:id="SS.1.20.15"><label>1931 ed. 1.20.15</label> ato mānaviruddhān

                         <l xml:id="SS.1.20.16"><label>1931 ed. 1.20.16</label> ata ūrdhvaṃ
                              rasadvandvāni rasato vīryato vipākataś ca viruddhāni vakṣyāmaḥ tatra
                              madhurāmlau rasavīryaviruddhau madhuralavaṇau ca madhurakaṭukau ca

                              rasataḥ amlakaṭukau rasavipākābhyāṃ amlatiktāvamlakaṣāyau ca sarvataḥ
                              lavaṇakaṭukau rasavipākābhyāṃ lavaṇatiktau lavaṇakaṣāyau ca sarvataḥ

                              viśeṣeṇa vraṇakledavivardhanaḥ || </l>

                         <l xml:id="SS.1.20.26ab"><label>1931 ed. 1.20.26ab</label> madhuraś
                              cāvidāhī ca kaṣāyānuraso laghuḥ | </l>

                         <l xml:id="SS.1.20.26cd"><label>1931 ed. 1.20.26cd</label> dakṣiṇo mārutaḥ
                              śreṣṭhaś cakṣuṣyo balavardhanaḥ || </l>

                         <l xml:id="SS.1.20.27ab"><label>1931 ed. 1.20.27ab</label>
                              raktapittapraśamano na ca vātaprakopaṇaḥ | </l>

                         <l xml:id="SS.1.20.27cd"><label>1931 ed. 1.20.27cd</label> viśado
                              rūkṣaparuṣaḥ kharaḥ snehabalāpahaḥ || </l>

                         <l xml:id="SS.1.20.28ab"><label>1931 ed. 1.20.28ab</label> paścimo
                              mārutastīkṣṇaḥ kaphamedoviśoṣaṇaḥ | </l>

                         <l xml:id="SS.1.20.28cd"><label>1931 ed. 1.20.28cd</label> sadyaḥ
                              prāṇakṣayakaraḥ śoṣaṇas tu śarīriṇām || </l>

                         <l xml:id="SS.1.20.29ab"><label>1931 ed. 1.20.29ab</label> uttaro mārutaḥ
                              snigdho mṛdurmadhura eva ca | </l>

                         <l xml:id="SS.1.20.29cd"><label>1931 ed. 1.20.29cd</label> kaṣāyānurasaḥ
                              śīto doṣāṇāṃ cāprakopaṇaḥ || </l>

                         <l xml:id="SS.1.20.30ab"><label>1931 ed. 1.20.30ab</label> tasmāc ca
                              prakṛtisthānāṃ kledano balavardhanaḥ | </l>

                         <l xml:id="SS.1.20.30cd"><label>1931 ed. 1.20.30cd</label>
                              kṣīṇakṣayaviṣārtānāṃ viśeṣeṇa tu pūjitaḥ || </l>
                         <p ana="trailer"> iti suśrutasaṃhitāyāṃ sūtrasthāne hitāhitīyo nāma viṃśo
                              'dhyāyaḥ || </p>
                    </div>




                    <div n="21" type="adhyāya">
                         <head> ekaviṃśatitamo 'dhyāyaḥ |</head>

                         <l xml:id="SS.1.21.1"><label>1931 ed. 1.21.1</label> athāto vraṇapraśnam
                              adhyāyaṃ vyākhyāsyāmaḥ || </l>

                         <l xml:id="SS.1.21.2"><label>1931 ed. 1.21.2</label> yathovāca bhagavān
                              dhanvantariḥ || </l>

                         <l xml:id="SS.1.21.3"><label>1931 ed. 1.21.3</label> vātapittaśleṣmāṇa eva
                              dehasaṃbhavahetavaḥ | tair evāvyāpannair adhomadhyor dhvasanniviṣṭaiḥ
                              śarīramidaṃ dhāryate 'gāram iva sthūṇābhis tisṛbhir ataś ca
                              tristhūṇamāhureke | ta eva ca vyāpannāḥ pralayahetavaḥ | tadebhir eva
                              śoṇitacaturthaiḥ saṃbhavasth itipralayeṣv apyavirahitaṃ śarīraṃ
                              bhavati || </l>

                         <l xml:id="SS.1.21.4"><label>1931 ed. 1.21.4</label> bhavati cātra | </l>

                         <l xml:id="SS.1.21.4ab"><label>1931 ed. 1.21.4ab</label> narte dehaḥ
                              kaphādasti na pittānna ca mārutāt | </l>

                         <l xml:id="SS.1.21.4cd"><label>1931 ed. 1.21.4cd</label> śoṇitād api vā
                              nityaṃ deha etais tu dhāryate || </l>

                         <l xml:id="SS.1.21.5"><label>1931 ed. 1.21.5</label> tatra vā
                              gatigandhanayor iti dhātuḥ tapa santāpe śliṣa āliṅgane eteṣāṃ
                              kṛdvihitaiḥ pratyayair vātaḥ pittaṃ śleṣmeti ca rūpāṇi bhavanti || </l>

                         <l xml:id="SS.1.21.6"><label>1931 ed. 1.21.6</label> doṣasthānānyata
                              ūrdhvaṃ vakṣyāmaḥ tatra samāsena vātaḥ śroṇigudasaṃśrayaḥ taduparyadho
                              nābheḥ pakvāśayaḥ pakvāmāśayamadhyaṃ pittasya āmāśayaḥ śleṣmaṇaḥ || </l>

                         <l xml:id="SS.1.21.7"><label>1931 ed. 1.21.7</label> ataḥ paraṃ pañcadhā
                              vibhajyante | tatra vātasya vātavyādhau vakṣyāmaḥ pittasya
                              yakṛtplīhānau hṛdayaṃ dṛṣtistvak pūrvoktaṃ ca
                              śleṣmaṇastūraḥśiraḥkaṇṭhasandhaya iti pūrvoktaṃ ca etāni khalu doṣāṇāṃ
                              sthānānyavyāpannānām || </l>

                         <l xml:id="SS.1.21.8ab"><label>1931 ed. 1.21.8ab</label>
                              visargādānavikṣepaiḥ somasūryānilā yathā | </l>

                         <l xml:id="SS.1.21.8cd"><label>1931 ed. 1.21.8cd</label> dhārayanti
                              jagaddehaṃ kaphapittānilās tathā || </l>

                         <l xml:id="SS.1.21.9"><label>1931 ed. 1.21.9</label> tatra jijñāsyaṃ kiṃ
                              pittavyatirekādanyo 'gniḥ āhosvit pittamevāgnir iti | atrocyate na
                              khalu pittavyatirekādanyo 'gnirupalabhyate āgneyatvāt pitte
                              dahanapacanādiṣvabhipravartamāneṣv agnivadupacāraḥ kriyate 'ntaragnir
                              iti kṣiṇe hy agniguṇe tatsamānadravyopayogādativṛddhe
                              śītakriyopayogādāgamāc ca paśyāmo na khalu pittavyatirekādanyo 'gnir
                              iti || </l>

                         <l xml:id="SS.1.21.10"><label>1931 ed. 1.21.10</label> taccādṛṣṭahetukena
                              viśeṣeṇa pakvāmāśayamadhyasthaṃ pittaṃ caturvidhamannapānaṃ pacati
                              vivecayati ca doṣarasamūtrapurīṣāṇi tatrastham eva cātmaśaktyā śeṣāṇāṃ
                              pittasthānānāṃ śarīrasya cāgnikarmaṇā'nugrahaṃ karoti tasmin pitte
                              pācako 'gnir iti saṃjñā yat tu yakṛtplīhnoḥ pittaṃ tasmin rañjako
                              'gnir iti saṃjñā sa rasasya rāgakṛduktaḥ yat pittaṃ hṛdayasaṃsthaṃ
                              tasmin sādhako 'gnir iti saṃjñā so
                              'bhiprārthitamanorathasādhanakṛduktaḥ yaddṛṣṭyāṃ pittaṃ tasminnālocako
                              'gnir iti saṃjñā sa rūpagrahaṇādhikṛtaḥ yat tu tvaci pittaṃ tasmin
                              bhrājako 'gnir iti saṃjñā so 'bhyaṅgapariṣekāvagāhāvalepanādīnāṃ
                              kriyādravyāṇāṃ paktā chāyānāṃ ca prakāśakaḥ || </l>

                         <l xml:id="SS.1.21.11ab"><label>1931 ed. 1.21.11ab</label> pittaṃ tīkṣṇaṃ
                              dravam pūti nīlaṃ pītaṃ tathaiva ca | </l>

                         <l xml:id="SS.1.21.11cd"><label>1931 ed. 1.21.11cd</label> uṣṇaṃ kaṭurasaṃ
                              caiva vidagdhaṃ cāmlam eva ca || </l>

                         <l xml:id="SS.1.21.12"><label>1931 ed. 1.21.12</label> ata ūrdhvaṃ
                              śleṣmasthānānyanuvyākhyāsyāmaḥ | tatra āmāśayaḥ
                              pittāśayasyopariṣṭhāttatpratyanīkatvād ūrdhvagatitvāt tejasaś candra
                              iva ādityasya sa caturvidhasyāhārasyādhāraḥ sa ca tatraudakair guṇair
                              āhāraḥ praklinno bhinnasaṃghātaḥ sukhajaraś ca bhavati || </l>

                         <l xml:id="SS.1.21.13ab"><label>1931 ed. 1.21.13ab</label> mādhuryāt
                              picchilatvāc ca prakleditvāt tathaiva ca | </l>

                         <l xml:id="SS.1.21.13cd"><label>1931 ed. 1.21.13cd</label> āmāśaye
                              saṃbhavati śleṣmā madhuraśītalaḥ || </l>

                         <l xml:id="SS.1.21.14"><label>1931 ed. 1.21.14</label> sa tatrastha eva
                              svaśaktyā śeṣāṇāṃ śleṣmasthānānāṃ śarīrasya codakakarmaṇā'nugrahaṃ
                              karoti uraḥsthastrikasandhāraṇamātmavīryeṇānnarasasahitena
                              hṛdayāvalambanaṃ karoti jihvāmūlakaṇṭhastho jihvendriyasya saumyatvāt
                              samyagrasajñāne vartate śiḥrasthaḥ snehasaṃtarpaṇādhikṛtatvād
                              indriyāṇāmātmavīryeṇānugrahaṃ karoti sandhisthas tu śleṣmā
                              sarvasandhisaṃśleṣāt sarvasandhyagranuhaṃ karoti || </l>

                         <l xml:id="SS.1.21.15ab"><label>1931 ed. 1.21.15ab</label> śleṣmā śveto
                              guruḥ snigdhaḥ picchilaḥ śīta eva ca | </l>

                         <l xml:id="SS.1.21.15cd"><label>1931 ed. 1.21.15cd</label>
                              madhurastvavigdhaḥ syādvidagdho lavaṇaḥ srṃtaḥ || </l>

                         <l xml:id="SS.1.21.16"><label>1931 ed. 1.21.16</label> śoṇitasya sthānaṃ
                              yakṛtplīhānau tac ca prāgabhihitaṃ tatrastham eva śeṣāṇāṃ
                              śoṇitasthānānāmanugrahaṃ karoti || </l>

                         <l xml:id="SS.1.21.17ab"><label>1931 ed. 1.21.17ab</label> anuṣṇaśītaṃ

                              visraṃ syādvidāhaś cāsya pittavat || </l>

                         <l xml:id="SS.1.21.18"><label>1931 ed. 1.21.18</label> etāni khalu
                              doṣasthānāni eṣu saṃcīyante doṣāḥ | prāk saṃcayahetur uktaḥ | tatra
                              saṃcitānāṃ khalu doṣāṇāṃ stabdhapūrṇakoṣṭhatā pītāvabhāsatā mandoṣmatā
                              cāṅgānāṃ gauravamālasyaṃ cayakāraṇavidveṣaś ceti liṅgāni bhavanti |
                              tatra prathamaḥ kriyākālaḥ || </l>

                         <l xml:id="SS.1.21.19"><label>1931 ed. 1.21.19</label> ata ūrdhvaṃ
                              prakopaṇāni vakṣyāmaḥ | tatra
                              balavadvigrahātivyāyāmavyavāyādhyayanaprapatanapradhāvanaprapīḍanābhighātalaṅghanaplavanataraṇarātrijāgaraṇabhāraharaṇagajaturagarathapadāticaryākaṭukaṣāyatiktarūkṣalaghuśītavīryaśuṣkaśākavallūravarakoddālakakoradūṣaśyāmākanīvāramudgamasūrāḍhakīhareṇukalāyaniṣpāvānaśanaviṣamāśanādhyaśanavātamūtrapurīṣaśukracchardikṣavathūdgārabāṣpavegavighātādibhir
                              viśeṣair vāyuḥ prakopamāpadyate || </l>

                         <l xml:id="SS.1.21.20ab"><label>1931 ed. 1.21.20ab</label> sa
                              śītābhrapravāteṣu gharmānte ca viśeṣataḥ | </l>

                         <l xml:id="SS.1.21.20cd"><label>1931 ed. 1.21.20cd</label>
                              pratyūṣasyaparāhṇe tu jīrṇe 'nne ca prakupyati || </l>

                         <l xml:id="SS.1.21.21"><label>1931 ed. 1.21.21</label>
                              krodhaśokabhayāyāsopavāsavidagdhamaithunopagamanakaṭvamlalavaṇatīkṣṇoṣṇalaghuvidāhitilatailapiṇyākakulatthasarṣapātasīharitakaśākagodhāmatsyājāvikamāṃsadadhitakrakūrcikāmastusauvīrakasurāvikārāmlaphalakaṭvaraprabhṛtibhiḥ
                              pittaṃ prakopamāpadyate || </l>

                         <l xml:id="SS.1.21.22ab"><label>1931 ed. 1.21.22ab</label> taduṣṇair

                         <l xml:id="SS.1.21.22cd"><label>1931 ed. 1.21.22cd</label> madhyāhne
                              cārdharātre ca jīryatyanne ca kupyati || </l>

                         <l xml:id="SS.1.21.23"><label>1931 ed. 1.21.23</label>
                              divāsvapnāvyāyāmālasyamadhurāmlalavaṇaśītasnigdhagurupicchilābhiṣyandihāyanakayavakanaiṣadhetkaṭamāṣamahāmāṣagodhūma-tila-piṣṭa-vikṛtidadhidugdhakṛśarāpāyasekṣu-vikārānūpaudakamāṃsavasābisamṛṇālakaserukaśṛṅgāṭakamadhura-vallī-phalasamaśanādhyaśanaprabhṛtibhiḥ

                         <l xml:id="SS.1.21.24cd"><label>1931 ed. 1.21.24cd</label> pūrvāhṇe ca
                              pradoṣe ca bhuktamātre prakupyati || </l>

                         <l xml:id="SS.1.21.25"><label>1931 ed. 1.21.25</label> pittaprakopaṇair eva

                              divāsvapnakrodhānalātapaśramābhighātājīrṇaviruddhādhyaśanādibhir

                         <l xml:id="SS.1.21.26ab"><label>1931 ed. 1.21.26ab</label> yasmādraktmaṃ

                         <l xml:id="SS.1.21.26cd"><label>1931 ed. 1.21.26cd</label> tasmāt tasya
