                         <l xml:id="SS.1.21.27"><label>1931 ed. 1.21.27</label> teṣāṃ prakopāt
                              koṣṭhatodasaṃcaraṇāmlikāpipāsāparidāhānnadveṣahṛdayotkledāś ca jāyante
                              | tatra dvitīyaḥ kriyākālaḥ || </l>

                         <l xml:id="SS.1.21.28"><label>1931 ed. 1.21.28</label> ata ūrdhvaṃ prasaraṃ
                              vakṣyāmaḥ teṣām ebhir ātaṅkaviśeṣaiḥ prakupitānāṃ (paryuṣita)
                              kiṇvodakapiṣṭasamavāya ivodriktānāṃ prasaro bhavati | teṣāṃ vāyur
                              gatimattvāt prasaraṇahetuḥ saty apy acaitanye | sa hi rajobhūyiṣṭhaḥ
                              rajaś ca pravartakaṃ sarvabhāvānām | yathā mahānudakasaṃcayo
                              'tivṛddhaḥ setumavadāryāpareṇodakena vyāmiśraḥ sarvataḥ pradhāvati
                              evaṃ doṣāḥ kadācidekaśo dviśaḥ samastāḥ śoṇitasahitā vā'nekadhā
                              prasaranti | tad yathā vātaḥ pittaṃ śleṣmā śoṇitaṃ vātapitte
                              vātaśleṣmāṇau pittaśleṣmāṇau vātaśoṇite pittaśoṇite śleṣmaśoṇite
                              vātapittaśoṇitāni vātaśleṣmaśoṇitāni pittaśleṣmaśoṇitāni
                              vātapittakaphāḥ vātapittakaphaśoṇitāni ity evaṃ pañcadaśadhā prasanti
                              || </l>

                         <l xml:id="SS.1.21.29ab"><label>1931 ed. 1.21.29ab</label> kṛtsne 'rdhe
                              'vayave vā'pi yatrāṅge kupito bhṛśam | </l>

                         <l xml:id="SS.1.21.29cd"><label>1931 ed. 1.21.29cd</label> doṣo vikāraṃ
                              nabhasi meghavattatra varṣati || </l>

                         <l xml:id="SS.1.21.30ab"><label>1931 ed. 1.21.30ab</label> nātyarthaṃ
                              kupitaś cāpi līno mārgeṣu tiṣṭhati | </l>

                         <l xml:id="SS.1.21.30cd"><label>1931 ed. 1.21.30cd</label> niṣpratyanīkaḥ
                              kālena hetumāsādya kupyati || </l>

                         <l xml:id="SS.1.21.31"><label>1931 ed. 1.21.31</label> tatra vāyoḥ
                              pittasthānagatasya pittavat pratīkāraḥ pittasya ca kaphasthānagatasya
                              kaphavat kaphasya ca vātasthānagatasya vātavat eṣa kriyāvibhāgaḥ || </l>

                         <l xml:id="SS.1.21.32"><label>1931 ed. 1.21.32</label> evaṃ prakupitānāṃ
                              prasaratāṃ ca vāyor vimārgagamanāṭopau oṣacoṣaparidāhadhūmāyanāni
                              pittasya arocakāvipākāṅgasādāś chardiś ceti śleṣmaṇo liṅgāni bavanti
                              tatra tṛtīyaḥ kriyākālaḥ || </l>

                         <l xml:id="SS.1.21.33"><label>1931 ed. 1.21.33</label> ata ūrdhvaṃ
                              sthānasaṃśrayaṃ | evaṃ prakupitāḥ tāṃstān śarīrapradeśānāgamya tāṃstān
                              vyādhīn janayanti | te yadodarasanniveśaṃ kurvanti tadā
                              gulmavidradhyudarāgnisaṅgānāhavisūcikātisāraprabhṛtīn janayanti
                              bastigatāḥ pramehāśmarīmūtrāghātamūtradoṣaprabhṛtīn vṛṣaṇagatā vṛddhīḥ
                              meḍhragatā niruddhaprakaśopadaṃśaśūkadoṣaprabhṛtīn gudagatā
                              bhagandarārśaḥprabhṛtīn ūrdhvajatrugatāstūrdhvajān
                              tavaṅnāṃsaśoṇitasthāḥ kṣudrarogān kuṣṭhāni visarpāṃś ca medogatā
                              granthyapacyarbudagalagaṇḍālajīprabhṛtīn asthigatā
                              vidradhyanuśayīprabhṛtīn pādagatāḥ
                              ślīpadavātaśoṇitavātakaṇṭakaprabhṛtīn sarvāṅgāgatā
                              jvarasaravāṅgarogaprabhṛtīn teṣāmevamabhiniviṣṭānāṃ
                              pūrvarūpaprādurbhāvaḥ taṃ pratirogaṃ vakṣyāmaḥ | tatra pūrvarūpagateṣu
                              caturthaḥ kriyākālaḥ || </l>

                         <l xml:id="SS.1.21.34"><label>1931 ed. 1.21.34</label> ata ūrdhvaṃ
                              vyādherdarśanaṃ vakṣyāmaḥ śophārbudagranthividradhivisarpaprabhṛtīnāṃ
                              pravyaktalakṣaṇatā jvarātīsāraprabhṛtīnāṃ ca | tatra pañcamaḥ
                              kriyākālaḥ || </l>

                         <l xml:id="SS.1.21.35"><label>1931 ed. 1.21.35</label> ata
                              ūrdhvameteṣāmavadīrṇānāṃ braṇabhāvamāpannānāṃ ṣaṣṭhaḥ kriyākālaḥ
                              jvarātisāraprabhṛtīnāṃ ca dīrghakālānubandhaḥ | tatrāpratikriyamāṇe
                              'sādhyatām upayānti || </l>

                         <l xml:id="SS.1.21.36"><label>1931 ed. 1.21.36</label> bhavanti cātra | </l>

                         <l xml:id="SS.1.21.36ab"><label>1931 ed. 1.21.36ab</label> saṃcayaṃ ca
                              prakopaṃ ca prasaraṃ sthānasaṃśrayam | </l>

                         <l xml:id="SS.1.21.36cd"><label>1931 ed. 1.21.36cd</label> vyaktiṃ bhedaṃ
                              ca yo vetti doṣāṇāṃ sa bhavedbhiṣak || </l>

                         <l xml:id="SS.1.21.37ab"><label>1931 ed. 1.21.37ab</label> saṃcaye 'pahṛtā
                              doṣā labhante nottarā gatīḥ | </l>

                         <l xml:id="SS.1.21.37cd"><label>1931 ed. 1.21.37cd</label> te tūttarāsu
                              gatiṣu bhavanti balavattarāḥ || </l>

                         <l xml:id="SS.1.21.38ab"><label>1931 ed. 1.21.38ab</label> sarvair bhāvais
                              tribhir vā'pi dvābhyāmekena vā punaḥ | </l>

                         <l xml:id="SS.1.21.38cd"><label>1931 ed. 1.21.38cd</label> saṃsarge kupitaḥ
                              kruddhaṃ doṣaṃ doṣo 'nudhāvati || </l>

                         <l xml:id="SS.1.21.39ab"><label>1931 ed. 1.21.39ab</label> saṃsarge yo
                              garīyān syādupakramyaḥ sa vai bhavet | </l>

                         <l xml:id="SS.1.21.39cd"><label>1931 ed. 1.21.39cd</label>
                              śeṣadoṣāvirodhena sannipāte tathaiva ca || </l>

                         <l xml:id="SS.1.21.40ab"><label>1931 ed. 1.21.40ab</label> vṛṇoti yasmāt
                              rūḍhe 'pi vraṇavas tu na naśyati | </l>

                         <l xml:id="SS.1.21.40cd"><label>1931 ed. 1.21.40cd</label>
                              ādehadhāraṇāttasmād draṇa ity ucyate budhaiḥ || </l>
                         <p ana="trailer">iti suśrutasaṃhitāyāṃ sūtrashtāne vraṇapraśnādhyāyo
                              nāmaikaviṃśodhyāyaḥ </p>
                    </div>



                    <div n="22" type="adhyāya">
                         <head> dvāviṃśatitamo 'dhyāyaḥ |</head>

                         <l xml:id="SS.1.22.1"><label>1931 ed. 1.22.1</label> athāto
                              vraṇāsrāvavijñānīyam adhyāyaṃ vyākhyāsyamaḥ || </l>

                         <l xml:id="SS.1.22.2"><label>1931 ed. 1.22.2</label> yathovāca bhagavān
                              dhanvantariḥ || </l>

                         <l xml:id="SS.1.22.3"><label>1931 ed. 1.22.3</label>
                              tvaṅnāṃsasirāsnāyvasthisandhikoṣṭhamarmāṇītyaṣṭau vraṇavastūni | atra
                              sarvavraṇasanniveśaḥ || </l>

                         <l xml:id="SS.1.22.4"><label>1931 ed. 1.22.4</label> tatra
                              ādyaikavastusanniveśī tvagbhedī vraṇaḥ sūpacaraḥ śeṣāḥ
                              svayamavaddīryamāṇā durupacārāḥ || </l>

                         <l xml:id="SS.1.22.5"><label>1931 ed. 1.22.5</label> tatrāyataś caturasro
                              vṛttastripuṭaka iti vraṇākṛtisamāsaḥ śeṣās tu vikṛtākṛtayo durupakramā
                              bhavanti || </l>

                         <l xml:id="SS.1.22.6"><label>1931 ed. 1.22.6</label> sarva eva vraṇāḥ
                              kṣipraṃ saṃrohantyātmavatāṃ subhiṣagbhiś copakrāntāḥ anātmavatāmajñaiś
                              copakrāntāḥ praduṣyanti pravṛddhatvāc ca doṣāṇāṃ || </l>

                         <l xml:id="SS.1.22.7"><label>1931 ed. 1.22.7</label> tatrātisaṃvṛto
                              'tivivṛto 'tikaṭhino 'timṛdurutsanno 'vasanno 'tiśīto 'tyuṣṇaḥ
                              kṛṣṇaraktapītaśuklādīnāṃ varṇānām anyatamavarṇo bhairavaḥ
                              pūtipūyamāṃsasirāsnāyuprabhṛtibhiḥ pūrṇaḥ
                              pūtipūyāsrāvyunmārgyutsaṅgyamanojñadarśanagandho 'tyarthaṃ vedanāvān
                              dāhapākarāgakaṇḍūśophapiḍakopadruto 'tyarthaṃ duṣṭaśoṇitāsrāvī
                              dīrghakālānubandhī ceti duṣṭavraṇaliṅgāni | tasya doṣocchrāyeṇa
                              ṣaṭtvaṃ vibhajya yathāsvaṃ pratīkāre prayateta || </l>

                         <l xml:id="SS.1.22.8"><label>1931 ed. 1.22.8</label> ata ūrdhvaṃ
                              sarvasrāvān vakṣyāmaḥ tatra ghṛṣṭāsu chinnāsu vā tvakṣu sphoṭeṣu
                              bhinneṣu vidāriteṣu vā salilaprakāśo bhavatyāsrāvaḥ kiṃcidvisraḥ
                              pītāvabhāsaś ca māṃsagataḥ sadyaś chinnāsu sirāsu raktātipravṛttiḥ
                              pakvāsu ca toyanāḍībhir iva toyāgamanaṃ pūyasya āsrāvaś cātra tanur
                              vicchinnaḥ picchilo 'valambī śyāvo 'vaśyāyapratimaś ca snāyugataḥ
                              snigdho ghanaḥ siṃghāṇakapratimaḥ saraktaś ca asthigato
                              'sthanyabhihate sphuṭite bhinne doṣāvadārite vā doṣabhakṣitatvād asthi
                              niḥsāraṃ śuktidhautamivābhāti āsrāvaś cātra majjamiśraḥ sarudhiraḥ
                              snigdhaś ca saṃdhigataḥ pīḍyamāno na pravartate
                              ākuñcanaprasāraṇonnamanavinamanapradhāvanotkāsanapravāhaṇaiś ca
                              sravati āsrāvaś cātra picchilo 'valambī saphenapūyarudhironmathitaś ca
                              koṣṭhagato 'sṛṅnūtrapurīṣapūyodakāni sravati
                              marmagatastvagādiṣvavaruddhatvānnocyate | tatra
                              tvagādigatānāmāsrāvāṇāṃ yathākramaṃ
                              pāruṣyaśyāvāvaśyāyadadhimastukṣārodakamāṃsadhāvanapulākodakasannibhatvāni
                              mārutādbhavanti pittād
                              gomedagomūtrabhasmaśaṅkhakaṣāyodakamādhvīkatailasannibhatvāni
                              pittavadraktādativisratvaṃ ca
                              kaphānnavanītakāsīsamajjapiṣṭatilanārikelodakavarāhavasāsannibhatvāni
                              sannipātānnārikelodakair
                              vārukarasakāñjikaprasādārukodakapriyaṅguphalayakṛnmudgayūṣasavarṇatvānīti
                              || </l>

                         <l xml:id="SS.1.22.9"><label>1931 ed. 1.22.9</label> ślokau cātra bhavataḥ
                              | </l>
                         <lg>

                              <l xml:id="SS.1.22.9ab"><label>1931 ed. 1.22.9ab</label>
                                   pakvāśayādasādhyas tu pulākodakasannibhiḥ |</l>

                              <l xml:id="SS.1.22.9cd"><label>1931 ed. 1.22.9cd</label>
                                   kṣārodakanibhaḥ srāvo varjyo raktāśayātsravan || </l>
                         </lg>
                         <lg>

                              <l xml:id="SS.1.22.10ab"><label>1931 ed. 1.22.10ab</label> āmāśayāt
                                   kalāyāmbhonibhaś ca trikasandhijaḥ |</l>

                              <l xml:id="SS.1.22.10cd"><label>1931 ed. 1.22.10cd</label> srāvānetān
                                   parīkṣyādau tataḥ karmācaredbhiṣak ||</l>
                         </lg>

                         <l xml:id="SS.1.22.11"><label>1931 ed. 1.22.11</label> ata ūrdhvaṃ
                              sarvavraṇavedanā vakṣyāmaḥ
                              todanabhedanatāḍanacchedanāyamanamanthanavikṣepaṇacum
                              cumāyananirdahanāvabhañjanasphoṭanavidāraṇotpāṭanakampanavividhaśūlaviśleṣaṇavikiraṇapūraṇastambhanasvapnākuñcanāṅkuśikāḥ
                              saṃbhavanti animittavividhavedanāprādurbhāvo vā muhurmuhur
                              yatrāgacchanti vedanāviśeṣāstaṃ vātikam iti vidyāt
                              oṣacoṣaparidāhadhūmāyanāni yatra gātramaṅgārāvakīrṇam iva pacyate
                              yatra coṣmābhivṛddhiḥ kṣate kṣārāvasiktavac ca vedanāviśeṣāstaṃ
                              paittikam iti vidyāt pittavadraktasamutthaṃ jānīyāt kaṇḍūrgurutvaṃ
                              suptatvam upadeho 'lpavedanatvaṃ stambhaḥ śaityaṃ ca yatra taṃ
                              ślaiṣmikam iti vidyāt yatra sarvāsāṃ vedanānām utpattis taṃ
                              sānnipātikam iti vidyāt || </l>

                         <l xml:id="SS.1.22.12"><label>1931 ed. 1.22.12</label> ata ūrdhvaṃ
                              vraṇavarṇān vakṣyāmaḥ bhasmakapotāsthivarṇaḥ paruṣo 'ruṇaḥ kṛṣṇa iti
                              mārutajasya nīlaḥ pīto haritaḥ śyāvaḥ kṛṣṇo raktaḥ kapilaḥ piṅgala iti
                              raktapittasamutthayoḥ śvetaḥ snigdhaḥ pāṇḍur iti śleṣmajasya
                              sarvavarṇopetaḥ sānnipātika iti || </l>

                         <l xml:id="SS.1.22.13"><label>1931 ed. 1.22.13</label> bhavati cātra | </l>

                         <l xml:id="SS.1.22.13ab"><label>1931 ed. 1.22.13ab</label> na kevalaṃ
                              vraṇeṣūkto vedanāvarṇasaṃgrahaḥ | </l>

                         <l xml:id="SS.1.22.13cd"><label>1931 ed. 1.22.13cd</label>
                              sarvaśophavikāreṣu vraṇaval lakṣayed bhiṣak || </l>
                    </div>




                    <div n="23" type="adhyāya">
                         <head>trayoviṃśatitamo 'dhyāyaḥ |</head>

                         <l xml:id="SS.1.23.1"><label>1931 ed. 1.23.1</label> athātaḥ
                              kṛtyākṛtyavidhim adhyāyaṃ vyākhyāsyāmaḥ || </l>

                         <l xml:id="SS.1.23.2"><label>1931 ed. 1.23.2</label> yathovāca bhagavān
                              dhanantariḥ || </l>

                         <l xml:id="SS.1.23.3"><label>1931 ed. 1.23.3</label> tatra vayaḥsthānāṃ
                              dṛḍhānāṃ prāṇavatāṃ sattvavatāṃ ca sucikitsyā vraṇāḥekasmin vā puruṣe
                              yatraitad guṇacatuṣṭayaṃ tasya sukhasādhanīyatamāḥ | tatra
                              vayaḥsthānāṃ pratyagradhātutvād āśu vraṇā rohanti dṛḍhānāṃ
                              sthirabahumāṃsatvāc chastram avacāryamāṇaṃ sirāsnāyvādiviśeṣān na
                              prāpnoti prāṇavatāṃ vedanābhighātāhārayantraṇādibhir na glānir
                              utpadyate sattvavatāṃ dāruṇair api kriyāviśeṣair na vyathā bhavati
                              tasmād eteṣāṃ sukhasādhanīyatamāḥ || </l>

                         <l xml:id="SS.1.23.4"><label>1931 ed. 1.23.4</label> ta eva viparītaguṇā
                              vṛddhakṛśālpaprāṇabhīruṣu draṣṭavyāḥ || </l>

                         <l xml:id="SS.1.23.5"><label>1931 ed. 1.23.5</label>
                              sphikpāyuprajananalalāṭagaṇḍauṣṭhapṛṣṭhakarṇaphalakoṣodarajatrumukhābhyantarasaṃsthāḥ
                              sukharopaṇīyā vraṇāḥ || </l>

                         <l xml:id="SS.1.23.6"><label>1931 ed. 1.23.6</label>
                              akṣidantanāsāpāṅgaśrotranābhijaṭharasevanīnitambapārśvakukṣivakṣaḥkakṣāstanasandhibhāgagatāḥ
                              saphenapūyaraktānilavāhino 'ntaḥśalyāś ca duścikitsyāḥ adhobhāgāś
                              cordhvabhāganirvāhiṇo romāntopanakhamarmajaṅghāsthisaṃśritāś ca
                              bhagandaram api cāntarmukhaṃ sevanīkuṭakāsthisaṃśritam || </l>

                         <l xml:id="SS.1.23.7ab"><label>1931 ed. 1.23.7ab</label> kuṣṭhināṃ
                              viṣajuṣṭānāṃ śoṣiṇāṃ madhumehinām | </l>

                         <l xml:id="SS.1.23.7cd"><label>1931 ed. 1.23.7cd</label> vraṇāḥ kṛcchreṇa
                              sidhyanti yeṣāṃ cāpi vraṇe vraṇāḥ || </l>

                         <l xml:id="SS.1.23.8"><label>1931 ed. 1.23.8</label>
                              avapāṭikāniruddhaprakaśasanniruddhagudajaṭharagranthikṣatakrimayaḥ
                              pratiśyāyajāḥ koṣṭhajāś ca tvagdoṣiṇāṃ pramehiṇāṃ vā ye parikṣateṣu
                              dṛśyante śarkarā sikatāmeho vātakuṇḍalikā'ṣṭhīlā dantaśarkaropakuśaḥ
                              kaṇṭhaśālūkaṃ niṣkoṣaṇadūṣitāś ca dantaveṣṭā
                              visarpāsthikṣatoraḥkṣatavraṇagranthiprabhṛtayaś ca yāpyāḥ || </l>

                         <l xml:id="SS.1.23.9ab"><label>1931 ed. 1.23.9ab</label> sādhyā yāpyatvam
                              āyānti yāpyāś cāsādhyatāṃ tathā | </l>

                         <l xml:id="SS.1.23.9cd"><label>1931 ed. 1.23.9cd</label> ghnanti prāṇān
                              asādhyās tu narāṇām akriyāvatām || </l>

                         <l xml:id="SS.1.23.10ab"><label>1931 ed. 1.23.10ab</label> yāpanīyaṃ
                              vijānīyāt kriyā dhārayate tu yam | </l>

                         <l xml:id="SS.1.23.10cd"><label>1931 ed. 1.23.10cd</label> kriyāyāṃ tu
                              nivṛttāyāṃ sadya eva vinaśyati || </l>

                         <l xml:id="SS.1.23.11ab"><label>1931 ed. 1.23.11ab</label> prāptā kriyā
                              dhārayati yāpyavayādhitam āturam | </l>

                         <l xml:id="SS.1.23.11cd"><label>1931 ed. 1.23.11cd</label>
                              prapatiṣyadivāgāraṃ viṣkambhaḥ sādhuyoajitaḥ || </l>

                         <l xml:id="SS.1.23.12"><label>1931 ed. 1.23.12</label> ata ūrdhvam asādhyān
                              vakṣyāmaḥ māṃsapiṇḍavad udgatāḥ prasekino 'ntaḥpūyavedanāvanto
                              'śvāpānavad udvṛttauṣṭhāḥ kecit kaṭhinā gośṛṅgavad
                              unnatamṛdumāṃsaprarohāḥ apare
                              duṣṭarudhirāsrāviṇastanuśītapicchilasrāviṇo vā madhyonnatāḥ kecid
                              avasannaśuṣiraparyantāḥ śaṇatūlavat snāyujālavanto durdarśanāḥ
                              vasāmedomajjamastuluṅgasrāviṇaś ca doṣasamutthāḥ
                              pītāsitamūtrapurīṣavātavāhinaś ca koṣṭhasthāḥ ta
                              evobhayatobhāgavraṇamukheṣu pūyaraktanirvāhiṇaḥ (ā.kṣīṇamāṃsānāṃ ca)
                              sarvato gatayaś cāṇumukhā māṃsabudbudavantaḥ saśabdavātavāhinaś ca
                              śiraḥkaṇṭhasthāḥ kṣīṇamāṃsānāṃ ca pūyaraktanirvāhiṇo
                              'rocakāvipākakāsaśvāsopadravayuktāḥ bhinne vā śiraḥkapāle yatra
                              mastuluṅgadarśanaṃ tridoṣaliṅgaprādurbhāvaḥ kāsaśvāsau vā yasyeti || </l>

                         <l xml:id="SS.1.23.13"><label>1931 ed. 1.23.13</label> bhavanti cātra | </l>

                         <l xml:id="SS.1.23.13ab"><label>1931 ed. 1.23.13ab</label> vasāṃ medo 'tha
                              majjānaṃ mastuluṅgaṃ ca yaḥ sravet | </l>

                         <l xml:id="SS.1.23.13cd"><label>1931 ed. 1.23.13cd</label> āgantus tu
                              vraṇaḥ sidhyen na sidhyed doṣasaṃbhavaḥ || </l>

                         <l xml:id="SS.1.23.14ab"><label>1931 ed. 1.23.14ab</label> amarmopahite
                              deśe sirāsandhyasthivarjite | </l>

                         <l xml:id="SS.1.23.14cd"><label>1931 ed. 1.23.14cd</label> vikāro yo
                              'nuparyeti tad asādhyasya lakṣaṇam || </l>

                         <l xml:id="SS.1.23.15ab"><label>1931 ed. 1.23.15ab</label> krameṇopacayaṃ
                              prāpya dhatūn anugataḥ śanaiḥ | </l>

                         <l xml:id="SS.1.23.15cd"><label>1931 ed. 1.23.15cd</label> na śakya
                              unmūlayituṃ vṛddho vṛkṣa ivāmayaḥ || </l>

                         <l xml:id="SS.1.23.16ab"><label>1931 ed. 1.23.16ab</label> sa sthiratvān
                              mahattvāc ca dhātvanukramaṇena ca | </l>

                         <l xml:id="SS.1.23.16cd"><label>1931 ed. 1.23.16cd</label>
                              nihantyauṣadhavīryāṇi mantrān duṣṭagraho yathā || </l>

                         <l xml:id="SS.1.23.17ab"><label>1931 ed. 1.23.17ab</label> ato yo viparītaḥ
                              syāt sukhasādhyaḥ sa ucyate | </l>

                         <l xml:id="SS.1.23.17cd"><label>1931 ed. 1.23.17cd</label> abaddhamūlaḥ
                              kṣupako yadvad utpāṭane sukhaḥ || </l>

                         <l xml:id="SS.1.23.18ab"><label>1931 ed. 1.23.18ab</label> tribhir doṣair
                              anākrāntaḥ śyāvauṣṭhaḥ piḍakī samaḥ | </l>

                         <l xml:id="SS.1.23.18cd"><label>1931 ed. 1.23.18cd</label> avedano
                              nirāsrāvo vraṇaḥ śuddha ihocyate || </l>

                         <l xml:id="SS.1.23.19ab"><label>1931 ed. 1.23.19ab</label>
                              kapotavarṇapratimā yasyāntāḥ kledavarjitāḥ | </l>

                         <l xml:id="SS.1.23.19cd"><label>1931 ed. 1.23.19cd</label> sthirāś
                              cipiṭikāvanto rohatīti tam ādiśet || </l>

                         <l xml:id="SS.1.23.20ab"><label>1931 ed. 1.23.20ab</label> rūḍhavartmānam
                              agranthim aśūnam arujaṃ vraṇam | </l>

                         <l xml:id="SS.1.23.20cd"><label>1931 ed. 1.23.20cd</label> tvaksavarṇaṃ

                         <l xml:id="SS.1.23.21cd"><label>1931 ed. 1.23.21cd</label> harṣāt krodhād

                    <div n="24" type="adhyāya">
                         <head> caturviṃśatitamo 'dhyāyaḥ |</head>

                         <l xml:id="SS.1.24.1"><label>1931 ed. 1.24.1</label> athāto
                              vyādhisamuddeśīyam adhyāyaṃ vyākhyāsyāmaḥ || </l>

                         <l xml:id="SS.1.24.2"><label>1931 ed. 1.24.2</label> yathovāca bhagavān
                              dhanvantariḥ || </l>

                         <l xml:id="SS.1.24.3"><label>1931 ed. 1.24.3</label> dvividhās tu vyādhayaḥ
                              śastrasādhyāḥ snehādikriyāsādhyāś ca | tatra śastrasādhyeṣu
                              snehādikriyā na pratiṣidhyate snehādikriyāsādhyeṣu śastrakarma na
                              kriyate || </l>

                         <l xml:id="SS.1.24.4"><label>1931 ed. 1.24.4</label> asmin punaḥ śāstre
                              sarvatantrasāmānyāt sarveṣāṃ vyādhīnāṃ yathāsthūlam avarodhaḥ kriyate
                              | prāgabhihitaṃ tadduḥkhasaṃyogā vyādhaya iti | tac ca duḥkhaṃ
                              trividhaṃ ādhyātmikaṃ ādhibhautikaṃ ādhidaivikam iti | tat tu
                              saptavidhe vyādhāv upanipatati | te punaḥ saptavidhā vyādhayaḥ tad
                              yathā ādibalapravṛttāḥ janmabalapravṛttāḥ doṣabalapravṛttāḥ
                              saṃghātabalapravṛttāḥ kālabalapravṛttāḥ daivabalapravṛttāḥ
                              svabhāvabalapravṛttā iti || </l>

                         <l xml:id="SS.1.24.5"><label>1931 ed. 1.24.5</label> tatrādibalapravṛttā ye
                              śukraśoṇitadoṣānvayāḥ kuṣṭhārśaḥprabhṛtayaḥ te 'pi dvividhāḥ mātṛjāḥ
                              pitṛjāś ca | janmabalapravṛttā ye māturapacārāt
                              paṅgujātyandhabadhiramūkaminminavāmanaprabhṛtayo jāyante te 'pi
                              dvividhā rasakṛtāḥ dauhṛdāpacārakṛtāś ca | doṣabalapravṛttā ya
                              ātaṅkasamutpannā mithyāhārācārakṛtāś ca te 'pi dvividhāḥ
                              āmāśayasamutthāḥ pakvāśayasamutthāś ca | punaś ca dvividhāḥ śārīrā
                              mānasāś ca | ta ete ādhyātmikāḥ || </l>

                         <l xml:id="SS.1.24.6"><label>1931 ed. 1.24.6</label> saṃghātabalapravṛttā
                              ya āgantavo durbalasya balavadvigrahāt te 'pi dvividhāḥ śastrakṛtā
                              vyālakṛtāś ca | ete ādhibhautikāḥ || </l>

                         <l xml:id="SS.1.24.5x"><label>1931 ed. 1.24.7</label> kālabalapravṛttā ye
                              śītoṣṇavātavarṣāprabhṛtinimittāḥ te 'pi dvividhāḥ vyāpannartukṛtā
                              avyāpannartukṛtāś ca |</l>

                         <l xml:id="SS.1.24.7"> daivabalapravṛttā ye devadrohādabhiśastakā
                              atharvaṇakṛtā upasargajāś ca te 'pi dvividhāḥ vidyudaśanikrtāḥ
                              piśācādikṛtāś ca punaś ca dvividhāḥ saṃsargajā ākasmikāś ca |
                              svabhāvabalapravṛttāḥ kṣutpipāsājarāmṛtyunidrāprabhṛtayaḥ te 'pi
                              dvividhāḥ kālakṛtā akālakṛtāś ca tatra parirakṣaṇakṛtāḥ kālakṛtāḥ
                              aparirakṣaṇakṛtā akālakṛtāḥ | ete ādhidaivikāḥ | atra
                              sarvavyādhyavarodhaḥ || </l>

                         <l xml:id="SS.1.24.8"><label>1931 ed. 1.24.8</label> sarveṣāṃ ca vyādhīnāṃ
                              vātapittaśleṣmāṇa eva mūlaṃ talliṅgatvād dṛṣṭaphalatvād āgamāc ca |
                              yathā hi kṛtsnaṃ vikārajātaṃ viśvarūpeṇāvasthitaṃ sattva<pc
                                   > </pc>rajas<pc> </pc>tamāṃsi na vyatiricyante evam eva kṛtsnaṃ
                              vikārajātaṃ viśvarūpeṇāvasthitam avyatiricya vātapittaśleṣmāṇo
                              vartante | doṣadhātumalasaṃsargād āyatanaviśeṣān nimittataś caiṣāṃ
                              vikalpaḥ | doṣadūṣiteṣv atyarthaṃ dhātuṣu saṃjñā kriyate rasajo 'yaṃ
                              śoṇitajo 'yaṃ māṃsajo 'yaṃ medojo 'yaṃ asthijo 'yaṃ majjajo 'yaṃ
                              śukrajo 'yam vyādhir iti || </l>

                         <l xml:id="SS.1.24.9"><label>1931 ed. 1.24.9</label> tatra
                              annāśraddhārocakāvipākāṅgamardajvarahṛllāsatṛptigauravahṛtpāṇḍurogamārgoparodhakārśyavairasyāṅgasādākālavalipalitadarśanaprabhṛtayo
                              rasadoṣajā vikārāḥ
                              kuṣṭhavisarpapiḍakāmaśakanīlikātilakālakanyacchavyaṅgendraluptaplīhavidradhigulmavātaśoṇitārśo
                              'rbudāṅgamardāsṛgdararaktapittaprabhṛtayo raktadoṣajāḥ
                              gudamukhameḍhrapākāś ca adhimāṃsārbudārśo
                              'dhijihvopajihvopakuśagalaśuṇḍikālajīmāṃsasaṃghātauṣṭhaprakopagalagaṇḍagaṇḍamālāprabhṛtayo
                              māṃsadoṣajāḥ
                              granthivṛddhigalagaṇḍārbudamedojauṣṭhaprakopamadhumehātisthaulyātisvedaprabhṛtayo
                              medodoṣajāḥ adhyasthyadhidantāsthitodaśūlakunakhaprabhṭayo
                              'sthidoṣajāḥ
                              tamodarśanamūrcchābhramaparvasthūlamūlārurjanmanetrābhisyandaprabhṛtayo
                              majjadoṣajāḥ klaibyāpraharṣaśukrāśmarīśukramehaśukradoṣādayaś ca
                              taddoṣajāḥ tvagdoṣāḥ saṅgo 'tipravṛttirayathāpravṛttir vā
                              malāyatanadoṣāḥ indriyāṇām apravṛttir ayathā pravṛttir
                              vendriyāyatanadoṣāḥ ity eṣa samāsa uktaḥ vistaraṃ nimittāni caiṣāṃ
                              pratirogaṃ vakṣyāmaḥ || </l>

                         <l xml:id="SS.1.24.10"><label>1931 ed. 1.24.10</label> bhavati cātra | </l>

                         <l xml:id="SS.1.24.10ab"><label>1931 ed. 1.24.10ab</label> kupitānāṃ hi
                              doṣāṇāṃ śarīre paridhāvatām | </l>

                         <l xml:id="SS.1.24.10cd"><label>1931 ed. 1.24.10cd</label> yatra saṅgaḥ
                              khavaiguṇyād vyādhis tatropajāyate || </l>

                         <l xml:id="SS.1.24.11"><label>1931 ed. 1.24.11</label> bhūyo 'tra jijñāsyaṃ
                              kiṃ vātādīnāṃ jvarādīnāṃ ca nityaḥ saṃśleṣaḥ paricchedo vā iti yadi
                              nityaḥ saṃśleṣaḥ syāt tarhi nityāturāḥ sarva eva prāṇinaḥ syuḥ athāpy
                              anyathā vātādīnāṃ jvarādīnāṃ cānyatra vartamānānām anyatra liṅgaṃ na
                              bhavatīti kṛtvā yad ucyate vātādayo jvarādīnāṃ mūlānīti tan na |
                              atrocyate doṣān pratyākhyāya jvarādayo na bhavanti atha ca na nityaḥ
                              saṃbandhaḥ yathā hi vidyudvātāśanivarṣāṇyākāśaṃ pratyākhyāya na
                              bhavanti saty apy ākāśe kadācin na bhavanti atha ca nimittatas tata
                              evotpattir iti taraṅgabudbudādayaś codakaviśeṣāḥ eva vātādīnāṃ
                              jvarādīnāṃ ca nāpy evam saṃśleṣo na paricchedaḥ śāśvatikaḥ atha ca
                              nimittata evotpattir iti || </l>

                         <l xml:id="SS.1.26.7"><label>1931 ed. 1.26.7</label> adhikāro hi
                              lohaveṇuvṛkṣatṛṇaśṛṅgāsthimayeṣu tatrāpi viśeṣato loheṣveva
                              viśasanārthopapannatvāllohasya lohānām api durvāratvād aṇumukhatvād

                         <l xml:id="SS.1.26.9-10"><label>1931 ed. 1.26.9</label> tāni vegakṣayāt

                              'sthivivarapeśīprabhṛtiṣu vā śarīrapradeśeṣu || <label>1931 ed.
                                   1.26.10</label> tatra śalyalakṣaṇam ucyamānam upadhāraya | tat tu
                              dvividhaṃ sāmānyaṃ vaiśeṣikaṃ ca | śyāvaṃ piḍakācitaṃ
                              śophavedanāvantaṃ muhurmuhuḥ śoṇitāsrāviṇaṃ budbudavad unnataṃ
                              mṛdumāṃsaṃ ca vraṇaṃ jānīyāt saśalyo 'yam iti | sāmānyam etal lakṣaṇam
                              uktam | vaiśeṣikaṃ tu tvaggate vivarṇaḥ śopho bhavaty āyataḥ kaṭhinaś
                              ca māṃsagate śophābhivṛddhiḥ śalyamārgānupasaṃrohaḥ pīḍanāsahiṣṇutā
                              coṣapākau ca peśyantarasthe 'py etad eva coṣaśophavarjaṃ sirāgate
                              sirādhmānam sirāśūlaṃ sirāśophaś ca snāyugate snāyujālotkṣepaṇaṃ
                              saṃrambhaś cogrā ruk ca srotogate srotasāṃ svakarmaguṇahāniḥ;
                              dhamanīsthe saphenaṃ raktam īrayann anilaḥ saśabdo nirgacchaty
                              aṅgamardaḥ pipāsā hṛllāsaś ca asthigate vividhavedanāprādurbhāvaḥ
                              śophaś ca asthivivaragate 'sthipūrṇatā'sthitodaḥ saṃharṣo balavāṃś ca
                              sandhigate 'sthivacceṣṭoparamaś ca koṣṭhagata āṭopānāhau
                              mūtrapurīṣāhāradarśanaṃ ca vraṇamukhāt marmagate marmaviddhāvac
                              ceṣṭate | sūkṣmagatiṣu śalyeṣv etāny eva lakṣaṇāny aspaṣṭāni bhavanti
                              || </l>

                         <l xml:id="SS.1.26.11"><label>1931 ed. 1.26.11</label> mahānty alpāni vā
                              śuddhadehānām anulomasanniviṣṭāni rohanti viśeṣataḥ
                              kaṇṭhasrotaḥsirātvakpeśyasthivivareṣu

                         <l xml:id="SS.1.26.12"><label>1931 ed. 1.26.12</label> tatra tvakpranaṣṭe
                              snigdhasvinnāyāṃ mṛnmāṣayavagodhūmagomayamṛditāyāṃ tvaci yatra
                              saṃrambho vedanā vā bhavati tatra śalyaṃ vijānīyāt
                              styānaghṛtamṛccandanakalkair vā pradigdhāyāṃ śalyoṣmaṇā+āśu visarati
                              ghṛtam upaśuṣyati vā lepo yatra tatra śalyaṃ vijānīyāt māṃsapranaṣṭe
                              snehasvedādibhiḥ kriyāviśeṣair aviruddair āturam upapādayet karśitasya
                              tu śithilībhūtam anavabaddhaṃ kṣubhyamāṇaṃ yatra saṃrambhaṃ vedanāṃ vā

                              snehasvedopapannānyasthīni bandhanapīḍanābhyāṃ bhṛśam upācared yatra

                         <l xml:id="SS.1.27.1"><label>1931 ed. 1.27.1</label> athātaḥ
                              śalyāpanayanīyam adhyāyaṃ vyākhyāsyāmaḥ || </l>

                         <l xml:id="SS.1.27.2"><label>1931 ed. 1.27.2</label> yathovāca bhagavān
                              dhanvantariḥ || </l>

                         <l xml:id="SS.1.27.3"><label>1931 ed. 1.27.3</label> śalyaṃ
                              dvividhamavabaddhamanavabaddhaṃ ca || </l>

                         <l xml:id="SS.1.27.4"><label>1931 ed. 1.27.4</label> tatra
                              samāsenānavabaddhaśalyoddharaṇārthaṃ pañcadaśa hetūn vakṣyāmaḥ | tad
                              yathā svabhāvaḥ pācanaṃ bhedanaṃ dāraṇaṃ pīḍanaṃ pramārjanaṃ
                              nirdhmāpanaṃ vamanaṃ virecanaṃ prakṣālanaṃ pratimarśaḥ pravāhaṇaṃ
                              ācūṣaṇaṃ ayaskānto harṣaś ceti || </l>

                         <l xml:id="SS.1.27.5"><label>1931 ed. 1.27.5</label>
                              tatrāśrukṣavathūdgārakāsamūtrapurīṣānilaiḥ svabhāvabalapravṛttair
                              nayanādibhyaḥ patati māṃsāvagāḍhaṃ śalyamavidahyamānaṃ pācayitvā
                              prakothā(ā.pā)ttasya pūyaśoṇitavegād gauravād vā patati |
                              pakvamabhidyamānaṃ bhedayed dārayed vā | bhinnamanirasyamānaṃ
                              pīḍanīyaiḥ pīḍayet pāṇibhir vā | aṇūny akṣaśalyāni
                              pariṣecanādhmāpanair bālavastrapāṇibhiḥ pramārjayet |
                              āhāraśeṣaśleṣmahīnāṇuśalyāni śvasanotkāsanapradhamanair nirdhamet |
                              annaśalyāni vamanāṅgulipratimarśaprabhṛtibhiḥ | virecanaiḥ
                              pakvāśayagatāni | vraṇadoṣāśayagatāni prakṣālanaiḥ |
                              vātamūtrapurīṣagarbhasaṅgeṣu pravāhaṇamuktaṃ |
                              mārutodakasaviṣarudhiraduṣṭastanyeṣv ācūṣaṇam āsyena viṣāṇair vā |
                              anulomam anavabaddham akarṇam analpavraṇamukham ayaskāntena | hṛdy
                              avasthitam anekakāraṇotpannaṃ śokaśalyaṃ harṣeṇeti || </l>

                         <l xml:id="SS.1.27.6"><label>1931 ed. 1.27.6</label> sarvaśalyānāṃ tu
                              mahatām aṇūnāṃ vā dvāv evāharaṇahetū bhavataḥ pratilomo 'nulomaś ca || </l>

                              saṃsvedya vidahya pradihya sarpirmadhubhyāṃ baddhvā+ācārikam upadiśet
                              | (? sirāsnāyuvilagnaṃ śalākādibhir vimocyāpanayet
                              śvayathugrastavāraṅgaṃ samavapīḍya śvayathuṃ durbalavāraṅgaṃ
                              kuśādibhir baddhvā |) </l>

                         <l xml:id="SS.1.27.13"><label>1931 ed. 1.27.13</label> hṛdayamabhito

                              durupaharamanyato 'pabādhyamānaṃ pāṭayitvoddharet || </l>

                         <l xml:id="SS.1.27.14"><label>1931 ed. 1.27.14</label> asthivivarapraviṣṭam

                              balavadbhiḥ suparigṛhītasya yantreṇa grāhayitvā śalyavāraṅgaṃ
                              pravibhujya dhanurguṇair baddhaikataś cāsya pañcāṅgyām
                              upasaṃyatasyāśvasya vaktrakavike badhnīyāt athainaṃ kaśayā tāḍayed
                              yathonnamayan śiro vegena śalyam uddharati dṛḍhāṃ vā vṛkṣaśākhām
                              avanamya tasyāṃ pūrvavad baddhvoddharet || </l>

                              praṇāśaṃ dīpacakṣuṣoḥ |
                              <caesura/>
                               yaḥ paśyed devatānāṃ ca (ā.vā) prakampam avanes tathā || </l>

                         <l xml:id="SS.1.29.64"><label>1931 ed. 1.29.64</label> yasya chardir vireko
                              vā daśanāḥ prapatanti vā |
                              <caesura/>
                               śālmalīṃ kiṃśukaṃ yūpaṃ valmīkaṃ pāribhadrakam || </l>

                         <l xml:id="SS.1.29.65"><label>1931 ed. 1.29.65</label> puṣpāḍhyaṃ kovidāraṃ
                              vā citāṃ vā yo 'dhirohati |
                              <caesura/>
                               kārpāsatailapiṇyākalohāni lavaṇaṃ tilān || </l>

                         <l xml:id="SS.1.29.66"><label>1931 ed. 1.29.66</label> labhetāśnīta vā
                              pakvam annaṃ yaś ca pibet surām |
                              <caesura/>
                               svasthaḥ sa labhate vyādhiṃ vyādhito mṛtyum ṛcchati || </l>

                         <l xml:id="SS.1.29.67"><label>1931 ed. 1.29.67</label> yathāsvaṃ
                              prakṛtisvapno vismṛto vihatas tathā |
                              <caesura/>
                               cintākṛto divā dṛṣto bhavanty aphaladās tu te || </l>

                         <l xml:id="SS.1.29.68"><label>1931 ed. 1.29.68</label> jvaritānāṃ śunā
                              sakhyaṃ kapisakhyaṃ tu śoṣiṇām |
                              <caesura/>
                               unmāde rākṣasaiḥ pretair apasmāre pravartanam || </l>

                         <l xml:id="SS.1.29.69"><label>1931 ed. 1.29.69</label> mehātisāriṇāṃ
                              toyapānaṃ snehasya kuṣṭhinām |
                              <caesura/>
                               gulmeṣu sthāvarotpattiḥ koṣṭhe mūrdhni śiroruji || </l>

                         <l xml:id="SS.1.29.70"><label>1931 ed. 1.29.70</label> śaṣkulībhakṣaṇaṃ
                              chardyāmadhvā śvāsapipāsayoḥ |
                              <caesura/>
                               haridraṃ bhojanaṃ vā'pi yasya syāt pāṇḍurogiṇaḥ || </l>

                         <l xml:id="SS.1.29.71"><label>1931 ed. 1.29.71</label> raktapittī pibed yas
                              tu śoṇitaṃ sa vinaśyati |
                              <caesura/>
                               svapnānevaṃvidhān dṛṣṭvā prātarutthāya yatnavān || </l>

                         <l xml:id="SS.1.29.72"><label>1931 ed. 1.29.72</label>
                              dadyānmāṣāṃstilāṃllohaṃ viprebhyaḥ kāñcanaṃ tathā |
                              <caesura/>
                               japec cāpi śubhān mantrān gāyatrīṃ tripadāṃ tathā || </l>

                         <l xml:id="SS.1.29.73"><label>1931 ed. 1.29.73</label> dṛṣṭvā tu prathame
                              yāme svapyād dhyātvā punaḥ śubham |
                              <caesura/>
                               japedvā'nyatamaṃ vede brahmacārī samāhitaḥ || </l>

                         <l xml:id="SS.1.29.74"><label>1931 ed. 1.29.74</label> devatāyatane caiva
                              vasedrātritrayaṃ tathā |
                              <caesura/>
                               viprāṃś ca pūjayennityaṃ duḥsvapnāt pravimucyate || </l>

                         <l xml:id="SS.1.29.75"><label>1931 ed. 1.29.75</label> ata ūrdhvaṃ
                              pravakṣyāmi praśastaṃ svapnadarśanam |
                              <caesura/>
                               devān dvijān govṛṣabhān jīvataḥ suhṛdo nṛpān || </l>

                         <l xml:id="SS.1.29.76"><label>1931 ed. 1.29.76</label> samiddham agniṃ
                              sādhūṃś ca nirmalāni jalāni ca |
                              <caesura/>
                               paśyet kalyāṇalābhāya vyādher apagamāya ca || </l>

                         <l xml:id="SS.1.29.77"><label>1931 ed. 1.29.77</label> māṃsaṃ matsyān
                              srajaḥ śvetā vāsāṃsi ca phalāni ca |
                              <caesura/>
                               labhante dhanalābhāya vyādher apagamāya ca || </l>

                         <l xml:id="SS.1.29.78"><label>1931 ed. 1.29.78</label>
                              mahāprāsādasaphalavṛkṣavāraṇaparvatān |
                              <caesura/>
                               āroheddravyalābhāya vyādherapagamāya ca || </l>

                         <l xml:id="SS.1.29.79"><label>1931 ed. 1.29.79</label> nadīnadasamudrāṃś ca
                              kṣubhitān kaluṣodakān |
                              <caesura/>
                               taret kalyāṇalābhāya vyādher apagamāya ca || </l>

                         <l xml:id="SS.1.29.79cdI"/>

                         <l xml:id="SS.1.29.79cdII"/>

                         <l xml:id="SS.1.29.80"><label>1931 ed. 1.29.80</label> urago vā jalauko vā
                              bhramaro vā'pi yaṃ daśet |
                              <caesura/>
                               ārogyaṃ nirdiśettasya dhanalābhaṃ ca buddhimān || </l>

                         <l xml:id="SS.1.29.81"><label>1931 ed. 1.29.81</label> evaṃrūpān śubhān
                              svapnān yaḥ paśyed vyādhito naraḥ |
                              <caesura/>
                               sa dīrghāyur iti jñeyas tasmai karma samācaret || </l>
                         <p ana="trailer">iti suśrutasaṃhitāyāṃ sūtrasthāne
                              viparītāviparītasvapnanidarśanīyo nāmaikonatriṃśattamo 'dhyāyaḥ ||
                         </p>
                    </div>




                    <div n="30" type="adhyāya">
                         <head> triṃśattamo 'dhyāyaḥ |</head>

                         <l xml:id="SS.1.30.1"><label>1931 ed. 1.30.1</label> athātaḥ
                              pañcendriyārthavipratipattim adhyāyaṃ vyākhyāsyāmaḥ || </l>

                         <l xml:id="SS.1.30.2"><label>1931 ed. 1.30.2</label> yathovāca bhagavān
                              dhanvantariḥ || </l>

                         <l xml:id="SS.1.30.3"><label>1931 ed. 1.30.3</label> śarīraśīlayor yasya
                              prakṛter vikṛtir bhavet |
                              <caesura/>
                               tat tva riṣṭaṃ samāsena vyāsatas tu nibodha me || </l>

                         <l xml:id="SS.1.30.4"><label>1931 ed. 1.30.4</label> śṛṇoti vividhān śabdān
                              yo divyānām abhāvataḥ |
                              <caesura/>
                               samudrapurameghānām asaṃpattau ca niḥsvanān || </l>

                         <l xml:id="SS.1.30.5"><label>1931 ed. 1.30.5</label> tān svanānnāvagṛhṇāti
                              manyate cānyaśabdavat |
                              <caesura/>
                               grāmyāraṇyasvanāṃś cāpi viparītān śṛṇoti ca || </l>

                         <l xml:id="SS.1.30.6"><label>1931 ed. 1.30.6</label> dviṣacchabdeṣu ramate
                              suhṛcchabdeṣu kupyati |
                              <caesura/>
                               na śṛṇoti ca yo 'kasmāttaṃ bruvanti gatāyuṣam || </l>

                         <l xml:id="SS.1.30.7"><label>1931 ed. 1.30.7</label> yas tūṣṇam iva gṛhṇāti
                              śītamuṣṇaṃ ca śītavat |
                              <caesura/>
                               saṃjātaśītapiḍako yaś ca dāhena pīḍyate || </l>

                         <l xml:id="SS.1.30.8"><label>1931 ed. 1.30.8</label> uṣṇagātro 'timātraṃ ca
                              yaḥ śītena pravepate |
                              <caesura/>
                               prahārān nābhijānāti yo 'ṅgacchedamathāpi vā || </l>

                         <l xml:id="SS.1.30.9"><label>1931 ed. 1.30.9</label> pāṃśunevāvakīrṇāni yaś
                              ca gātrāṇi manyate |
                              <caesura/>
                               varṇānyatā vā rājyo vā yasya gātre bhavanti hi || </l>

                         <l xml:id="SS.1.30.10"><label>1931 ed. 1.30.10</label> snātānuliptaṃ yaṃ
                              cāpi bhajante nīlamakṣikāḥ |
                              <caesura/>
                               sugandhirvā'ti yo 'kasmāt taṃ bruvanti gatāyuṣam || </l>

                         <l xml:id="SS.1.30.11"><label>1931 ed. 1.30.11</label> viparītena gṛhṇāti
                              rasān yaś copayojitān |
                              <caesura/>
                               upayuktāḥ kramādyasya rasā doṣābhivṛddhaye || </l>

                         <l xml:id="SS.1.30.12"><label>1931 ed. 1.30.12</label> yasya doṣāgnisāmyaṃ
                              ca kuryur mithyopayojitāḥ |
                              <caesura/>
                               yo vā rasān na saṃvetti gatāsuṃ taṃ pracakṣate || </l>

                         <l xml:id="SS.1.30.13"><label>1931 ed. 1.30.13</label> sugandhaṃ vetti
                              durgandhaṃ durgandhasya sugandhitām |
                              <caesura/>
                               gṛhṇīte vā 'nyathā gandhaṃ śānte dīpe ca nīrujaḥ || </l>

                         <l xml:id="SS.1.30.14"><label>1931 ed. 1.30.14</label> yo vā gandhān na
                              jānāti gatāsuṃ taṃ vinirdiśet |
                              <caesura/>
                               dvandvānyuṣṇahimādīni kālāvasthā diśas tathā || </l>

                         <l xml:id="SS.1.30.15"><label>1931 ed. 1.30.15</label> viparītena gṛhṇāti
                              bhāvān anyāṃś ca yo naraḥ |
                              <caesura/>
                               divā jyotīṃṣi yaś cāpi jvalitānīva paśyati || </l>

                         <l xml:id="SS.1.30.16"><label>1931 ed. 1.30.16</label> rātrau sūryaṃ
                              jvalantaṃ vā divā vā candravarcasam |
                              <caesura/>
                               ameghopaplave yaś ca śakracāpataḍidguṇān || </l>

                         <l xml:id="SS.1.30.17"><label>1931 ed. 1.30.17</label> taḍittvato 'sitān yo
                              vā nirmale gagane ghanān |
                              <caesura/>
                               vimānayānaprāsādair yaś ca saṃkulamambaram || </l>

                         <l xml:id="SS.1.30.18"><label>1931 ed. 1.30.18</label> yaś cānilaṃ
                              mūrtimantam antarikṣaṃ ca paśyati |
                              <caesura/>
                               dhūmanīhāravāsobhir āvṛtām iva medinīm || </l>

                         <l xml:id="SS.1.30.19"><label>1931 ed. 1.30.19</label> pradīptam iva lokaṃ
                              ca yo vā plutam ivāmbhasā |
                              <caesura/>
                               bhūmim aṣṭāpadākārāṃ lekhābhir yaś ca paśyati || </l>

                         <l xml:id="SS.1.30.20"><label>1931 ed. 1.30.20</label> na paśyati
                              sanakṣatrāṃ yaś cā devīm arundhatīm |
                              <caesura/>
                               dhruvam ākāśagaṅgāṃ vā taṃ vadanti gatāyuṣam || </l>

                         <l xml:id="SS.1.30.21"><label>1931 ed. 1.30.21</label>
                              jyotsnādarśoṣṇatoyeṣu chāyāṃ yaś ca na paśyati |
                              <caesura/>
                               paśyaty ekāṅgahīnāṃ vā vikṛtāṃ vā'nyasattvajām || </l>

                         <l xml:id="SS.1.30.22"><label>1931 ed. 1.30.22</label>
                              śvakākakaṅkagṛdhrāṇāṃ pretānāṃ yakṣarakṣasām |
                              <caesura/>
                               piśācoraganāgānāṃ bhūtānāṃ vikṛtām api || </l>

                         <l xml:id="SS.1.30.22cdI"/>



                         <l xml:id="SS.1.30.23"><label>1931 ed. 1.30.23</label> yo vā
                              mayūrakaṇṭhābhaṃ vidhūmaṃ vahnim īkṣate |
                              <caesura/>
                               āturasya bhavenmṛtyuḥ svastho vyādhimāvāpnuyāt || </l>

                         <l xml:id="SS.1.30.22cdII"/>

                         <l xml:id="SS.1.30.22cdIII"/>

                         <l xml:id="SS.1.30.22cdIV"/>

                         <l xml:id="SS.1.30.22cdV"/>

                         <l xml:id="SS.1.30.22cdVI"/>

                         <l xml:id="SS.1.30.22cdVIx"/>

                         <p ana="trailer">iti suśrutasaṃhitāyāṃ sūtrasthāne
                              pañcendriyārthavipratipattir nāma triṃśo 'dhyāyaḥ || </p>
                    </div>


                    <div n="31" type="adhyāya">
                         <head> ekatriṃśattamo 'dhyāyaḥ |</head>

                         <l xml:id="SS.1.31.1"><label>1931 ed. 1.31.1</label> athātaś
                              chāyāvipratipattim adhyāyaṃ vyākhyāsyāmaḥ || </l>

                         <l xml:id="SS.1.31.2"><label>1931 ed. 1.31.2</label> yathovāca bhagavān
                              dhanvantariḥ || </l>

                         <l xml:id="SS.1.31.3"><label>1931 ed. 1.31.3</label> śyāvā lohitikā nīlā
                              pītikā vā'pi mānavam |
                              <caesura/>
                               abhidravanti yaṃ chāyāḥ sa parāsur asaṃśayam || </l>

                         <l xml:id="SS.1.31.4"><label>1931 ed. 1.31.4</label> hrīr apakramate yasya
                              prabhādhṛtismṛtiśriyaḥ |
                              <caesura/>
                               akasmād yaṃ bhajante vā sa parāsur asaṃśayam || </l>

                         <l xml:id="SS.1.31.5"><label>1931 ed. 1.31.5</label> yasyādharauṣṭhaḥ
                              patitaḥ kṣiptaś cordhvaṃ tathottaraḥ |
                              <caesura/>
                               ubhau vā jāmbavābhāsau durlabhaṃ tasya jīvitam || </l>

                         <l xml:id="SS.1.31.6"><label>1931 ed. 1.31.6</label> āraktā daśanā yasya
                              śyāvā vā syuḥ patanti vā |
                              <caesura/>
                               khañjanapratimā vā'pi taṃ gatāyuṣam ādiśet || </l>

                         <l xml:id="SS.1.31.7"><label>1931 ed. 1.31.7</label> kṛṣṇā stabdhā'valiptā
                              vā jihvā śūnā ca yasya vai |
                              <caesura/>
                               karkaśā vā bhavedyasya so 'cirād vijahāty asūn || </l>

                         <l xml:id="SS.1.31.8"><label>1931 ed. 1.31.8</label> kuṭilā sphuṭitā vā'pi
                              śuṣkā vā yasya nāsikā |
                              <caesura/>
                               avasphūrjati magnā vā na sa jīvati mānavaḥ || </l>

                         <l xml:id="SS.1.31.9"><label>1931 ed. 1.31.9</label> saṃkṣipte viṣame
                              stabdhe rakte sraste ca locane |
                              <caesura/>
                               syātāṃ vā prasrute yasya sa gatāyurnaro dhruvam || </l>

                         <l xml:id="SS.1.31.10"><label>1931 ed. 1.31.10</label> keśāḥ sīmantino
                              yasya saṃkṣipte vinate bhruvau |
                              <caesura/>
                               lunanti cākṣipakṣmāṇi so 'cirādyāti mṛtyave || </l>

                         <l xml:id="SS.1.31.11"><label>1931 ed. 1.31.11</label> nāharaty annam
                              āsyasthaṃ na dhārayati yaḥ śiraḥ |
                              <caesura/>
                               ekāgradṛṣṭir mūḍhātmā sadyaḥ prāṇān jahāti saḥ || </l>

                         <l xml:id="SS.1.31.12"><label>1931 ed. 1.31.12</label> balavān durbalo
                              vā'pi saṃmohaṃ yo 'dhigacchati |
                              <caesura/>
                               utthāpyamāno bahuśastaṃ pakvaṃ bhiṣagādiśet || </l>

                         <l xml:id="SS.1.31.13"><label>1931 ed. 1.31.13</label> uttānaḥ sarvadā śete
                              pādau vikurute ca yaḥ |
                              <caesura/>
                               viprasāraṇaśīlo vā na sa jīvati mānavaḥ || </l>

                         <l xml:id="SS.1.31.14"><label>1931 ed. 1.31.14</label> śītapādakarocchvāsaś
                              chinnocchvāsaś ca yo bhavet |
                              <caesura/>
                               kākocchvāsaś ca yo martyas taṃ dhīraḥ parivarjayet || </l>

                         <l xml:id="SS.1.31.15"><label>1931 ed. 1.31.15</label> nidrā na chidyate
                              yasya yo vā jāgarti sarvadā |
                              <caesura/>
                               muhyed vā vaktukāmaś ca pratyākhyeyaḥ sa jānatā || </l>

                         <l xml:id="SS.1.31.16"><label>1931 ed. 1.31.16</label> uttarauṣṭhaṃ ca yo
                              lihyād utkārāṃś ca karoti yaḥ |
                              <caesura/>
                               pretair vā bhāṣate sārdhaṃ pretarūpaṃ tam ādiśet || </l>

                         <l xml:id="SS.1.31.17"><label>1931 ed. 1.31.17</label> svebhyaḥ
                              saromakūpebhyo yasya raktaṃ pravartate |
                              <caesura/>
                               puruṣasyāviṣārtasya sadyo jahyāt sa jīvitam || </l>

                         <l xml:id="SS.1.31.18"><label>1931 ed. 1.31.18</label> vātāṣṭhīlā tu hṛdaye
                              yasyor dhvam anuyāyinī |
                              <caesura/>
                               rujā'nnavidveṣakarī sa parāsur asaṃśayam || </l>

                         <l xml:id="SS.1.31.19"><label>1931 ed. 1.31.19</label> ananyopadravakṛtaḥ
                              śophaḥ pādasamutthitaḥ |
                              <caesura/>
                               puruṣaṃ hanti nārīṃ tu mukhajo guhyajo dvayam || </l>

                         <l xml:id="SS.1.31.20"><label>1931 ed. 1.31.20</label> atisāro jvaro hikkā
                              chardiḥ śūnāṇḍameḍhratā |
                              <caesura/>
                               śvāsinaḥ kāsino vā'pi yasya taṃ kṣīṇam ādiśet || </l>

                         <l xml:id="SS.1.31.21"><label>1931 ed. 1.31.21</label> svedo dāhaś ca
                              balavān hikkā śvāsaś ca mānavam |
                              <caesura/>
                               balavantam api prāṇair viyuñjanti na saṃśayaḥ || </l>

                         <l xml:id="SS.1.31.22"><label>1931 ed. 1.31.22</label> śyāvā jihvā bhaved
                              yasya savyaṃ cākṣi nimajjati |
                              <caesura/>
                               mukhaṃ ca jāyate pūti yasya taṃ parivarjayet || </l>

                         <l xml:id="SS.1.31.23"><label>1931 ed. 1.31.23</label> vaktram āpūryate
                              'śrubhiḥ svidyataś caraṇāv ubhau |
                              <caesura/>
                               cakṣuś cākulatāṃ yāti yamarāṣṭraṃ gamiṣyataḥ || </l>

                         <l xml:id="SS.1.31.24"><label>1931 ed. 1.31.24</label> atimātraṃ laghūni
                              syur gātrāṇi gurukāṇi vā |
                              <caesura/>
                               yasyākasmāt sa vijñeyo gantā vaivasvatālayam || </l>

                         <l xml:id="SS.1.31.25"><label>1931 ed. 1.31.25</label>
                              paṅkamatsyavasātailaghṛtagandhāṃś ca ye narāḥ |
                              <caesura/>
                               mṛṣṭagandhāṃś ca ye vānti gantāras te yamālayam || </l>

                         <l xml:id="SS.1.31.26"><label>1931 ed. 1.31.26</label> yūkā lalāṭam āyānti
                              baliṃ nāśnanti vāyasāḥ |
                              <caesura/>
                               yeṣāṃ vā'pi ratir nāsti yātāras te yamālayam || </l>

                         <l xml:id="SS.1.31.27"><label>1931 ed. 1.31.27</label> jvarātisāraśophāḥ
                              syur yasyānyonyāvasādinaḥ |
                              <caesura/>
                               prakṣīṇabalamāṃsasya nāsau śakyaś cikitsitum || </l>

                         <l xml:id="SS.1.31.28"><label>1931 ed. 1.31.28</label> kṣīṇasya yasya
                              kṣuttṛṣṇe hṛdyair miṣṭair hitais tathā |
                              <caesura/>
                               na śāmyato 'nnapānaiś ca tasya mṛtyur upasthitaḥ || </l>

                         <l xml:id="SS.1.31.29"><label>1931 ed. 1.31.29</label> pravāhikā śiraḥśūlaṃ
                              koṣṭhaśūlaṃ ca dāruṇam |
                              <caesura/>
                               pipāsā balahāniś ca tasya mṛtyur upasthitaḥ || </l>

                         <l xml:id="SS.1.31.30"><label>1931 ed. 1.31.30</label> viṣameṇopacāreṇa
                              karmabhiś ca purākṛtaiḥ |
                              <caesura/>
                               anityatvāc ca jantūnāṃ jīvitaṃ nidhanaṃ vrajet || </l>

                         <l xml:id="SS.1.31.31"><label>1931 ed. 1.31.31</label> pretā bhūtāḥ piśācāś
                              ca rakṣāṃsi vividhāni ca |
                              <caesura/>
                               maraṇābhimukhaṃ nityam upasarpanti mānavam || </l>

                         <l xml:id="SS.1.31.32"><label>1931 ed. 1.31.32</label> tāni bheṣajavīryāṇi
                              pratighnanti jighāṃsayā |
                              <caesura/>
                               tasmān moghāḥ kriyāḥ sarvā bhavanty eva gatāyuṣām || </l>
                         <p ana="trailer">iti suśrutasaṃhitāyāṃ sūtrasthāne
                              chāyāvipratipattirnāmaikatriṃśattamo 'dhyāyaḥ || </p>

                    </div>



               </div>
          </body>
     </text>
</TEI>
